
---

# شرح منصة Perchance —

تُعدّ Perchance منصةً قويةً لبناء مولدات نصوص عشوائية وأدوات تفاعلية عبر الإنترنت، وتعتمد على بيئة تحرير ثنائية المحور تجمع بين منطق البيانات وتصميم الواجهة.

---

## نظرة عامة على بيئة التحرير

يتألف محرر Perchance من **محررَين رئيسيَّين** يعملان معاً لبناء المولد:

### 1. محرر القوائم (List Editor)
هو قلب المولد، ويُستخدم لكتابة البيانات والمنطق وتوليد المخرجات. يدعم صيغةً خاصةً بـ Perchance تقوم على:

- **القوائم الهرمية** المنظَّمة بمسافات بادئة (Tab أو مسافتان — يجب الالتزام بأحدهما طوال المشروع).
- **التعليقات** باستخدام `//` — تُتجاهَل كليًّا ولا تؤثر في المخرجات.
- **تخزين المتغيرات** بصيغة `[x = list.selectOne, ""]` (الفاصلة والنص الفارغ يجعلانه صامتاً لا يطبع).
- **الوصول إلى القوائم الفرعية** بصيغة `[list[variable]]` — بدون نقطة.
- **الشروط** بصيغة `[value >= 50 ? "Pass" : "Fail"]`.

يدعم المحرر أيضاً **تضمين HTML مباشرةً** داخل عناصر القائمة (وسوم مثل `<b>`, `<i>`, `<br>`, `<span>`)؛ غير أن `<script>` و`<style>` غير مدعومَين هنا ويجب وضعهما في محرر HTML حصراً.

---

### 2. محرر HTML (HTML Editor)
يُستخدم لبناء واجهة المستخدم وتصميمها والتحكم في التفاعل. يدعم HTML و CSS و JavaScript كاملاً. تُستدعى القوائم من JavaScript على النحو التالي:

| الأسلوب | المُرجَع | متى تستخدمه |
|--------|---------|-------------|
| `list.selectOne` | نص خام غير محلول | نادراً — فقط إذا لم تكن هناك قوائم متداخلة |
| `list.evaluateItem()` | نص محلول بالكامل ✅ | **الافتراضي** — يحل جميع المراجع المتداخلة |
| `list.selectMany(n)` | مصفوفة | لاختيار عدة عناصر دفعةً واحدة |

> **قاعدة:** استخدم دائماً `evaluateItem()` ما لم يكن لديك سبب صريح للعكس.

يمكن عرض قيمة قائمة مباشرةً في HTML بالأقواس المربعة `[output]` (تُحلَّل عند تحميل الصفحة)، أو ديناميكياً عبر JavaScript:

```javascript
document.getElementById('out').textContent = output.evaluateItem();
```

---

## الاستيراد والإضافات

### استيراد المولدات والإضافات
تُستورَد المولدات والإضافات الخارجية في **أعلى محرر القوائم** بالصيغة:

```perchance
aliasName = {import:plugin-name}
```

- `aliasName` هو الاسم الذي تستخدمه للاستدعاء لاحقاً — اختر اسماً واضحاً وثابتاً.
- لا تُنتج الإضافات مخرجاتٍ تلقائياً — يجب استدعاؤها صراحةً.
- استورد كل إضافة مرةً واحدةً فقط، وتجنَّب استيراد ما لا تستخدمه.

### أبرز الإضافات المتاحة

| الإضافة | الاستيراد | الاستخدام |
|--------|----------|-----------|
| توليد صور | `image = {import:text-to-image-plugin}` | `[image(promptData)]` |
| توليد نصوص بالذكاء الاصطناعي | `ai = {import:ai-text-plugin}` | `await ai.textStream({...})` في JS |
| تخزين مستمر مشترك | `kv = {import:kv-plugin}` | `await kv.set/get/delete/list(...)` |
| تعليقات الزوار | `commentsPlugin = {import:comments-plugin}` | `[commentsPlugin(commentOptions)]` في HTML |
| نسخ إلى الحافظة | `copy = {import:copy-text-plugin}` | داخل المولد |

> **تنبيه:** إضافتا `ai-text-plugin` و`kv-plugin` غير متزامنتان — يجب استخدام `async/await` معهما دائماً.

---

## تصدير القوائم

جميع القوائم المُعرَّفة في المولد قابلة للاستيراد من مولدات أخرى تلقائياً، مما يتيح بناء مولدات مركّبة من وحدات أصغر وأكثر قابلية للصيانة.

---

- [Plugins | Perchance.org Wiki](https://perchance.fandom.com/wiki/Plugins)

               <!-- ==========================================
                  تبويب: الدليل والمساعدة | Help & Guide Tab
                  ========================================== -->
               <div id="guideTab" class="tab-content guide-content">

                  <div class="section-header">
                     <span><span class="ms">menu_book</span> Help & Guide</span>
                  </div>

                  <!-- مقدمة الدليل | Guide Introduction -->
                  <div style="background:var(--acc3); padding:12px; border-radius:8px; margin-bottom:16px; border-left:4px solid var(--acc2)">
                     <strong style="color:var(--acc2); font-size:0.95rem">
                        <span class="ms">menu_book</span> Unlimited Story Writer Pro v3.3.0
                     </strong>
                     <p style="margin:6px 0 0 0; font-size:0.8rem; color:var(--txt2); line-height:1.4">
                        Advanced AI story generator with multi-chapter management, real-time analytics, timeline visualization, content filtering, and 9+ AI-powered writing tools. Supports multiple languages with auto-detection and RTL.
                     </p>
                  </div>

                  <h3><span class="ms">my_location</span> Core Features</h3>
                  <p><strong>Multi-Chapter System:</strong> Stories auto-split into chapters at 5000-6000 words. Each chapter gets comprehensive AI-generated summaries for perfect continuity.</p>
                  <p><strong>Content Filtering:</strong> 3 levels (None/Standard/Child-Safe) with real-time AI enforcement. Child-Safe mode enables colorful kids theme automatically.</p>
                  <p><strong>Smart Generation:</strong> AI maintains perfect continuity across chapters using cumulative summaries and character/location/event tracking.</p>
                  <p><strong>Auto-Save:</strong> Saves every 5 seconds while typing. Auto-backup every 5 minutes with restore capability (keeps last 10 backups).</p>
                  <p><strong>Multi-Language:</strong> Supports Arabic, English, Chinese, Japanese, Korean, Russian, Hebrew, Thai, Persian with auto-detection and RTL support.</p>

                  <h3><span class="ms">settings</span> Story Settings</h3>
                  <p><strong>Genre:</strong> 14 options including Horror, Mystery, Fantasy, Sci-Fi, Romance, Historical, Adventure, Drama, Psychological, Thriller, Comedy, Western, Dystopian, Crime.</p>
                  <p><strong>Tone:</strong> 12 options including Dark, Suspenseful, Dramatic, Poetic, Realistic, Humorous, Inspirational, Melancholic, Optimistic, Cynical, Mysterious, Romantic.</p>
                  <p><strong>Paragraph Length:</strong> 6 levels from Very Short (1-2 lines) to Epic (16-20 lines).</p>
                  <p><strong>Description Density:</strong> 6 levels from Minimal (action-focused) to Ultra-rich (immersive cinematic scenes).</p>
                  <p><strong>Pacing Control:</strong> 5-level slider from very slow (extremely detailed) to very fast (rapid progression).</p>
                  <p><strong>Advanced Options:</strong> Custom writing style, character constraints, forbidden content list, required elements.</p>

                  <h3><span class="ms">search</span> Component Analysis</h3>
                  <p><strong>Auto-Extract:</strong> Click Refresh (<span class="ms">refresh</span>) to automatically extract Characters, Locations, Items, Events, Themes, and Conflicts from your story.</p>
                  <p><strong>Selective Extraction:</strong> Use settings (<span class="ms">settings</span>) to choose which components to extract. Extracted data guides AI generation.</p>
                  <p><strong>Manual Editing:</strong> Edit component boxes directly. AI considers these when generating new content.</p>
                  <p><strong>Perfect Continuity:</strong> AI references all components to maintain story consistency across chapters.</p>

                  <h3><span class="ms">route</span> Story Paths</h3>
                  <p><strong>Auto-Generation:</strong> After each AI Assist, generates 2-10 possible story paths based on current content.</p>
                  <p><strong>Path Styles:</strong> 12 options - Default, Positive, Negative, Tragedy, Twist, Cliffhanger, Revelation, Redemption, Submission, Defiance, Corruption, Obsession.</p>
                  <p><strong>Editable Paths:</strong> Modify any path before selecting. Use ↺ to reset, ➤ to apply to story.</p>
                  <p><strong>Smart Continuation:</strong> Selected path seamlessly continues your narrative with maintained style and tone.</p>

                  <h3><span class="ms">bar_chart</span> Analytics Dashboard</h3>
                  <p><strong>Basic Stats:</strong> Total words, chapter count, average words/chapter, reading time, character count.</p>
                  <p><strong>Content Distribution:</strong> Dialogue vs narrative percentage, average sentence length, average paragraph length.</p>
                  <p><strong>Character Screen Time:</strong> Tracks how often each character appears. Shows top 5 with percentage bars.</p>
                  <p><strong>Readability Score:</strong> Calculates reading level, complexity, unique words, and vocabulary diversity.</p>
                  <p><strong>Emotion Analysis:</strong> Detects emotional tone (Joy, Sadness, Anger, Fear, Love) with percentage distribution.</p>
                  <p><strong>Real-Time Updates:</strong> Click Refresh (<span class="ms">refresh</span>) to analyze current story state instantly.</p>

                  <h3><span class="ms">smart_toy</span> AI Writing Tools</h3>
                  <p><strong><span class="ms">person</span> AI Name Generator:</strong> Generate authentic names from 18 cultures. Select gender, quantity (5-30), output language, and custom requirements.</p>
                  <p><strong><span class="ms">assignment</span> AI Story Templates:</strong> Generate complete story structures for 13 genres with 3-15 chapters.</p>
                  <p><strong><span class="ms">chat</span> Interactive Dialogue:</strong> Generate realistic conversations between any two characters with context awareness.</p>
                  <p><strong><span class="ms">search</span> Consistency Checker:</strong> AI analyzes entire story for plot holes, timeline contradictions, and logic gaps.</p>
                  <p><strong><span class="ms">theater_comedy</span> Character Voice Analyzer:</strong> Analyzes individual character speech patterns and vocabulary.</p>
                  <p><strong><span class="ms">article</span> AI Writing Coach:</strong> Get personalized advice on 6 topics - Plot, Characters, Dialogue, Description, Pacing, Style.</p>
                  <p><strong><span class="ms">visibility</span> Multiple POV Manager:</strong> Add characters as POV options, then switch perspectives seamlessly.</p>
                  <p><strong><span class="ms">fast_rewind</span> Flashback Manager:</strong> Generate well-structured flashbacks with time period, characters, and emotional resonance.</p>
                  <p><strong><span class="ms">calendar_month</span> Timeline Visualizer:</strong> Create interactive story timeline with event plotting on dramatic arc. Three views: Visual, List, Statistics.</p>

                  <h3><span class="ms">folder</span> Chapter Management</h3>
                  <p><strong>Auto-Split:</strong> Stories automatically split at 5000-6000 words.</p>
                  <p><strong>Manual Add:</strong> Click + button anytime to create new chapter.</p>
                  <p><strong>Chapter Tabs:</strong> Double-click to rename. Click × to delete (with confirmation).</p>
                  <p><strong>Smart Summaries:</strong> AI generates detailed summaries preserving all events, characters, and plot threads.</p>

                  <h3><span class="ms">schedule</span> Backup & Recovery</h3>
                  <p><strong>Auto-Backup:</strong> Every 5 minutes automatically. Keeps last 10 backups with timestamps.</p>
                  <p><strong>Manual Backup:</strong> Click <span class="ms">save</span> in editor header anytime.</p>
                  <p><strong>Restore:</strong> View all backups with title, timestamp, word count, and chapter count.</p>

                  <h3><span class="ms">download</span> Export System</h3>
                  <p><strong>Export Dropdown:</strong> 3 format options - Text File (.txt), Markdown (.md), HTML (.html).</p>
                  <p><strong>Combined Export:</strong> All chapters combined automatically with clear separators.</p>
                  <p><strong>HTML Export:</strong> Includes professional styling with Georgia serif font and chapter navigation.</p>

                  <h3><span class="ms">bolt</span> Keyboard Shortcuts</h3>
                  <p><strong>Ctrl+S / ⌘+S:</strong> Save story instantly.</p>
                  <p><strong>Ctrl+G / ⌘+G:</strong> Generate new content with AI Assist.</p>
                  <p><strong>Ctrl+N / ⌘+N:</strong> Create new chapter.</p>
                  <p><strong>F11:</strong> Toggle focus mode - hides sidebar and controls.</p>

                  <h3><span class="ms">palette</span> Themes & Display</h3>
                  <p><strong>Dark Theme:</strong> Default dark mode optimized for extended writing sessions.</p>
                  <p><strong>Light Theme:</strong> Clean white background for daytime use.</p>
                  <p><strong>Kids Theme:</strong> Colorful, friendly design. Auto-enabled with Child-Safe filter.</p>

                  <h3><span class="ms">shield</span> Content Filtering</h3>
                  <p><strong>No Filter (<span class="ms">lock</span>):</strong> All content types allowed. Not suitable for children.</p>
                  <p><strong>Standard Filter (<span class="ms">shield</span>):</strong> Moderate filtering. Suitable for teens and adults.</p>
                  <p><strong>Child-Safe Filter (<span class="ms">palette</span>):</strong> Maximum protection. Only positive, age-appropriate content. Perfect for children under 13.</p>

                  <h3><span class="ms">lightbulb</span> Pro Tips</h3>
                  <p><strong>Start Broad:</strong> Begin with clear setup and characters. Let AI expand details gradually.</p>
                  <p><strong>Use Components:</strong> Regularly run component analysis to help AI track story elements.</p>
                  <p><strong>Leverage Paths:</strong> When stuck, generate paths for fresh direction ideas.</p>
                  <p><strong>Check Consistency:</strong> Run consistency checker after major plot developments.</p>
                  <p><strong>Backup Before Experiments:</strong> Create manual backup before trying risky narrative choices.</p>
                  <p><strong>Focus Mode Writing:</strong> Use F11 when drafting to eliminate distractions.</p>

                  <h3><span class="ms">language</span> Language Support</h3>
                  <p><strong>Auto-Detection:</strong> AI automatically detects story language and generates content in same language.</p>
                  <p><strong>Supported Languages:</strong> Arabic (RTL), English, Chinese, Japanese, Korean, Russian, Hebrew (RTL), Thai, Persian.</p>
                  <p><strong>RTL Support:</strong> Automatic right-to-left text direction for Arabic and Hebrew.</p>

                  <h3><span class="ms">warning</span> Important Notes</h3>
                  <p><strong>Token Limits:</strong> Keep chapters under 10,000 words for best results.</p>
                  <p><strong>Internet Required:</strong> AI features require active internet connection.</p>
                  <p><strong>Browser Storage:</strong> Stories saved in browser. Export regularly for backup.</p>

            <label
               style="padding:14px 16px; border:2px solid var(--bg1); border-radius:10px; cursor:pointer; transition:all 0.2s; display:block"
               onmouseover="this.style.borderColor='#dc2626'; this.style.background='var(--bg3)'"
               onmouseout="this.style.borderColor='var(--bg2)'; this.style.background='var(--bg2)'"
            >
               <input type="radio" name="contentFilter" value="none" style="margin-right:8px; transform:scale(1.2)">
               <strong style="color:#dc2626; font-size:0.95rem"><span class="ms">lock</span> No Filter</strong>
               <p style="margin:4px 0 0 26px; color:#666; font-size:0.8rem; line-height:1.3">All content types allowed. May include mature themes.</p>
               <p style="margin:3px 0 0 26px; color:#dc2626; font-size:0.75rem; font-weight:600">
                  <span class="ms">warning</span> Not suitable for children
               </p>
            </label>

            <!-- فلتر قياسي | Standard Filter -->
            <label
               style="padding:14px 16px; border:2px solid var(--bg1); border-radius:10px; cursor:pointer; transition:all 0.2s; display:block"

<script>
// ============================================================
// منطق التطبيق الرئيسي | Main Application Logic
// ============================================================

// ============================================================
// 2. تهيئة الإضافات الخارجية | External Plugins Initialization
// ============================================================

let copyTextPlugin, downloadPlugin, printPlugin, urlParamsPlugin, seederPlugin;

async function initializePlugins() {
   try {
      [copyTextPlugin, downloadPlugin, printPlugin, urlParamsPlugin, seederPlugin] = await Promise.all([
         import('https://perchance.org/api/copyTextPlugin').catch(() => null),
         import('https://perchance.org/api/downloadPlugin').catch(() => null),
         import('https://perchance.org/api/printPlugin').catch(() => null),
         import('https://perchance.org/api/urlParamsPlugin').catch(() => null),
         import('https://perchance.org/api/seederPlugin').catch(() => null)
      ]);

      // تحميل القصة من URL إن وُجدت | Load story from URL if present
      if (urlParamsPlugin) {
         const storyParam = urlParamsPlugin.get('story');
         if (storyParam) {
            loadStoryFromURL(storyParam);
         }
      }

      console.log('✅ تم تحميل الإضافات بنجاح');
   } catch (e) {
      console.warn('⚠️ فشل تحميل بعض الإضافات:', e);
   }
}


// ============================================================
// 3. دوال التصدير المحسّنة (تستخدم الإضافات) | Enhanced Export Functions
// ============================================================

// تصدير القصة كـ TXT مع دعم الإضافة | Export story as TXT with plugin support
async function exportStory() {
   saveCurrentChapter();
   let title = elements.storyTitle.value.trim() || "Story";
   let fullContent = '';

   window.storyData.chapters.forEach((ch, idx) => {
      if (idx > 0) {
         fullContent += '\n\n' + '='.repeat(80) + '\n';
         fullContent += `${ch.name.toUpperCase()}\n`;
         fullContent += '='.repeat(80) + '\n\n';
      }
      fullContent += ch.content;
   });

   if (!fullContent.trim()) {
      showStatus("Nothing to export");
      return;
   }

   // محاولة الإضافة أولاً، ثم الطريقة البديلة | Try plugin first, fallback to blob
   if (downloadPlugin) {
      try {
         await downloadPlugin.downloadText(fullContent, `${title}.txt`);
         showStatus("Exported to TXT via plugin");
         return;
      } catch (e) {
         console.warn('فشلت إضافة التحميل، استخدام الطريقة البديلة');
      }
   }

   let blob = new Blob([fullContent], { type: "text/plain;charset=utf-8" });
   let url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
   let a = document.createElement("a");
   a.href = url;
   a.download = `${title}.txt`;
   a.click();
   URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
   showStatus("Exported to TXT");
}

// نسخ القصة بالكامل | Quick copy entire story
async function quickCopyStory() {
   saveCurrentChapter();
   let fullContent = elements.storyTitle.value + '\n\n';
   window.storyData.chapters.forEach(ch => {
      fullContent += `${ch.name}\n\n${ch.content}\n\n`;
   });

   if (copyTextPlugin) {
      try {
         await copyTextPlugin.copy(fullContent);
         showStatus("✅ Story copied!");
         return;
      } catch (e) {
         console.warn('فشلت إضافة النسخ، استخدام الطريقة البديلة');
      }
   }

   try {
      await navigator.clipboard.writeText(fullContent);
      showStatus("✅ Story copied!");
   } catch (e) {
      showStatus("❌ Copy failed");
   }
}

// طباعة القصة | Print story
async function printStory() {
   saveCurrentChapter();
   if (printPlugin) {
      try {
         let html = generatePrintableHTML();
         await printPlugin.print(html);
         return;
      } catch (e) {
         console.warn('فشلت إضافة الطباعة، استخدام الطريقة البديلة');
      }
   }
   window.print();
}

// توليد HTML قابل للطباعة | Generate printable HTML
function generatePrintableHTML() {
   let title = elements.storyTitle.value.trim() || "Story";
   let html = `
      <div style="font-family:Georgia,serif;max-width:800px;margin:40px auto;padding:20px">
         <h1 style="text-align:center">${title}</h1>
   `;
   window.storyData.chapters.forEach((ch, idx) => {
      if (idx > 0) html += '<hr style="margin:40px 0">';
      html += `<h2>${ch.name}</h2>`;
      ch.content.split('\n\n').forEach(p => {
         if (p.trim()) html += `<p style="text-indent:2em;line-height:1.8">${p}</p>`;
      });
   });
   html += '</div>';
   return html;
}

// مشاركة القصة عبر رابط | Share story via URL
async function shareStoryViaURL() {
   await saveStory();
   const title = elements.storyTitle.value.trim() || "Untitled";
   const storyId = title.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, '-');

   if (urlParamsPlugin && seederPlugin) {
      try {
         const seed = await seederPlugin.generate(JSON.stringify(window.storyData));
         const shareURL = `${window.location.origin}${window.location.pathname}?story=${storyId}&seed=${seed}`;
         await navigator.clipboard.writeText(shareURL);
         alert(`✅ تم نسخ رابط المشاركة!\n\n${shareURL}\n\nيمكن لأي شخص لديه هذا الرابط تحميل قصتك.`);
         return;
      } catch (e) {
         console.warn('فشلت المشاركة عبر الرابط:', e);
      }
   }
   alert('⚠️ إضافات المشاركة غير متوفرة');
}

// تحميل قصة من رابط | Load story from URL
async function loadStoryFromURL(storyId) {
   try {
      const seed = urlParamsPlugin?.get('seed');
      if (seed && seederPlugin) {
         const data = await seederPlugin.restore(seed);
         Object.assign(window.storyData, JSON.parse(data));
         let chapter = window.storyData.chapters.find(ch => ch.id === window.storyData.currentChapter);
         if (chapter) {
            elements.storyContent.value = chapter.content;
            elements.storyTitle.value = window.storyData.title || '';
         }
         renderChapterTabs();
         updateWordCount();
         showStatus('✅ تم تحميل القصة من الرابط');
      } else {
         await loadStory(storyId);
      }
   } catch (e) {
      console.error('فشل تحميل القصة من الرابط:', e);
   }
}

// ============================================================
// 5. نظام إيقاف الذكاء الاصطناعي | AI Abort System
// ============================================================

let currentAIController    = null;
let isAIRunning            = false;
let shouldAbortGeneration  = false;

// تحديث حالة زر الإيقاف | Update abort button visibility
function setAIRunning(running) {
   isAIRunning = running;
   const globalBtn = document.getElementById('globalAbortBtn');
   if (globalBtn) {
      if (running) {
         globalBtn.style.display = 'inline-flex';
         globalBtn.style.visibility = 'visible';
      } else {
         setTimeout(() => { globalBtn.style.display = 'none'; }, 300);
      }
   }
}

// إيقاف عملية الذكاء الاصطناعي الحالية | Abort current AI operation
function abortCurrentAI() {
   console.log('🛑 تم طلب الإيقاف من المستخدم');
   shouldAbortGeneration = true;

   if (currentAIController) {
      try {
         currentAIController.abort();
      } catch (e) {
         console.warn('فشل إيقاف المتحكم:', e);
      }
      currentAIController = null;
   }

   setAIRunning(false);
   showStatus("❌ Operation cancelled");

   // إخفاء جميع مؤشرات التقدم | Hide all progress indicators
   const allProgress = [
      'storyProgress', 'componentsProgress', 'pathsProgress',
      'timelineProgress', 'nameGeneratorProgress',
      'templateGeneratorProgress', 'dialogueSidebarProgress',
      'consistencySidebarProgress'
   ];
   allProgress.forEach(id => {
      const el = document.getElementById(id);
      if (el) el.style.display = 'none';
   });
}

function abortAllAI() {
   abortCurrentAI();
}

// غلاف generateText مع دعم الإيقاف | Wrapper for generateText with abort support
async function generateTextAbortable(options) {
   shouldAbortGeneration = false;
   const controller = new AbortController();
   currentAIController = controller;
   setAIRunning(true);

   try {
      let aborted = false;
      const originalOnChunk = options.onChunk;

      const wrappedOnChunk = (data) => {
         if (shouldAbortGeneration) {
            console.log('🛑 تم منع chunk بواسطة علم الإيقاف');
            aborted = true;
            throw new Error('Operation cancelled by user');
         }
         if (originalOnChunk) originalOnChunk(data);
      };

      const result = await generateText({
         ...options,
         onChunk: wrappedOnChunk,
         signal: controller.signal
      });

      if (shouldAbortGeneration || aborted) {
         throw new Error('Operation cancelled by user');
      }

      return result;
   } catch (error) {
      if (
         error.name === 'AbortError' ||
         error.message?.includes('abort') ||
         error.message?.includes('cancel') ||
         shouldAbortGeneration
      ) {
         console.log('✅ تم إيقاف التوليد بنجاح');
         throw new Error('Operation cancelled by user');
      }
      throw error;
   } finally {
      if (currentAIController === controller) {
         currentAIController = null;
         setAIRunning(false);
      }
      shouldAbortGeneration = false;
   }
}

// 7. فحص الفلتر عند التحميل | Filter Check on Load
