(function checkFilterOnLoad() {
   let filterAlreadySelected = false;
   try {
      filterAlreadySelected = localStorage.getItem('contentFilterSelected') === 'true';
   } catch (e) {
      console.warn('localStorage غير متاح');
   }

   if (filterAlreadySelected) {
      const modal = document.getElementById('filterSelectionModal');
      if (modal) modal.style.display = 'none';
      initEditor();
   }
})();


// ============================================================
// 8. كشف اللغة والاتجاه | Language Detection & RTL Support
// ============================================================

// فحص وجود نص عربي | Check if text contains Arabic
function hasArabic(text) {
   if (!text || text.length < 10) return false;
   let arabicChars = (text.match(/[\u0600-\u06FF]/g) || []).length;
   let totalChars = text.replace(/\s/g, '').length;
   return totalChars > 0 && (arabicChars / totalChars) > 0.3;
}

// كشف لغة النص | Detect text language
function detectLanguage(text) {
   if (!text || text.length < 10) {
      let storyText = elements.storyTitle.value + ' ' + elements.storyContent.value;
      if (storyText.trim().length > 10) {
         text = storyText;
      } else {
         return 'English';
      }
   }
   if (hasArabic(text))                              return 'Arabic';
   if (/[\u4E00-\u9FFF]/.test(text))                 return 'Chinese';
   if (/[\u3040-\u309F\u30A0-\u30FF]/.test(text))    return 'Japanese';
   if (/[\uAC00-\uD7AF]/.test(text))                 return 'Korean';
   if (/[\u0400-\u04FF]/.test(text))                 return 'Russian';
   if (/[\u0590-\u05FF]/.test(text))                 return 'Hebrew';
   if (/[\u0E00-\u0E7F]/.test(text))                 return 'Thai';
   return 'English';
}

// توليد تعليمات اللغة للـ AI | Generate language instruction for AI prompt
function getLanguageInstruction(contextText = '') {
   let language = detectLanguage(contextText || elements.storyContent.value || elements.storyTitle.value);
   if (language === 'English') return '';
   return `\n\nCRITICAL LANGUAGE REQUIREMENT: You MUST write EVERYTHING in ${language} language. This is non-negotiable. Every word, sentence, and paragraph must be in ${language}.`;
}

// تطبيق اتجاه النص العربي | Apply Arabic RTL direction
function applyArabicStyle(element) {
   if (hasArabic(element.value || element.textContent)) {
      element.style.direction   = 'rtl';
      element.style.textAlign   = 'right';
      element.style.fontFamily  = "'Tajawal',Arial,sans-serif";
   } else {
      element.style.direction   = 'ltr';
      element.style.textAlign   = 'left';
      element.style.fontFamily  = "Arial,sans-serif";
   }
}


// ============================================================
// 9. نظام فلترة المحتوى | Content Filtering System
// ============================================================

// الحصول على تعليمات الفلتر للـ AI | Get filter instructions for AI prompt
function getFilterInstructions() {
   const filter = window.storyData.contentFilter || 'standard';
   const instructions = {
      'none': '',
      'standard': `\n\nCONTENT FILTERING ACTIVE - STANDARD LEVEL:
- Avoid explicit sexual content
- Limit graphic violence descriptions
- Reduce use of strong profanity
- Keep mature themes subtle and tasteful
- Maintain story quality while being mindful of sensitive content`,
      'child': `\n\nCONTENT FILTERING ACTIVE - CHILD-SAFE LEVEL (STRICT):
MANDATORY REQUIREMENTS:
- NO violence, death, or scary content
- NO romantic or sexual themes
- NO profanity or inappropriate language
- NO dark, frightening, or disturbing scenarios
- NO alcohol, drugs, or dangerous activities
- ONLY positive, educational, and age-appropriate content
- Focus on: friendship, adventure, learning, kindness, fun, imagination
- Use simple, clear language suitable for children ages 6-12
- Include positive messages and moral lessons
- Create uplifting, encouraging, and joyful narratives`
   };
   return instructions[filter] || instructions['standard'];
}

// اسم الفلتر للعرض | Get display name of filter
function getFilterDisplayName(filter) {
   const names = {
      'none':     'No Filter',
      'standard': 'Standard Filter',
      'child':    'Child-Safe Filter'
   };
   return names[filter] || 'Unknown';
}

// تحديث شارة الفلتر في الرأس | Update filter badge in header
function updateFilterBadge() {
   const badge = document.querySelector('.filter-badge');
   if (!badge) return;

   const filter = window.storyData.contentFilter || 'standard';
   const badgeClass = filter === 'none' ? 'filter-none' : filter === 'standard' ? 'filter-standard' : 'filter-child';
   const filterIcons = { 'none': 'lock', 'standard': 'shield', 'child': 'palette' };

   badge.className = `filter-badge ${badgeClass}`;
   badge.style.cursor = 'pointer';
   badge.setAttribute('onclick', 'openFilterSettings()');
   badge.innerHTML = `<span class="ms" style="font-size:14px">${filterIcons[filter]}</span> <span id="filterBadgeText">${getFilterDisplayName(filter)}</span>`;
}

// تطبيق الفلتر المختار في البداية | Apply initial filter selection
function applyInitialFilter() {
   const selected = document.querySelector('input[name="contentFilter"]:checked');
   if (!selected) {
      alert('Please select a content filter level');
      return;
   }

   window.storyData.contentFilter = selected.value;

   try {
      localStorage.setItem('contentFilterSelected', 'true');
      localStorage.setItem('contentFilterValue', selected.value);
   } catch (e) {
      console.warn('localStorage غير متاح:', e);
   }

   if (selected.value === 'child') {
      window.storyData.theme = 'kids';
   }

   document.getElementById('filterSelectionModal').style.display = 'none';
   initEditor();
   updateFilterBadge();
   showStatus(`Content filter set to: ${getFilterDisplayName(selected.value)}`);
}

// فتح نافذة تغيير الفلتر | Open filter settings modal
function openFilterSettings() {
   const modal = document.createElement('div');
   modal.id = 'filterSettingsModal';
   modal.style.cssText = 'display:flex;position:fixed;top:0;left:0;width:100%;height:100%;background:var(--ovr1);z-index:9999;align-items:center;justify-content:center';

   const currentFilter = window.storyData.contentFilter || 'standard';
   modal.innerHTML = `
      <div style="background:var(--bg2);padding:30px;border-radius:12px;max-width:500px;border:1px solid var(--brd2)">
         <h3 style="margin:0 0 20px 0;color:var(--txt1)">Change Content Filter</h3>
         <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:12px;margin-bottom:25px">
            <label style="padding:15px;border:2px solid var(--brd1);border-radius:8px;cursor:pointer;display:block;${currentFilter === 'none' ? 'background:var(--acc3)' : ''}">
               <input type="radio" name="newFilter" value="none" ${currentFilter === 'none' ? 'checked' : ''} style="margin-right:8px">
               <strong style="color:var(--dng1)"><span class="ms">lock</span> No Filter</strong>
               <small style="display:block;margin-top:4px;color:var(--txt2);margin-left:24px">All content allowed</small>
            </label>
            <label style="padding:15px;border:2px solid var(--brd1);border-radius:8px;cursor:pointer;display:block;${currentFilter === 'standard' ? 'background:var(--acc3)' : ''}">
               <input type="radio" name="newFilter" value="standard" ${currentFilter === 'standard' ? 'checked' : ''} style="margin-right:8px">
               <strong style="color:var(--wrn)"><span class="ms">shield</span> Standard Filter</strong>
               <small style="display:block;margin-top:4px;color:var(--txt2);margin-left:24px">Moderate filtering</small>
            </label>
            <label style="padding:15px;border:2px solid var(--brd1);border-radius:8px;cursor:pointer;display:block;${currentFilter === 'child' ? 'background:var(--acc3)' : ''}">
               <input type="radio" name="newFilter" value="child" ${currentFilter === 'child' ? 'checked' : ''} style="margin-right:8px">
               <strong style="color:var(--suc1)"><span class="ms">palette</span> Child-Safe Filter</strong>
               <small style="display:block;margin-top:4px;color:var(--txt2);margin-left:24px">Maximum protection + Kids theme</small>
            </label>
         </div>
         <div style="display:flex;gap:10px;justify-content:flex-end">
            <button onclick="closeFilterSettings()" class="btn-secondary">Cancel</button>
            <button onclick="applyFilterChange()" class="btn-success">Apply</button>
         </div>
      </div>
   `;
   document.body.appendChild(modal);
}

function closeFilterSettings() {
   const modal = document.getElementById('filterSettingsModal');
   if (modal) modal.remove();
}

// تطبيق تغيير الفلتر | Apply filter change
function applyFilterChange() {
   const selected = document.querySelector('input[name="newFilter"]:checked');
   if (!selected) return;

   const oldFilter = window.storyData.contentFilter;
   const newFilter = selected.value;

   if (oldFilter === newFilter) {
      closeFilterSettings();
      return;
   }

   // تحذير عند الانتقال لفلتر أقل تقييداً | Warn when lowering restriction
   if ((oldFilter === 'child' && newFilter !== 'child') || (oldFilter === 'standard' && newFilter === 'none')) {
      if (!confirm('Warning: You are switching to a less restrictive content filter. This may allow inappropriate content. Continue?')) {
         return;
      }
   }

   window.storyData.contentFilter = newFilter;

   if (newFilter === 'child') {
      initializeChildSafety();
      if (window.storyData.theme !== 'kids') {
         window.storyData.theme = 'kids';
         applyTheme();
      }
   }

   // العودة للثيم الداكن عند إلغاء ثيم الأطفال | Revert kids theme when filter changes
   if (newFilter !== 'child' && window.storyData.theme === 'kids') {
      window.storyData.theme = 'dark';
      applyTheme();
   }

   updateFilterBadge();
   closeFilterSettings();
   saveStory();
   showStatus(`Content filter changed to: ${getFilterDisplayName(newFilter)}`);
}


// ============================================================
// 10. إدارة السمات (الثيمات) | Theme Management
// ============================================================

// تبديل السمة | Toggle between themes
function toggleTheme() {
   if (window.storyData.contentFilter === 'child') {
      window.storyData.theme = 'kids';
   } else {
      window.storyData.theme = window.storyData.theme === 'dark' ? 'light' : 'dark';
   }
   applyTheme();
   saveStory();
}

// تطبيق السمة على المستند | Apply theme to document
function applyTheme() {
   const theme = window.storyData.theme || 'dark';
   document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme', theme);
   document.body.style.background = getComputedStyle(document.documentElement).getPropertyValue('--bg1').trim();

   const themeIcon = document.getElementById('themeIcon');
   if (themeIcon) {
      const themeIconMap = { 'dark': 'dark_mode', 'light': 'light_mode', 'kids': 'palette' };
      themeIcon.innerHTML = `<span class="ms">${themeIconMap[theme] || 'dark_mode'}</span>`;
   }
}


// ============================================================
// 11. وضع ملء الشاشة ووضع التركيز | Fullscreen & Focus Mode
// ============================================================

// تبديل ملء الشاشة | Toggle fullscreen
function toggleFullscreen() {
   if (!document.fullscreenElement) {
      document.documentElement.requestFullscreen().catch(err => {
         console.error('فشل الدخول إلى وضع ملء الشاشة:', err);
         showStatus('Fullscreen not supported');
      });
   } else {
      if (document.exitFullscreen) document.exitFullscreen();
   }
}

// تحديث أيقونة زر ملء الشاشة | Update fullscreen button icon
document.addEventListener('fullscreenchange', () => {
   const btn = document.getElementById('fullscreenBtn');
   if (btn) {
      if (document.fullscreenElement) {
         btn.innerHTML = '<span class="ms">fullscreen_exit</span>';
         btn.title = 'Exit Fullscreen (F12)';
      } else {
         btn.innerHTML = '<span class="ms">fullscreen</span>';
         btn.title = 'Fullscreen (F12)';
      }
   }
});

// تبديل وضع التركيز (إخفاء الشريط الجانبي والتحكم) | Toggle focus mode
function toggleFocusMode() {
   window.storyData.focusMode = !window.storyData.focusMode;
   applyFocusMode();
}

function applyFocusMode() {
   if (window.storyData.focusMode) {
      elements.sidebar.style.display = 'none';
      elements.resizer.style.display = 'none';
      elements.chapterTabsSection.style.display = 'none';
      elements.controlsSection.style.display = 'none';
      elements.editorHeader.style.display = 'none';
   } else {
      elements.sidebar.style.removeProperty('display');
      elements.resizer.style.removeProperty('display');
      elements.chapterTabsSection.style.removeProperty('display');
      elements.controlsSection.style.removeProperty('display');
      elements.editorHeader.style.removeProperty('display');
   }
}


// ============================================================
// 12. إدارة الإعدادات | Settings Management
// ============================================================

// عرض/إخفاء لوحة الإعدادات | Toggle settings panel
function toggleSettings() {
   if (elements.settingsPanel.style.display === 'none' || !elements.settingsPanel.style.display) {
      elements.settingsPanel.style.display = 'block';
      loadSettings();
   } else {
      elements.settingsPanel.style.display = 'none';
      saveSettings();
   }
}

// تحميل الإعدادات المحفوظة إلى عناصر DOM | Load saved settings into DOM
function loadSettings() {
   if (!window.storyData || !window.storyData.settings) return;
   elements.genreSelect.value         = window.storyData.settings.genre || '';
   elements.toneSelect.value          = window.storyData.settings.tone || '';
   elements.paraLenSelect.value       = window.storyData.settings.paraLen || '';
   elements.descDensitySelect.value   = window.storyData.settings.descDensity || '';
   elements.pacingSlider.value        = window.storyData.settings.pacing || 3;
   document.getElementById('pacingVal').textContent = elements.pacingSlider.value;
   elements.customStyleInput.value    = window.storyData.settings.customStyle || '';
   elements.charConstraintsInput.value= window.storyData.settings.charConstraints || '';
   elements.forbiddenInput.value      = window.storyData.settings.forbidden || '';
   elements.requiredInput.value       = window.storyData.settings.required || '';
}

// حفظ الإعدادات من عناصر DOM | Save settings from DOM elements
function saveSettings() {
   if (!window.storyData) return;
   window.storyData.settings = {
      genre:           elements.genreSelect.value,
      tone:            elements.toneSelect.value,
      paraLen:         elements.paraLenSelect.value,
      descDensity:     elements.descDensitySelect.value,
      pacing:          parseInt(elements.pacingSlider.value),
      customStyle:     elements.customStyleInput.value,
      charConstraints: elements.charConstraintsInput.value,
      forbidden:       elements.forbiddenInput.value,
      required:        elements.requiredInput.value
   };
}

// بناء تعليمات الإعدادات للـ AI | Build settings instructions for AI prompt
function getSettingsInstructions() {
   saveSettings();
   let instructions = '';

   if (window.storyData.settings.genre) {
      let genreMap = {
         'horror':       'Horror genre with frightening, suspenseful elements',
         'mystery':      'Mystery genre with clues, investigation, and revelation',
         'fantasy':      'Fantasy genre with magical elements and fantastical worlds',
         'scifi':        'Science fiction with futuristic technology and concepts',
         'romance':      'Romance genre focusing on relationships and emotional connections',
         'historical':   'Historical setting with period-accurate details',
         'adventure':    'Adventure genre with exciting quests and challenges',
         'drama':        'Dramatic genre with emotional depth and character conflict',
         'psychological':'Psychological focus on mental states and motivations',
         'thriller':     'Thriller with high tension and suspense',
         'comedy':       'Comedy with humor and lighthearted moments',
         'western':      'Western setting with frontier themes',
         'dystopian':    'Dystopian future with societal breakdown',
         'crime':        'Crime fiction with investigation and criminal elements'
      };
      instructions += `\nGenre: ${genreMap[window.storyData.settings.genre] || window.storyData.settings.genre}`;
   }

   if (window.storyData.settings.tone) {
      let toneMap = {
         'dark':          'Dark, ominous tone with heavy atmosphere',
         'suspenseful':   'Suspenseful, tension-filled tone',
         'dramatic':      'Dramatic, emotionally charged tone',
         'poetic':        'Poetic, lyrical prose with beautiful imagery',
         'realistic':     'Realistic, grounded tone',
         'humorous':      'Humorous, light tone with comedic elements',
         'inspirational': 'Inspirational, uplifting tone',
         'melancholic':   'Melancholic, sad tone',
         'optimistic':    'Optimistic, hopeful tone',
         'cynical':       'Cynical, skeptical tone',
         'mysterious':    'Mysterious, enigmatic tone',
         'romantic':      'Romantic, passionate tone'
      };
      instructions += `\nTone: ${toneMap[window.storyData.settings.tone] || window.storyData.settings.tone}`;
   }

   let pacingDesc = ['very slow, extremely detailed', 'slow, highly detailed', 'moderate, balanced detail', 'fast, action-focused', 'very fast, rapid progression'][window.storyData.settings.pacing - 1];
   instructions += `\nPacing: ${pacingDesc}`;

   if (window.storyData.settings.paraLen) {
      let paraMap = {
         'veryshort': '1-2 sentence paragraphs for sharp, punchy prose',
         'short':     '3-5 sentence paragraphs for quick pacing',
         'medium':    '6-8 sentence paragraphs for balanced flow',
         'long':      '9-12 sentence paragraphs for detailed scenes',
         'verylong':  '13-15 sentence paragraphs for immersive depth',
         'epic':      '16-20 sentence paragraphs for epic, elaborate scenes'
      };
      instructions += `\nParagraph length: ${paraMap[window.storyData.settings.paraLen]}`;
   }

   if (window.storyData.settings.descDensity) {
      let descMap = {
         'minimal':   'Minimal descriptions, action-focused with sparse details',
         'sparse':    'Sparse descriptions, brief and concise',
         'moderate':  'Moderate descriptions, balanced approach',
         'rich':      'Rich, detailed descriptions engaging multiple senses',
         'veryrich':  'Very rich, elaborate descriptions with extensive sensory detail',
         'ultrarich': 'Ultra-rich, immersive descriptions creating vivid, cinematic scenes'
      };
      instructions += `\nDescription density: ${descMap[window.storyData.settings.descDensity]}`;
   }

   if (window.storyData.settings.customStyle)     instructions += `\nWriting style: ${window.storyData.settings.customStyle}`;
   if (window.storyData.settings.charConstraints) instructions += `\nCharacter constraints: ${window.storyData.settings.charConstraints}`;
   if (window.storyData.settings.forbidden)       instructions += `\n\nFORBIDDEN CONTENT (NEVER include): ${window.storyData.settings.forbidden}`;
   if (window.storyData.settings.required)        instructions += `\nRequired elements to include: ${window.storyData.settings.required}`;

   return instructions;
}


// ============================================================
// 13. إعدادات مكونات القصة | Story Components Settings
// ============================================================

// إظهار/إخفاء خيارات الاستخراج | Toggle component extraction options
function toggleComponentSettings() {
   elements.componentSettings.style.display = elements.componentSettings.style.display === 'none' ? 'block' : 'none';
   updateComponentVisibility();
}

// تحديث ظهور أقسام المكونات | Update visibility of component sections
function updateComponentVisibility() {
   document.getElementById('charactersSection').style.display = document.getElementById('extractCharacters').checked ? 'block' : 'none';
   document.getElementById('locationsSection').style.display  = document.getElementById('extractLocations').checked  ? 'block' : 'none';
   document.getElementById('itemsSection').style.display      = document.getElementById('extractItems').checked      ? 'block' : 'none';
   document.getElementById('eventsSection').style.display     = document.getElementById('extractEvents').checked     ? 'block' : 'none';
   document.getElementById('themesSection').style.display     = document.getElementById('extractThemes').checked     ? 'block' : 'none';
   document.getElementById('conflictsSection').style.display  = document.getElementById('extractConflicts').checked  ? 'block' : 'none';
}


// ============================================================
// 14. إدارة الفصول | Chapter Management
// ============================================================

// رسم ألسنة الفصول | Render chapter tabs
function renderChapterTabs() {
   let tabsHtml = '';
   window.storyData.chapters.forEach((ch) => {
      let active     = ch.id === window.storyData.currentChapter ? 'active' : '';
      let wordCount  = ch.content.trim() ? ch.content.trim().split(/\s+/).length : 0;
      let canDelete  = window.storyData.chapters.length > 1
         ? `<span class="chapter-close" onclick="event.stopPropagation();deleteChapter(${ch.id})"><span class="ms">close</span></span>`
         : '';

      tabsHtml += `<button class="chapter-tab ${active}" onclick="switchChapter(${ch.id})" ondblclick="editChapterName(${ch.id})">
         <span class="chapter-label">${ch.name} (${wordCount}w)</span>
         ${canDelete}
      </button>`;
   });

   tabsHtml += `<button id="addChapterBtn" onclick="addNewChapterManual()" class="add-chapter-btn" title="Add New Chapter">
      <span class="ms">add</span>
   </button>`;

   elements.chapterTabsContainer.innerHTML = tabsHtml;
}

// حذف فصل | Delete a chapter
function deleteChapter(chapterId) {
   if (window.storyData.chapters.length <= 1) {
      alert("Cannot delete the last chapter.");
      return;
   }
   let chapter = window.storyData.chapters.find(ch => ch.id === chapterId);
   if (!chapter) return;
   if (!confirm(`Delete "${chapter.name}"? This cannot be undone.`)) return;

   window.storyData.chapters = window.storyData.chapters.filter(ch => ch.id !== chapterId);

   if (window.storyData.currentChapter === chapterId) {
      window.storyData.currentChapter = window.storyData.chapters[0].id;
      let newChapter = window.storyData.chapters[0];
      elements.storyContent.value    = newChapter.content;
      elements.storyContent.readOnly = newChapter.readonly || false;
      applyArabicStyle(elements.storyContent);
   }

   // جعل الفصل الأخير قابلاً للتعديل | Ensure last chapter is editable
   let lastChapter = window.storyData.chapters[window.storyData.chapters.length - 1];
   if (lastChapter) {
      lastChapter.readonly = false;
      if (window.storyData.currentChapter === lastChapter.id) {
         elements.storyContent.readOnly = false;
      }
   }

   updateWordCount();
   renderChapterTabs();
   showStatus("Chapter deleted");
}

// تعديل اسم الفصل | Edit chapter name
function editChapterName(chapterId) {
   editingChapterId = chapterId;
   let chapter = window.storyData.chapters.find(ch => ch.id === chapterId);
   if (chapter) {
      document.getElementById('chapterNameInput').value = chapter.name;
      document.getElementById('chapterNameModal').style.display = 'flex';
   }
}

function closeChapterNameModal() {
   document.getElementById('chapterNameModal').style.display = 'none';
   editingChapterId = null;
}

function saveChapterName() {
   if (editingChapterId) {
      let chapter = window.storyData.chapters.find(ch => ch.id === editingChapterId);
      if (chapter) {
         let newName = document.getElementById('chapterNameInput').value.trim();
         if (newName) {
            chapter.name = newName;
            renderChapterTabs();
         }
      }
   }
   closeChapterNameModal();
}

// التبديل بين الفصول | Switch active chapter
function switchChapter(chapterId) {
   if (isCreatingChapter) {
      showStatus("Please wait, creating chapter...");
      return;
   }
   saveCurrentChapter();
   window.storyData.currentChapter = chapterId;
   let chapter = window.storyData.chapters.find(ch => ch.id === chapterId);
   if (chapter) {
      elements.storyContent.value    = chapter.content;
      elements.storyContent.readOnly = chapter.readonly || false;
      elements.storyContent.disabled = false;
      applyArabicStyle(elements.storyContent);
      updateWordCount();
      renderChapterTabs();
      elements.newChapterBtn.style.display  = 'none';
      elements.chapterWarning.style.display = 'none';
   }
}

// حفظ محتوى الفصل الحالي | Save current chapter content
function saveCurrentChapter() {
   if (!window.storyData || !window.storyData.chapters) return;
   let chapter = window.storyData.chapters.find(ch => ch.id === window.storyData.currentChapter);
   if (chapter && !chapter.readonly && elements.storyContent) {
      chapter.content = elements.storyContent.value;
   }
}

// إضافة فصل جديد يدوياً مع ملخص وفقرة افتتاحية | Add new chapter manually with summary + opening
async function addNewChapterManual() {
   if (isCreatingChapter && arguments.length === 0) {
      console.log('جاري إنشاء فصل بالفعل');
      return;
   }
   saveCurrentChapter();

   let lastChapter = window.storyData.chapters[window.storyData.chapters.length - 1];
   if (!lastChapter.content.trim()) {
      alert("Last chapter is empty. Add content before creating a new chapter.");
      return;
   }
   if (lastChapter.readonly && window.storyData.chapters.length > 1) {
      console.log('الفصل الأخير للقراءة فقط، التبديل إليه');
      switchChapter(lastChapter.id);
      return;
   }

   showStatus("Creating comprehensive summary...");
   elements.storyProgress.style.display = 'flex';
   elements.storyContent.disabled = true;

   try {
      const allContent        = getAllChaptersContent();
      let languageInstruction = getLanguageInstruction(allContent);
      let filterInstructions  = getFilterInstructions();

      // توليد ملخص شامل | Generate comprehensive summary
      let summaryResult = await generateTextAbortable({
         instruction: `Create a COMPREHENSIVE summary of this entire story so far. This summary will be used to maintain PERFECT continuity in the next chapter.

Include:
1. All major plot events in chronological order
2. All character relationships, developments, and current emotional states
3. All important locations and their significance
4. All key items/objects and their roles
5. Unresolved plot threads and tensions
6. The current situation and where the story stands now

Be detailed and thorough - this is critical for story continuity.${languageInstruction}${filterInstructions}

Story so far:
${allContent}`,
         temperature: 0.2
      });

      lastChapter.summary  = summaryResult.trim();
      lastChapter.readonly = true;

      let newId = Math.max(...window.storyData.chapters.map(ch => ch.id)) + 1;
      let newChapter = { id: newId, name: `Chapter ${newId}`, content: '', summary: '', readonly: false };
      window.storyData.chapters.push(newChapter);
      window.storyData.currentChapter = newId;

      showStatus("Generating opening paragraph...");

      // توليد الفقرة الافتتاحية للفصل الجديد | Generate opening paragraph for new chapter
      let openingText = '';
      await generateTextAbortable({
         instruction: `Based on this story summary, write the opening paragraph for the next chapter. Continue seamlessly from where the story left off.

CRITICAL INSTRUCTIONS:
- Write ONLY the opening paragraph (6-8 sentences)
- Match the exact writing style, tone, and language of the previous chapters
- Reference recent events naturally
- Maintain perfect continuity with all characters and plot threads
- DO NOT summarize - write active narrative${languageInstruction}${filterInstructions}

Story Summary:
${summaryResult}

Previous chapter ended with:
${lastChapter.content.slice(-1000)}

Write the opening paragraph for ${newChapter.name}:`,
         temperature: 0.7,
         onChunk: (data) => { openingText += data.textChunk; }
      });

      newChapter.content = openingText.trim() + '\n\n';
      elements.storyContent.value    = newChapter.content;
      elements.storyContent.readOnly = false;
      elements.storyContent.disabled = false;
      applyArabicStyle(elements.storyContent);
      updateWordCount();
      renderChapterTabs();
      elements.newChapterBtn.style.display  = 'none';
      elements.chapterWarning.style.display = 'none';
      showStatus("New chapter created with opening paragraph");
   } catch (e) {
      showStatus("Error creating chapter");
      console.error(e);
      elements.storyContent.disabled = false;
   } finally {
      elements.storyProgress.style.display = 'none';
      elements.storyContent.disabled = false;
   }
}

// إنشاء فصل جديد مع حماية من التشغيل المتكرر | Create chapter with duplicate-run protection
async function createNewChapter() {
   if (isCreatingChapter) {
      console.log('جاري إنشاء فصل بالفعل، تخطي...');
      return;
   }
   isCreatingChapter = true;
   try {
      await addNewChapterManual();
   } catch (e) {
      console.error('خطأ في إنشاء الفصل:', e);
      showStatus('خطأ في إنشاء الفصل');
   } finally {
      isCreatingChapter = false;
   }
}

// فحص حد الكلمات وتحفيز إنشاء فصل جديد تلقائياً | Check word limit and trigger auto chapter
function checkChapterLimit() {
   if (isCreatingChapter) {
      elements.newChapterBtn.style.display  = 'none';
      elements.chapterWarning.style.display = 'none';
      return;
   }
   if (checkChapterTimeout) clearTimeout(checkChapterTimeout);
   checkChapterTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
      let currentChapter = window.storyData.chapters.find(ch => ch.id === window.storyData.currentChapter);
      if (!currentChapter || currentChapter.readonly) {
         elements.newChapterBtn.style.display  = 'none';
         elements.chapterWarning.style.display = 'none';
         return;
      }
      let count = elements.storyContent.value.trim() ? elements.storyContent.value.trim().split(/\s+/).length : 0;

      if (count >= 5000 && count <= 6000) {
         elements.newChapterBtn.style.display  = 'inline-block';
         elements.chapterWarning.style.display = 'inline';
         elements.chapterWarning.textContent   = '⚠️ Ready for new chapter!';
      } else if (count > 6000 && !isCreatingChapter) {
         elements.newChapterBtn.style.display  = 'none';
         elements.chapterWarning.style.display = 'inline';
         elements.chapterWarning.textContent   = '⏳ Creating new chapter...';
         createNewChapter();
      } else {
         elements.newChapterBtn.style.display  = 'none';
         elements.chapterWarning.style.display = 'none';
      }
   }, 2000);
}


// ============================================================
// 15. توليد القصة الرئيسي | Core Story Generation
// ============================================================

async function _generateContentCore() {
   if (isCreatingChapter) {
      showStatus("Please wait, creating chapter...");
      return;
   }

   let currentContent  = elements.storyContent.value;
   let title           = elements.storyTitle.value;
   let chars           = elements.charactersBox.value;
   let locs            = elements.locationsBox.value;
   let items           = elements.itemsBox.value;
   let previousSummaries = '';

   let currentChapter  = window.storyData.chapters.find(ch => ch.id === window.storyData.currentChapter);
   let previousChapters= window.storyData.chapters.filter(ch => ch.id < window.storyData.currentChapter);

   // بناء ملخصات الفصول السابقة | Build previous chapters summaries
   if (previousChapters.length > 0) {
      previousSummaries = '\n\nPREVIOUS CHAPTERS COMPREHENSIVE SUMMARY:\n';
      previousChapters.forEach(ch => {
         if (ch.summary) previousSummaries += `\n${ch.name}:\n${ch.summary}\n`;
      });
   }

   let contextInfo = "";
   if (chars) contextInfo += `\n\nKnown Characters:\n${chars}`;
   if (locs)  contextInfo += `\n\nKnown Locations:\n${locs}`;
   if (items) contextInfo += `\n\nKnown Items:\n${items}`;

   let settingsInfo        = getSettingsInstructions();
   let languageInstruction = getLanguageInstruction(currentContent);
   let filterInstructions  = getFilterInstructions();

   showStatus("Generating story...");
   elements.storyProgress.style.display = 'flex';

   try {
      let promptInstructions = `You are a master storyteller. Create extremely realistic, logical narratives with:
- MAXIMUM REALISM: Every action must be completely believable
- RICH CHARACTERS: As many unique characters as possible with distinct personalities
- DIALOG-HEAVY: Extensive conversations dominating the narrative
- SLOW PROGRESSION: Describe only the next 10 minutes in extreme detail
- PERFECT CONTINUITY: Reference all previous elements consistently
- METICULOUS DETAIL: Engage all five senses in every scene
- LOGICAL FLOW: Every action has clear cause and reasonable effect${settingsInfo}${languageInstruction}${filterInstructions}${previousSummaries}${contextInfo}`;

      let prompt;
      if (currentContent) {
         prompt = `${promptInstructions}\n\nContinue this story (${currentChapter.name}) titled "${title}":\n\n${currentContent}\n\nContinue from here with the next 10 minutes in extreme detail:`;
      } else {
         prompt = `${promptInstructions}\n\nWrite the ${previousChapters.length > 0 ? 'next chapter of this' : 'beginning of a new'} story${title ? ' titled "' + title + '"' : ''}. Start with ${previousChapters.length > 0 ? 'continuing the narrative' : 'the first 10 minutes'} in extreme detail:`;
      }

      let startLength = elements.storyContent.value.length;
      await generateTextAbortable({
         instruction: prompt,
         onChunk: (data) => {
            if (shouldAbortGeneration) return;
            elements.storyContent.value += data.textChunk;
            updateWordCount();
            applyArabicStyle(elements.storyContent);
            elements.storyContent.scrollTop = elements.storyContent.scrollHeight;
            checkChapterLimit();
         }
      });

      if (elements.storyContent.value.length > startLength) {
         elements.storyContent.value += '\n\n';
         elements.storyContent.scrollTop = elements.storyContent.scrollHeight;
      }

      showStatus("Story generated");
      await generatePaths();
   } catch (error) {
      showStatus("Generation error");
      console.error(error);
   } finally {
      elements.storyProgress.style.display = 'none';
   }
}


// ============================================================
// 16. تحليل مكونات القصة | Story Components Analysis
// ============================================================

async function analyzeStory() {
   let text = elements.storyContent.value;
   if (!text || text.length < 100) {
      showStatus("No story to analyze");
      return;
   }

   showStatus("Analyzing components...");
   elements.componentsProgress.style.display = 'flex';

   // الخريطة: اسم القسم → العنصر والـ checkbox | Section name → element & checkbox
   const SECTION_MAP = [
      { key: 'CHARACTERS', checkId: 'extractCharacters', el: elements.charactersBox },
      { key: 'LOCATIONS',  checkId: 'extractLocations',  el: elements.locationsBox  },
      { key: 'ITEMS',      checkId: 'extractItems',       el: elements.itemsBox      },
      { key: 'EVENTS',     checkId: 'extractEvents',      el: elements.eventsBox     },
      { key: 'THEMES',     checkId: 'extractThemes',      el: elements.themesBox     },
      { key: 'CONFLICTS',  checkId: 'extractConflicts',   el: elements.conflictsBox  }
   ];

   let active = SECTION_MAP.filter(s => document.getElementById(s.checkId).checked);
   if (active.length === 0) {
      showStatus("Select at least one component type");
      elements.componentsProgress.style.display = 'none';
      return;
   }

   let languageInstruction = getLanguageInstruction(text);
   let filterInstructions  = getFilterInstructions();

   // بناء مثال للـ format بدون placeholders محيرة | Build format example without confusing placeholders
   const formatExample = active.map(s =>
      `${s.key}:\nName 1: description\nName 2: description`
   ).join('\n\n');

   const keysPattern = active.map(s => s.key).join('|');

   try {
      let result = await generateTextAbortable({
         instruction: `Extract story components. Reply ONLY in this exact format, nothing else:

${formatExample}

Rules:
- Use the EXACT section headers shown above (ALL CAPS with colon)
- One item per line: "Name: brief description"
- No bullets, no numbering, no extra commentary${languageInstruction}${filterInstructions}

Story text:
${text.slice(-4000)}`,
         temperature: 0.2
      });

      // تقسيم على رؤوس الأقسام مع دعم بداية النص والحروف المختلطة
      // Split on section headers — handles start-of-string & mixed case
      const headerRegex = new RegExp(`(?:^|\\n)(?=(${keysPattern})\\s*:)`, 'i');
      const parts = result.split(headerRegex).filter(p => p.trim());

      // بناء map: headerKey → content | Build map: headerKey → content
      const parsed = {};
      for (let i = 0; i < parts.length; i++) {
         const headerMatch = parts[i].match(new RegExp(`^(${keysPattern})\\s*:`, 'i'));
         if (headerMatch) {
            const key     = headerMatch[1].toUpperCase();
            const rawBody = parts[i].slice(headerMatch[0].length);
            // تصفية الأسطر الفارغة ونصوص الـ placeholder | Filter empty lines & placeholder text
            parsed[key] = rawBody
               .split('\n')
               .map(l => l.trim())
               .filter(l => l && !l.startsWith('[') && l.includes(':'))
               .join('\n');
         }
      }

      // تطبيق النتائج على العناصر | Apply results to DOM elements
      active.forEach(s => {
         const content = parsed[s.key];
         if (content) {
            s.el.value = content;
            applyArabicStyle(s.el);
         }
      });

      showStatus("Analysis complete");
   } catch (e) {
      showStatus("Analysis error");
      console.error(e);
   } finally {
      elements.componentsProgress.style.display = 'none';
   }
}


// ============================================================
// 17. توليد مسارات القصة | Story Paths Generation
// ============================================================

function togglePathSettings() {
   elements.pathSettings.style.display = elements.pathSettings.style.display === 'none' ? 'block' : 'none';
}

function getPathStyle() {
   let selected = document.querySelector('input[name="pathStyle"]:checked');
   return selected ? selected.value : '';
}

async function generatePaths() {
   let cnt = elements.storyContent.value;
   if (!cnt || cnt.length < 200) return;

   elements.pathsProgress.style.display = 'flex';

   let lang   = detectLanguage(cnt);
   let li     = lang !== 'English' ? `\n\nIMPORTANT: Respond in ${lang}.` : '';
   let filterInstructions = getFilterInstructions();
   let pst    = getPathStyle();
   let si     = '';

   // خريطة أنماط المسارات | Path style instructions map
   if (pst) {
      let styleMap = {
         positive:    '\n\nAll paths should lead to POSITIVE outcomes for the protagonist.',
         negative:    '\n\nAll paths should lead to NEGATIVE outcomes for the protagonist.',
         tragedy:     '\n\nAll paths should unfold as a TRAGEDY with inevitable downfall.',
         redemption:  '\n\nAll paths should focus on REDEMPTION and moral recovery.',
         twist:       '\n\nAll paths should include MAJOR PLOT TWISTS.',
         cliffhanger: '\n\nAll paths should end in a CLIFFHANGER.',
         revelation:  '\n\nAll paths should reveal a CRITICAL TRUTH.',
         Submission:  '\n\nAll paths should lead to SUBMISSION and acceptance of control or fate.',
         Defiance:    '\n\nAll paths should emphasize DEFIANCE and resistance.',
         Corruption:  '\n\nAll paths should explore gradual CORRUPTION.',
         Obsession:   '\n\nAll paths should revolve around OBSESSION with a single goal.'
      };
      si = styleMap[pst] || '';
   }

   let pathsCount  = parseInt(document.getElementById('pathsCount')?.value || 5, 10);
   let pathsLength = parseInt(document.getElementById('pathsLengthSlider')?.value || 30, 10);
   let pathsType   = document.getElementById('pathsTypeSelect')?.value || 'detailed';

   try {
      // بناء تعليمات النوع | Build type instructions
      const typeInstructionMap = {
         'detailed': `Write each path as a DETAILED narrative direction (around ${pathsLength} words each). Include character actions, emotional beats, and scene details.`,
         'brief':    `Write each path as a SHORT quick idea (around ${pathsLength} words each). Keep it concise and punchy — just the core concept.`,
         'mixed':    `Alternate between DETAILED paths (around ${pathsLength} words) and SHORT quick ideas (around ${Math.round(pathsLength * 0.4)} words). Label them: [Detailed] or [Quick].`
      };
      const typeInstruction = typeInstructionMap[pathsType] || typeInstructionMap['detailed'];

      let response = await generateTextAbortable({
         instruction: `Based on this story, suggest ${pathsCount} possible paths for what happens next.${si}${li}${filterInstructions}

WORD COUNT REQUIREMENT: ${typeInstruction}

Return a numbered list with NO extra commentary:
${Array.from({ length: pathsCount }, (_, i) => `${i + 1}. [path here]`).join('\n')}

Story:
${cnt.slice(-2000)}`,
         temperature: 0.7
      });

      let paths = response.trim().split('\n').filter(line => /^\d+\./.test(line));
      elements.pathsBox.innerHTML = '';

      paths.forEach(path => {
         let container      = document.createElement('div');
         container.className= 'path-item-container';

         let contentWrapper = document.createElement('div');
         contentWrapper.style.display = 'flex';
         contentWrapper.style.gap     = '5px';

         let textarea        = document.createElement('textarea');
         textarea.className  = 'path-textarea';
         textarea.value      = path;

         const autoResize = () => {
            textarea.style.height = 'auto';
            textarea.style.height = textarea.scrollHeight + 'px';
         };
         textarea.addEventListener('input', autoResize);

         if (hasArabic(path)) {
            textarea.style.fontFamily = "'Tajawal', Arial, sans-serif";
            textarea.style.direction  = 'rtl';
            textarea.style.textAlign  = 'right';
         }

         let btnContainer = document.createElement('div');
         btnContainer.style.display       = 'flex';
         btnContainer.style.flexDirection = 'column';
         btnContainer.style.gap           = '5px';

         // زر إرسال المسار إلى القصة | Send path to story button
         let sendBtn       = document.createElement('button');
         sendBtn.className = 'btn-small btn-success';
         sendBtn.innerHTML = '➤';
         sendBtn.title     = 'Send to story';
         sendBtn.onclick   = () => selectPath(textarea.value);

         // زر إعادة التعيين | Reset path button
         let resetBtn       = document.createElement('button');
         resetBtn.className = 'btn-small btn-secondary';
         resetBtn.innerHTML = '↺';
         resetBtn.title     = 'Reset';
         resetBtn.onclick   = () => {
            textarea.value = path;
            if (hasArabic(path)) {
               textarea.style.fontFamily = "'Tajawal', Arial, sans-serif";
               textarea.style.direction  = 'rtl';
               textarea.style.textAlign  = 'right';
            }
            autoResize();
         };

         btnContainer.appendChild(sendBtn);
         btnContainer.appendChild(resetBtn);
         contentWrapper.appendChild(textarea);
         contentWrapper.appendChild(btnContainer);
         container.appendChild(contentWrapper);
         elements.pathsBox.appendChild(container);
         setTimeout(autoResize, 0);
      });
   } catch (e) {
      console.error('خطأ في توليد المسارات:', e);
   } finally {
      elements.pathsProgress.style.display = 'none';
   }
}

// تطوير مسار مختار | Develop a selected path
async function selectPath(path) {
   showStatus("Developing selected path...");
   elements.storyProgress.style.display = 'flex';

   try {
      let startLength = elements.storyContent.value.length;
      await generateTextAbortable({
         instruction: `Continue this story following this path: ${path}\n\nMaintain the same realistic style with maximum detail and dialogue.\n\nCurrent story:\n${elements.storyContent.value}\n\nContinue:`,
         onChunk: (data) => {
            if (shouldAbortGeneration) return;
            elements.storyContent.value += data.textChunk;
            updateWordCount();
            applyArabicStyle(elements.storyContent);
            elements.storyContent.scrollTop = elements.storyContent.scrollHeight;
            checkChapterLimit();
         }
      });

      if (elements.storyContent.value.length > startLength) {
         elements.storyContent.value += '\n\n';
         elements.storyContent.scrollTop = elements.storyContent.scrollHeight;
      }

      showStatus("Path complete");
      await generatePaths();
   } catch (e) {
      showStatus("Error");
      console.error(e);
   } finally {
      elements.storyProgress.style.display = 'none';
   }
}


// ============================================================
// 18. لوحة التحليلات | Analytics Dashboard
// ============================================================

function refreshAnalytics() {
   saveCurrentChapter();
   let allContent  = '';
   let totalWords  = 0;
   let chapterCount= window.storyData.chapters.length;

   window.storyData.chapters.forEach(ch => {
      allContent += ch.content + '\n\n';
      totalWords += ch.content.trim() ? ch.content.trim().split(/\s+/).length : 0;
   });

   // الإحصاءات الأساسية | Basic statistics
   document.getElementById('statTotalWords').textContent = totalWords.toLocaleString();
   document.getElementById('statChapters').textContent   = chapterCount;
   document.getElementById('statAvgWords').textContent   = Math.round(totalWords / chapterCount).toLocaleString();
   document.getElementById('statReadTime').textContent   = Math.round(totalWords / 200) + ' min';

   let charMatches = allContent.match(/[A-Za-z\u0600-\u06FF\u4E00-\u9FFF\u3040-\u30FF\u0400-\u04FF]/g);
   document.getElementById('statCharCount').textContent  = charMatches ? charMatches.length.toLocaleString() : 0;

   // توزيع الحوار والسرد | Dialogue vs narrative
   let dialogueMatches = allContent.match(/"[^"]*"/g);
   let dialogueWords   = dialogueMatches ? dialogueMatches.join(' ').split(/\s+/).length : 0;
   let dialoguePct     = totalWords > 0 ? Math.round((dialogueWords / totalWords) * 100) : 0;
   document.getElementById('statDialogue').textContent   = dialoguePct + '%';
   document.getElementById('statNarrative').textContent  = (100 - dialoguePct) + '%';

   let sentences    = allContent.split(/[.!?]+/).filter(s => s.trim());
   let avgSentLen   = sentences.length > 0 ? Math.round(totalWords / sentences.length) : 0;
   document.getElementById('statSentenceLen').textContent= avgSentLen + ' words';

   let paragraphs   = allContent.split(/\n\n+/).filter(p => p.trim());
   let avgParaLen   = paragraphs.length > 0 ? Math.round(totalWords / paragraphs.length) : 0;
   document.getElementById('statParaLen').textContent    = avgParaLen + ' words';

   // مستوى القراءة | Readability
   let readingLevel = calculateReadingLevel(avgSentLen, totalWords, charMatches ? charMatches.length : 0);
   let storyLanguage= detectLanguage(allContent);
   if (storyLanguage !== 'English') {
      document.getElementById('statReadLevel').textContent  = 'N/A';
      document.getElementById('statComplexity').textContent = 'English only';
   } else {
      document.getElementById('statReadLevel').textContent  = readingLevel.level;
      document.getElementById('statComplexity').textContent = readingLevel.complexity;
   }

   // التنوع اللغوي | Vocabulary diversity
   let words       = allContent.toLowerCase().match(/\b\w+\b/g) || [];
   let uniqueWords = new Set(words);
   document.getElementById('statUniqueWords').textContent = uniqueWords.size.toLocaleString();
   let vocabDiv    = words.length > 0 ? Math.round((uniqueWords.size / words.length) * 100) : 0;
   document.getElementById('statVocabDiv').textContent    = vocabDiv + '%';

   analyzeCharacterScreenTime(allContent);
   analyzeEmotions(allContent);

   // بطاقة إحصاء أمان الأطفال | Child safety stats card
   if (window.storyData.contentFilter === 'child') {
      const safetyStats = getChildSafetyStats();
      const safetyCard  = document.createElement('div');
      safetyCard.className = 'analytics-card';
      safetyCard.style.borderLeft = '3px solid #10b981';
      safetyCard.innerHTML = `
         <h4><span class="ms">shield</span> حالة نظام الأمان</h4>
         <div class="stat-row"><span>حالة المحتوى:</span>      <strong style="color:#10b981">${safetyStats.status}</strong></div>
         <div class="stat-row"><span>تذكيرات التعلم:</span>    <strong>${safetyStats.attempts}</strong></div>
         <div class="stat-row"><span>كلمات الفلتر المحملة:</span><strong>${safetyStats.wordsLoaded}</strong></div>
         <div class="stat-row"><span>اللغة:</span>             <strong>${safetyStats.language}</strong></div>
         <div class="stat-row"><span>فحص الأنماط:</span>       <strong style="color:#8b5cf6">${dangerousPatterns ? Object.keys(dangerousPatterns).length : 0} نشط</strong></div>
         <div class="stat-row"><span>سياقات آمنة:</span>       <strong style="color:#10b981">${safeContexts.en ? Object.keys(safeContexts.en).length : 0} قائمة بيضاء</strong></div>
         <button onclick="clearChildSafetyCache()" class="btn-small" style="margin-top:8px">
            <span class="ms">refresh</span> تحديث فلتر الأمان
         </button>
      `;
      document.getElementById('analyticsTab').appendChild(safetyCard);
   }

   showStatus("Analytics updated");
}

// حساب مستوى القراءة (معادلة Flesch) | Calculate reading level (Flesch formula)
function calculateReadingLevel(avgSentenceLen, totalWords, totalChars) {
   let avgSyllables = totalChars > 0 ? totalChars / totalWords * 0.6 : 0;
   let score = 206.835 - 1.015 * avgSentenceLen - 84.6 * avgSyllables;
   let level, complexity;

   if (score >= 90)      { level = 'Grade 5';     complexity = 'Very Easy'; }
   else if (score >= 80) { level = 'Grade 6';     complexity = 'Easy'; }
   else if (score >= 70) { level = 'Grade 7-8';   complexity = 'Fairly Easy'; }
   else if (score >= 60) { level = 'Grade 9-10';  complexity = 'Standard'; }
   else if (score >= 50) { level = 'Grade 11-12'; complexity = 'Fairly Difficult'; }
   else if (score >= 30) { level = 'College';     complexity = 'Difficult'; }
   else                  { level = 'Graduate';    complexity = 'Very Difficult'; }

   return { level, complexity };
}

// تحليل وقت ظهور الشخصيات | Analyze character screen time
function analyzeCharacterScreenTime(content) {
   let characters = elements.charactersBox.value.split('\n')
      .filter(line => line.includes(':'))
      .map(line => line.split(':')[0].trim());

   if (characters.length === 0) {
      document.getElementById('characterScreenTime').innerHTML = '<p style="color:var(--txt3);font-style:italic;text-align:center;padding:10px">No characters defined</p>';
      return;
   }

   let screenTime = {};
   characters.forEach(char => {
      let regex   = new RegExp('\\b' + char + '\\b', 'gi');
      let matches = content.match(regex);
      screenTime[char] = matches ? matches.length : 0;
   });

   let sorted       = Object.entries(screenTime).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1]);
   let totalMentions= sorted.reduce((sum, [_, count]) => sum + count, 0);
   let html = '';

   sorted.slice(0, 5).forEach(([char, count]) => {
      let pct = totalMentions > 0 ? Math.round((count / totalMentions) * 100) : 0;
      html += `<div style="margin-bottom:6px">
         <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:2px">
            <span style="color:var(--txt1)">${char}</span>
            <span style="color:var(--txt2)">${pct}% (${count})</span>
         </div>
         <div style="background:var(--brd2);height:6px;border-radius:3px;overflow:hidden">
            <div style="background:var(--acc1);height:100%;width:${pct}%"></div>
         </div>
      </div>`;
   });

   document.getElementById('characterScreenTime').innerHTML = html || '<p style="color:var(--txt3);font-style:italic">No character mentions found</p>';
}

// تحليل المشاعر في النص | Analyze emotions in text
function analyzeEmotions(content) {
   const emotionKeywords = {
      'Joy':     ['happy', 'joy', 'delight', 'pleased', 'cheerful', 'smiled', 'laughed', 'excited'],
      'Sadness': ['sad', 'sorrow', 'grief', 'depressed', 'miserable', 'cried', 'tears', 'unhappy'],
      'Anger':   ['angry', 'furious', 'rage', 'mad', 'irritated', 'annoyed', 'frustrated'],
      'Fear':    ['afraid', 'scared', 'terrified', 'frightened', 'anxious', 'worried', 'nervous'],
      'Love':    ['love', 'adore', 'cherish', 'affection', 'romance', 'passion', 'tender']
   };

   let emotions      = {};
   let totalEmotions = 0;

   for (let emotion in emotionKeywords) {
      let count = 0;
      emotionKeywords[emotion].forEach(keyword => {
         let regex   = new RegExp('\\b' + keyword + '\\w*\\b', 'gi');
         let matches = content.match(regex);
         if (matches) count += matches.length;
      });
      emotions[emotion] = count;
      totalEmotions += count;
   }

   let sorted = Object.entries(emotions).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1]);
   let html   = '';

   sorted.forEach(([emotion, count]) => {
      if (count === 0) return;
      let pct   = totalEmotions > 0 ? Math.round((count / totalEmotions) * 100) : 0;
      let emoji = { 'Joy': '😊', 'Sadness': '😢', 'Anger': '😠', 'Fear': '😰', 'Love': '💕' }[emotion];
      html += `<div style="margin-bottom:6px">
         <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:2px">
            <span style="color:var(--txt1)">${emoji} ${emotion}</span>
            <span style="color:var(--txt2)">${pct}% (${count})</span>
         </div>
         <div style="background:var(--brd2);height:6px;border-radius:3px;overflow:hidden">
            <div style="background:#8b5cf6;height:100%;width:${pct}%"></div>
         </div>
      </div>`;
   });

   document.getElementById('emotionAnalysis').innerHTML = html || '<p style="color:var(--txt3);font-style:italic">No emotional words detected</p>';
}

// 19. دوال التصدير الأصلية | Original Export Functions

// تصدير Markdown | Export as Markdown
function exportMarkdown() {
   saveCurrentChapter();
   let title    = elements.storyTitle.value.trim() || "Story";
   let markdown = `# ${title}\n\n`;
   window.storyData.chapters.forEach((ch, idx) => {
      if (idx > 0) markdown += `\n\n---\n\n`;
      markdown += `## ${ch.name}\n\n`;
      markdown += ch.content;
   });
   if (!markdown.trim()) { showStatus("Nothing to export"); return; }
   let blob = new Blob([markdown], { type: "text/markdown;charset=utf-8" });
   let url  = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
   let a    = document.createElement("a");
   a.href   = url; a.download = `${title}.md`; a.click();
   URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
   showStatus("Exported to Markdown");
}

// ============================================================
// 20. تخزين واسترجاع القصص | Story Storage & Retrieval
// ============================================================

// حفظ القصة في kv | Save story to kv storage
async function saveStory() {
   saveCurrentChapter();
   let title   = elements.storyTitle.value.trim() || "Untitled Story";
   let storyId = title.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, '-') + '-' + Date.now();

   await kv.stories.set(storyId, {
      id:            storyId,
      title:         title,
      chapters:      window.storyData.chapters,
      currentChapter:window.storyData.currentChapter,
      settings:      window.storyData.settings,
      theme:         window.storyData.theme,
      contentFilter: window.storyData.contentFilter,
      wordCount: window.storyData.chapters.reduce((sum, ch) => {
         return sum + (ch.content.trim() ? ch.content.trim().split(/\s+/).length : 0);
      }, 0),
      lastEdited: new Date().toISOString()
   });

   await kv.storySettings.set("lastEdited", storyId);
   showStatus("Saved successfully");
}

// مسح القصة الحالية | Clear current story
function clearStory() {
   if (elements.storyContent.value && !confirm("Start new story? Unsaved work will be lost.")) return;
   elements.storyTitle.value  = "";
   window.storyData.chapters  = [{ id: 1, name: 'Chapter 1', content: '', summary: '', readonly: false }];
   window.storyData.currentChapter = 1;
   elements.storyContent.value    = "";
   elements.storyContent.readOnly = false;
   elements.charactersBox.value   = "";
   elements.locationsBox.value    = "";
   elements.itemsBox.value        = "";
   elements.eventsBox.value       = "";
   elements.themesBox.value       = "";
   elements.conflictsBox.value    = "";
   elements.pathsBox.innerHTML    = "";
   updateWordCount();
   renderChapterTabs();
}

// تحميل قائمة القصص المحفوظة | Load saved stories list
async function loadStoryList() {
   let keys      = await kv.stories.keys();
   let savedList = document.getElementById('savedList');
   savedList.innerHTML = "";

   if (keys.length === 0) {
      savedList.innerHTML = "<p class='empty'>No saved stories</p>";
      return;
   }

   let controlsHtml = `
      <div style="display:flex;gap:6px;margin-bottom:12px;flex-wrap:wrap">
         <button onclick="toggleSelectAll()" class="btn-small btn-secondary" id="selectAllBtn">
            <span class="ms">check</span> Select All
         </button>
         <button onclick="deleteSelectedStories()" class="btn-small btn-danger" id="deleteSelectedBtn" style="display:none">
            <span class="ms">delete</span> Delete Selected (<span id="selectedCount">0</span>)
         </button>
      </div>
   `;
   savedList.innerHTML = controlsHtml;

   let stories = [];
   for (let key of keys) { stories.push(await kv.stories.get(key)); }
   stories.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.lastEdited) - new Date(a.lastEdited));

   for (let story of stories) {
      let item       = document.createElement("div");
      item.className = "saved-item";
      let titleStyle = hasArabic(story.title) ? "font-family:'Tajawal',Arial,sans-serif;direction:rtl" : "";
      let totalWords = story.wordCount || 0;
      let chapCount  = story.chapters ? story.chapters.length : 1;

      item.innerHTML = `
         <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;flex:1">
            <input type="checkbox" class="story-checkbox" data-story-id="${story.id}"
                   onchange="updateDeleteButton()"
                   style="width:18px;height:18px;cursor:pointer">
            <div style="${titleStyle};flex:1">
               <strong>${story.title}</strong><br>
               <small>${totalWords} words · ${chapCount} ch</small>
            </div>
         </div>
         <div style="display:flex;gap:4px">
            <button onclick="loadStory('${story.id}')" class="btn-small"><span class="ms">folder</span></button>
            <button onclick="deleteSingleStory('${story.id}')" class="btn-small btn-danger"><span class="ms">delete</span></button>
         </div>
      `;
      savedList.appendChild(item);
   }
}

// تحميل قصة محددة | Load a specific story
async function loadStory(id) {
   let story = await kv.stories.get(id);
   if (!story) return;

   elements.storyTitle.value = story.title;
   if (story.settings)      { window.storyData.settings = story.settings; }
   if (story.theme)         { window.storyData.theme = story.theme; applyTheme(); }
   if (story.contentFilter) { window.storyData.contentFilter = story.contentFilter; updateFilterBadge(); }

   if (story.chapters) {
      window.storyData.chapters       = story.chapters;
      window.storyData.currentChapter = story.currentChapter || 1;
      let chapter = window.storyData.chapters.find(ch => ch.id === window.storyData.currentChapter);
      if (chapter) {
         elements.storyContent.value    = chapter.content;
         elements.storyContent.readOnly = chapter.readonly || false;
      }
      renderChapterTabs();
   } else {
      elements.storyContent.value    = story.content || '';
      elements.storyContent.readOnly = false;
      window.storyData.chapters       = [{ id: 1, name: 'Chapter 1', content: story.content || '', summary: '', readonly: false }];
      window.storyData.currentChapter = 1;
      renderChapterTabs();
   }

   updateWordCount();
   applyArabicStyle(elements.storyTitle);
   applyArabicStyle(elements.storyContent);
   await kv.storySettings.set("lastEdited", id);
   showStatus("Loaded");
   switchTab('components');
}


// ============================================================
// 21. الحذف الجماعي والفردي للقصص | Bulk & Single Story Deletion
// ============================================================

function toggleSelectAll() {
   const checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('.story-checkbox');
   const allChecked = Array.from(checkboxes).every(cb => cb.checked);
   checkboxes.forEach(cb => { cb.checked = !allChecked; });
   updateDeleteButton();
}

function updateDeleteButton() {
   const checkboxes  = document.querySelectorAll('.story-checkbox:checked');
   const deleteBtn   = document.getElementById('deleteSelectedBtn');
   const countSpan   = document.getElementById('selectedCount');
   const selectAllBtn= document.getElementById('selectAllBtn');

   if (checkboxes.length > 0) {
      deleteBtn.style.display = 'inline-flex';
      countSpan.textContent   = checkboxes.length;
      selectAllBtn.innerHTML  = '<span class="ms">close</span> Deselect All';
   } else {
      deleteBtn.style.display = 'none';
      selectAllBtn.innerHTML  = '<span class="ms">check</span> Select All';
   }
}

async function deleteSelectedStories() {
   const checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('.story-checkbox:checked');
   const count = checkboxes.length;
   if (count === 0) return;
   if (!confirm(`Delete ${count} selected ${count === 1 ? 'story' : 'stories'}? This cannot be undone.`)) return;

   let deleted = 0;
   for (let checkbox of checkboxes) {
      const storyId = checkbox.getAttribute('data-story-id');
      try { await kv.stories.delete(storyId); deleted++; }
      catch (e) { console.error('فشل حذف القصة:', storyId, e); }
   }

   showStatus(`Deleted ${deleted} ${deleted === 1 ? 'story' : 'stories'}`);
   loadStoryList();
}

async function deleteSingleStory(id) {
   if (!confirm("Delete this story?")) return;
   let story = await kv.stories.get(id);
   if (story) { await kv.stories.delete(id); loadStoryList(); showStatus("Deleted"); }
}

// ============================================================
// 22. نظام النسخ الاحتياطي | Backup System
// ============================================================

// بدء النسخ الاحتياطي التلقائي كل 5 دقائق | Start auto backup every 5 minutes
async function startAutoBackup() {
   if (!kv || typeof kv.backups === 'undefined') {
      console.warn('النسخ الاحتياطي التلقائي معطل: kv.backups غير متاح');
      return;
   }
   if (autoBackupInterval) clearInterval(autoBackupInterval);
   autoBackupInterval = setInterval(async () => { await createBackup(true); }, 5 * 60 * 1000);
}

// إنشاء نسخة احتياطية (تلقائية أو يدوية) | Create backup (auto or manual)
async function createBackup(auto = false) {
   if (!kv || typeof kv.backups === 'undefined') {
      if (!auto) showStatus('Backup unavailable');
      return;
   }
   saveCurrentChapter();
   let backupId   = 'backup-' + Date.now();
   let backupData = {
      id:            backupId,
      title:         elements.storyTitle.value.trim() || "Untitled Story",
      chapters:      JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(window.storyData.chapters)),
      currentChapter:window.storyData.currentChapter,
      settings:      JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(window.storyData.settings)),
      timestamp:     new Date().toISOString(),
      auto:          auto
   };
   await kv.backups.set(backupId, backupData);

   // الاحتفاظ بآخر 10 نسخ فقط | Keep only last 10 backups
   let keys = await kv.backups.keys();
   if (keys.length > 10) {
      keys.sort();
      for (let i = 0; i < keys.length - 10; i++) { await kv.backups.delete(keys[i]); }
   }

   if (!auto) showStatus("Backup created");
   updateBackupInfo();
}

// تحديث معلومات النسخ الاحتياطي | Update backup info display
async function updateBackupInfo() {
   if (!kv || typeof kv.backups === 'undefined') {
      console.warn('kv.backups غير متاح');
      document.getElementById('backupCount').textContent    = '0';
      document.getElementById('lastBackupTime').textContent = 'Unavailable';
      return;
   }
   try {
      let keys = await kv.backups.keys();
      document.getElementById('backupCount').textContent = keys.length;
      if (keys.length > 0) {
         let lastBackup = await kv.backups.get(keys[keys.length - 1]);
         document.getElementById('lastBackupTime').textContent = new Date(lastBackup.timestamp).toLocaleString();
      } else {
         document.getElementById('lastBackupTime').textContent = 'Never';
      }
   } catch (e) {
      console.error('خطأ في الوصول إلى النسخ الاحتياطية:', e);
      document.getElementById('backupCount').textContent    = '0';
      document.getElementById('lastBackupTime').textContent = 'Error';
   }

   const sidebarTime  = document.getElementById('lastBackupTimeSidebar');
   const sidebarCount = document.getElementById('backupCountSidebar');
   if (sidebarTime)  sidebarTime.textContent  = document.getElementById('lastBackupTime').textContent;
   if (sidebarCount) sidebarCount.textContent = document.getElementById('backupCount').textContent;
}

// عرض نافذة النسخ الاحتياطية | Show backups modal
async function showBackups() {
   if (!kv || typeof kv.backups === 'undefined') { alert('Backup system unavailable'); return; }
   document.getElementById('backupsModal').style.display = 'flex';

   let keys = await kv.backups.keys();
   keys.sort().reverse();
   let html = '';

   for (let key of keys) {
      let backup    = await kv.backups.get(key);
      let date      = new Date(backup.timestamp);
      let wordCount = backup.chapters.reduce((sum, ch) => sum + (ch.content.trim().split(/\s+/).length), 0);
      html += `<div class="backup-item">
         <div>
            <strong style="color:var(--txt1)">${backup.title}</strong><br>
            <small style="color:var(--txt2)">
               ${date.toLocaleString()} · ${wordCount} words · ${backup.chapters.length} ch
               ${backup.auto ? '(auto)' : '(manual)'}
            </small>
         </div>
         <div style="display:flex;gap:5px">
            <button onclick="restoreBackup('${key}')" class="btn-small btn-success"><span class="ms">check</span> Restore</button>
            <button onclick="deleteBackup('${key}')" class="btn-small btn-danger"><span class="ms">delete</span> حذف</button>
         </div>
      </div>`;
   }

   if (keys.length === 0) {
      html = '<p style="color:var(--txt3);font-style:italic;text-align:center;padding:20px">لا توجد نسخ احتياطية متاحة</p>';
   }

   document.getElementById('backupsList').innerHTML = html;
}

function closeBackups() {
   document.getElementById('backupsModal').style.display = 'none';
}

// استعادة نسخة احتياطية | Restore a backup
async function restoreBackup(backupId) {
   if (!confirm("Restore this backup? Current work will be replaced.")) return;
   let backup = await kv.backups.get(backupId);
   if (!backup) return;

   elements.storyTitle.value          = backup.title;
   window.storyData.chapters          = backup.chapters;
   window.storyData.currentChapter    = backup.currentChapter;
   window.storyData.settings          = backup.settings;

   let chapter = window.storyData.chapters.find(ch => ch.id === window.storyData.currentChapter);
   if (chapter) {
      elements.storyContent.value    = chapter.content;
      elements.storyContent.readOnly = chapter.readonly || false;
   }

   renderChapterTabs();
   updateWordCount();
   applyArabicStyle(elements.storyTitle);
   applyArabicStyle(elements.storyContent);
   closeBackups();
   showStatus("Backup restored");
}

async function deleteBackup(backupId) {
   if (!confirm("Delete this backup?")) return;
   await kv.backups.delete(backupId);
   showBackups();
   updateBackupInfo();
}

// ============================================================
// 22.5 دوال مساعدة مشتركة | Shared Helper Functions
// ============================================================

// جمع محتوى جميع الفصول — Collect all chapters content
function getAllChaptersContent() {
   return window.storyData.chapters
      .filter(ch => ch.content.trim())
      .map(ch => `\n\n=== ${ch.name} ===\n${ch.content}`)
      .join('');
}

// إدراج نص في محرر القصة — Insert text into story editor
function insertToStory(text, prefix = '', suffix = '', statusMsg = 'Text inserted into story') {
   elements.storyContent.value += `\n\n${prefix}${text}${suffix}\n\n`;
   applyArabicStyle(elements.storyContent);
   updateWordCount();
   showStatus(statusMsg);
}

// 23. أدوات الذكاء الاصطناعي الجانبية | Sidebar AI Tools
// ============================================================
// — مولد الأسماء | Name Generator —
function openNameGenerator() { switchTab('nameGen'); }

// — قوالب القصة | Story Templates —
function openTemplates() { switchTab('templates'); }

// — دالة مساعدة لاستخراج أسماء الشخصيات من صندوق المكونات | Helper: get character names from components box —
function getCharacterNames() {
   return elements.charactersBox.value
      .split('\n')
      .filter(line => line.includes(':'))
      .map(line => line.split(':')[0].trim())
      .filter(name => name.length > 0);
}

// — تعبئة قائمة منسدلة بالشخصيات | Populate a select element with character names —
function populateCharacterDropdown(selectId, addEmpty = true) {
   const select = document.getElementById(selectId);
   if (!select) return;
   const names = getCharacterNames();
   select.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- Select from story --</option>';
   names.forEach(name => {
      const opt = document.createElement('option');
      opt.value = opt.textContent = name;
      select.appendChild(opt);
   });
}

// — عند اختيار شخصية من الـ Dialogue dropdown | On Dialogue dropdown selection —
function onDialogueCharSelect(selectEl, inputId) {
   const input = document.getElementById(inputId);
   if (input && selectEl.value) {
      input.value = selectEl.value;
   }
}

// — عند اختيار شخصية من الـ POV dropdown | On POV dropdown selection —
function onPOVCharSelect(selectEl) {
   onDialogueCharSelect(selectEl, 'povCharNameSidebar');
}

// — عند اختيار شخصية من الـ Flashback dropdown | On Flashback dropdown selection —
function onFlashbackCharSelect(selectEl) {
   const input = document.getElementById('flashbackCharsSidebar');
   if (input && selectEl.value) {
      // إذا كان الحقل فارغاً أضف الاسم، وإلا أضفه بفاصلة | Append with comma if not empty
      if (input.value.trim()) {
         input.value = input.value.trim() + ', ' + selectEl.value;
      } else {
         input.value = selectEl.value;
      }
      // إعادة القائمة للوضع الافتراضي | Reset dropdown
      selectEl.value = '';
   }
}

// — تعبئة حقلي الشخصية من المكونات | Populate dialogue character fields —
function populateDialogueCharacters() {
   // تعبئة القوائم المنسدلة | Fill dropdowns
   populateCharacterDropdown('dialogueChar1Select');
   populateCharacterDropdown('dialogueChar2Select');

   // تعبئة الحقول النصية إذا كانت فارغة | Pre-fill text inputs if empty
   const char1Input = document.getElementById('dialogueChar1Sidebar');
   const char2Input = document.getElementById('dialogueChar2Sidebar');
   if (!char1Input || !char2Input) return;
   const names = getCharacterNames();
   if (names.length >= 1 && !char1Input.value) char1Input.value = names[0];
   if (names.length >= 2 && !char2Input.value) char2Input.value = names[1];
}

// — توليد الحوار الجانبي | Generate sidebar dialogue —
async function generateDialogueSidebar() {
   const char1   = document.getElementById('dialogueChar1Sidebar').value.trim();
   const char2   = document.getElementById('dialogueChar2Sidebar').value.trim();
   const context = document.getElementById('dialogueContextSidebar').value.trim();

   if (!char1 || !char2) { alert("Please enter both character names."); return; }

   const progressIndicator = document.getElementById('dialogueSidebarProgress');
   const generatedDialogue = document.getElementById('generatedDialogueSidebar');
   progressIndicator.style.display = 'flex';
   generatedDialogue.innerHTML = '';

   try {
      let languageInstruction = getLanguageInstruction();
      let filterInstructions  = getFilterInstructions();
      let result = await generateTextAbortable({
         instruction: `Write a realistic dialogue between ${char1} and ${char2}. ${context ? 'Context: ' + context : ''}
      
Make the dialogue:
- Natural and believable
- Reflect each character's personality
- Include nonverbal cues and actions
- Show conflict or cooperation as appropriate
- Advance the scene or reveal character${languageInstruction}${filterInstructions}

Format as:
${char1}: "Dialogue here"
[Action or description]
${char2}: "Response here"
...`,
         temperature: 0.8
      });
      generatedDialogue.innerHTML     = result;
      generatedDialogue.style.color   = 'var(--txt1)';
   } catch (e) {
      generatedDialogue.innerHTML = `<p style="color:var(--dng1)">خطأ: ${e.message}</p>`;
   } finally {
      progressIndicator.style.display = 'none';
   }
}

// إدراج الحوار في القصة | Insert dialogue into story
function insertDialogueSidebar() {
   const dialogueContent = document.getElementById('generatedDialogueSidebar').innerText;
   if (dialogueContent && !dialogueContent.includes("Generating") && !dialogueContent.includes("Deleted")) {
      insertToStory(dialogueContent, '', '', 'Dialogue inserted into story');
      document.getElementById('dialogueContextSidebar').value = '';
      document.getElementById('generatedDialogueSidebar').innerHTML = '<p style="color:var(--txt3);text-align:center;padding:40px 10px;font-style:italic;margin:0">Click "Generate" to create dialogue</p>';
   } else {
      alert("Generate a dialogue first.");
   }
}

function openInteractiveDialogue()    { switchTab('dialogue'); populateDialogueCharacters(); }
function openConsistencyChecker()     { switchTab('consistency'); }
function openCharacterVoiceAnalyzer() { switchTab('voice'); populateVoiceCharacters(); }
function openAIWritingCoach()         { switchTab('coach'); }

function openFlashbackManager()       { switchTab('flashback'); }
