// 24. فحص الاتساق | Consistency Checker
// ============================================================

async function runConsistencyCheckSidebar() {
   const allContent = getAllChaptersContent();

   if (allContent.trim().length < 100) { alert("Not enough content to analyze."); return; }

   const progressIndicator = document.getElementById('consistencySidebarProgress2');
   const resultsDiv        = document.getElementById('consistencySidebarResults3');
   resultsDiv.style.display = 'none';
   progressIndicator.style.display = 'flex';

   try {
      let languageInstruction = getLanguageInstruction(allContent);
      let filterInstructions  = getFilterInstructions();
      let result = await generateTextAbortable({
         instruction: `Analyze this story for inconsistencies, plot holes, and continuity errors. Look for:
1. Timeline contradictions
2. Character description changes
3. Location or setting inconsistencies
4. Plot logic gaps
5. Unresolved story threads
6. Contradictory character actions or motivations

For each issue found, provide:
- The type of inconsistency
- Where it occurs (chapter or approximate location)
- The specific contradiction
- Suggested fix${languageInstruction}${filterInstructions}

Story: ${allContent.slice(-5000)}`,
         temperature: 0.3
      });
      resultsDiv.innerHTML    = result;
      resultsDiv.style.display= 'block';
   } catch (e) {
      resultsDiv.innerHTML    = `<p style="color:var(--dng1)">خطأ: ${e.message}</p>`;
      resultsDiv.style.display= 'block';
   } finally {
      progressIndicator.style.display = 'none';
   }
}

// ============================================================
// 25. المخطط الزمني | Timeline Visualizer
// ============================================================

function openTimeline() {
   document.getElementById('timelineModal').style.display = 'flex';
   if (timelineData.events.length === 0) {
      setTimeout(() => generateTimeline(), 500);
   }
}

function closeTimeline() {
   document.getElementById('timelineModal').style.display = 'none';
}

// توليد المخطط الزمني | Generate timeline from story
async function generateTimeline() {
   let allContent = '';
   let chapterInfo= [];

   window.storyData.chapters.forEach((ch) => {
      if (ch.content.trim()) {
         allContent += `\n\n=== ${ch.name} ===\n${ch.content}`;
         chapterInfo.push({ id: ch.id, name: ch.name, wordCount: ch.content.trim().split(/\s+/).length });
      }
   });

   if (allContent.trim().length < 100) {
      alert("Not enough content for a timeline. Write at least 100 words first.");
      return;
   }

   document.getElementById('timelineProgress').style.display = 'flex';
   document.getElementById('timelineCanvas').innerHTML = '<p style="color:var(--txt3);text-align:center;padding:100px 20px">Analyzing...</p>';

   try {
      let languageInstruction = getLanguageInstruction(allContent);
      let filterInstructions  = getFilterInstructions();

      let result = await generateTextAbortable({
         instruction: `Analyze this story and extract ALL significant time-based events. Create a detailed timeline.

For EACH event, provide:
- Event: [brief description of what happened]
- Time: [when it happened - be specific: "Day 1 morning", "3 days later", "Week 2", etc.]
- Chapter: [chapter number where it occurred]
- Characters: [who was involved]
- Conflict Level: [low/medium/high - how intense was this moment]
- Type: [plot/character/relationship/revelation/action]

Format EXACTLY as:
---
Event: [description]
Time: [specific time]
Chapter: ${chapterInfo[0].name}
Characters: [names]
Conflict: [low/medium/high]
Type: [type]
---

Extract MINIMUM 10 events, MAXIMUM 30 events. Focus on:
- Major plot developments
- Character decisions
- Relationship changes
- Conflicts and resolutions
- Revelations and discoveries
- Time markers (morning, evening, days/weeks later)${languageInstruction}${filterInstructions}

Story:
${allContent.slice(-6000)}

Generate timeline events:`,
         temperature: 0.4
      });

      timelineData.events = parseTimelineEvents(result, chapterInfo);
      if (timelineData.events.length === 0) throw new Error("No events could be parsed from the AI response");

      renderTimeline();
      updateTimelineStats();
      showStatus(`Timeline created: ${timelineData.events.length} events`);
   } catch (error) {
      console.error('خطأ في إنشاء المخطط الزمني:', error);
      document.getElementById('timelineCanvas').innerHTML = `
         <p style="color:var(--dng1);text-align:center;padding:100px 20px">
            Error creating timeline. Please try again.<br>
            <small>${error.message}</small>
         </p>`;
      showStatus("Timeline creation error");
   } finally {
      document.getElementById('timelineProgress').style.display = 'none';
   }
}

// تحليل استجابة الـ AI لاستخراج الأحداث | Parse AI response into events array
function parseTimelineEvents(text, chapterInfo) {
   let events = [];
   let blocks  = text.split('---').filter(b => b.trim());

   blocks.forEach((block, idx) => {
      let lines = block.trim().split('\n');
      let event = { id: 'event-' + idx, event: '', time: '', chapter: '', chapterNum: 0, characters: '', conflict: 'low', type: 'plot', position: 0 };

      lines.forEach(line => {
         let match = line.match(/^(Event|Time|Chapter|Characters|Conflict|Type):\s*(.+)/i);
         if (match) {
            let key   = match[1].toLowerCase();
            let value = match[2].trim();
            if (key === 'event')      event.event = value;
            else if (key === 'time')  event.time  = value;
            else if (key === 'chapter') {
               event.chapter = value;
               let chMatch   = value.match(/(?:chapter|ch\.?)\s*(\d+)/i) || value.match(/^(\d+)/);
               if (chMatch)  event.chapterNum = parseInt(chMatch[1] || chMatch[0]);
            }
            else if (key === 'characters') event.characters = value;
            else if (key === 'conflict')   event.conflict   = value.toLowerCase();
            else if (key === 'type')       event.type       = value.toLowerCase();
         }
      });

      if (event.event && event.time) {
         event.position = calculateTimePosition(event.time, event.chapterNum);
         events.push(event);
      }
   });

   return events;
}

// حساب موضع الحدث على المحور الزمني | Calculate event position on timeline axis
function calculateTimePosition(timeStr, chapterNum) {
   timeStr = timeStr.toLowerCase();
   let dayMatch   = timeStr.match(/day\s*(\d+)/);
   let weekMatch  = timeStr.match(/week\s*(\d+)/);
   let monthMatch = timeStr.match(/month\s*(\d+)/);

   if (monthMatch) return Math.min(100, parseInt(monthMatch[1]) * 30);
   if (weekMatch)  return Math.min(100, parseInt(weekMatch[1]) * 7);
   if (dayMatch)   return Math.min(100, parseInt(dayMatch[1]));

   if (timeStr.includes('morning') || timeStr.includes('dawn'))     return chapterNum * 20;
   if (timeStr.includes('afternoon') || timeStr.includes('noon'))   return chapterNum * 20 + 5;
   if (timeStr.includes('evening') || timeStr.includes('dusk'))     return chapterNum * 20 + 10;
   if (timeStr.includes('night') || timeStr.includes('midnight'))   return chapterNum * 20 + 15;

   return chapterNum * 20;
}

// رسم المخطط الزمني المرئي | Render visual timeline
function renderTimeline() {
   if (timelineData.events.length === 0) {
      document.getElementById('timelineCanvas').innerHTML = '<p style="color:var(--txt3);text-align:center;padding:100px 20px">No events to display</p>';
      return;
   }

   let canvas = document.getElementById('timelineCanvas');
   let sorted = [...timelineData.events].sort((a, b) => {
      return timelineData.sortOrder === 'chronological' ? a.position - b.position : a.chapterNum - b.chapterNum;
   });

   let html = '<div class="story-arc-container">';

   // منحنى القصة الدرامي | Dramatic story arc SVG
   html += `<svg class="story-arc-svg" viewBox="0 0 1000 400" preserveAspectRatio="none">
      <defs>
         <linearGradient id="arcGradient" x1="0%" y1="0%" x2="100%" y2="0%">
            <stop offset="0%"   style="stop-color:var(--arc-expo);stop-opacity:1" />
            <stop offset="25%"  style="stop-color:var(--arc-rising);stop-opacity:1" />
            <stop offset="50%"  style="stop-color:var(--dng1);stop-opacity:1" />
            <stop offset="75%"  style="stop-color:var(--wrn);stop-opacity:1" />
            <stop offset="100%" style="stop-color:var(--suc1);stop-opacity:1" />
         </linearGradient>
      </defs>
      <path class="arc-path" d="${generateArcPath()}" />
   </svg>`;

   // تسميات مراحل القصة | Story arc section labels
   const sections = [
      { name: 'Exposition',    class: 'arc-exposition', pos: 10 },
      { name: 'Rising Action', class: 'arc-rising',     pos: 30 },
      { name: 'Climax',        class: 'arc-climax',     pos: 50 },
      { name: 'Falling Action',class: 'arc-falling',    pos: 70 },
      { name: 'Resolution',    class: 'arc-resolution', pos: 90 }
   ];
   sections.forEach(section => {
      let point = getPointOnArc(section.pos);
      html += `<div class="arc-section-label ${section.class}" style="left:${point.x}%;top:${point.y - 8}%">${section.name}</div>`;
   });

   // علامات الفصول | Chapter markers
   let chapters = [...new Set(sorted.map(e => e.chapterNum))].sort((a, b) => a - b);
   chapters.forEach((chNum, idx) => {
      let progress = ((idx + 0.5) / chapters.length) * 100;
      let point    = getPointOnArc(progress);
      html += `<div class="timeline-chapter-marker" style="left:${point.x}%;top:${point.y}%">
         <div class="timeline-chapter-badge">فصل ${chNum}</div>
      </div>`;
   });

   // أحداث المخطط | Timeline events
   sorted.forEach((event, idx) => {
      let progress      = ((idx + 0.5) / sorted.length) * 100;
      let point         = getPointOnArc(progress);
      let conflictClass = event.conflict === 'high' ? 'conflict-high' : event.conflict === 'medium' ? 'conflict-medium' : 'conflict-low';
      let icon          = getEventIcon(event.type);
      html += `<div class="timeline-event ${conflictClass}" style="left:${point.x}%;top:${point.y}%" onclick="showEventDetails('${event.id}')">
         <div class="timeline-marker">${icon}</div>
         <div class="timeline-label">
            <strong>${event.event}</strong>
            <small>⏰ ${event.time}</small>
            <small>📖 ${event.chapter}</small>
            ${event.characters ? '<small>👥 ' + event.characters + '</small>' : ''}
         </div>
      </div>`;
   });

   html += '</div>';
   canvas.innerHTML = html;
   renderListView();
}

// مسار منحنى القصة الدرامي | Dramatic arc SVG path
function generateArcPath() {
   return 'M 0 350 Q 125 300, 250 250 Q 375 150, 500 50 Q 625 150, 750 250 Q 875 300, 1000 350';
}

// حساب نقطة على المنحنى | Calculate point on arc curve
function getPointOnArc(progress) {
   let x = progress;
   let y;
   if (progress < 50) {
      y = 87.5 - (Math.pow(progress / 50, 1.5) * 75);
   } else {
      y = 87.5 - (Math.pow((100 - progress) / 50, 1.2) * 75);
   }
   return { x, y };
}

// أيقونة نوع الحدث | Get event type icon
function getEventIcon(type) {
   const icons = { 'plot': '📖', 'character': '👤', 'relationship': '💕', 'revelation': '💡', 'action': '⚔️', 'conflict': '⚡' };
   return icons[type] || '📍';
}

// رسم قائمة الأحداث | Render timeline list view
function renderListView() {
   let sorted = [...timelineData.events].sort((a, b) => a.position - b.position);
   let html   = '';
   sorted.forEach(event => {
      let conflictColor = event.conflict === 'high' ? 'var(--dng1)' : event.conflict === 'medium' ? 'var(--wrn)' : 'var(--acc1)';
      html += `<div class="timeline-list-item" style="border-left-color:${conflictColor}">
         <div class="timeline-list-time">${event.time}</div>
         <div class="timeline-list-content">
            <div class="timeline-list-event">${getEventIcon(event.type)} ${event.event}</div>
            <div class="timeline-list-details">
               ${event.characters ? '👥 ' + event.characters + '<br>' : ''}
               🔥 الصراع: ${event.conflict}
            </div>
            <span class="timeline-list-chapter">${event.chapter}</span>
         </div>
      </div>`;
   });
   document.getElementById('timelineList').innerHTML = html || '<p style="color:var(--txt3);text-align:center;padding:50px">No events</p>';
}

// تحديث إحصاءات المخطط الزمني | Update timeline statistics
function updateTimelineStats() {
   let total      = timelineData.events.length;
   let byChapter  = {};
   let byType     = {};
   let byConflict = { low: 0, medium: 0, high: 0 };

   timelineData.events.forEach(e => {
      byChapter[e.chapter] = (byChapter[e.chapter] || 0) + 1;
      byType[e.type]       = (byType[e.type] || 0) + 1;
      byConflict[e.conflict] = (byConflict[e.conflict] || 0) + 1;
   });

   let html = `
      <div class="timeline-stat-card">
         <h4><span class="ms">bar_chart</span> Overview</h4>
         <div class="timeline-stat-row"><span>Total Events:</span>    <strong>${total}</strong></div>
         <div class="timeline-stat-row"><span>Chapters Covered:</span>    <strong>${Object.keys(byChapter).length}</strong></div>
         <div class="timeline-stat-row"><span>Avg Events/Chapter:</span><strong>${Math.round(total / Object.keys(byChapter).length)}</strong></div>
      </div>
      <div class="timeline-stat-card">
         <h4>🔥 Conflict Distribution</h4>
         <div class="timeline-stat-row"><span>High Conflict:</span>   <strong style="color:var(--dng1)">${byConflict.high}   (${Math.round(byConflict.high / total * 100)}%)</strong></div>
         <div class="timeline-stat-row"><span>Medium Conflict:</span> <strong style="color:var(--wrn)">${byConflict.medium} (${Math.round(byConflict.medium / total * 100)}%)</strong></div>
         <div class="timeline-stat-row"><span>Low Conflict:</span><strong>${byConflict.low}   (${Math.round(byConflict.low / total * 100)}%)</strong></div>
      </div>
      <div class="timeline-stat-card">
         <h4><span class="ms">content_copy</span> Event Types</h4>`;

   Object.entries(byType).forEach(([type, count]) => {
      html += `<div class="timeline-stat-row"><span>${getEventIcon(type)} ${type}:</span> <strong>${count} (${Math.round(count / total * 100)}%)</strong></div>`;
   });
   html += '</div>';
   document.getElementById('timelineStats').innerHTML = html;
}

// تبديل عرض المخطط الزمني | Switch timeline view
function switchTimelineView(view) {
   timelineData.currentView = view;
   document.querySelectorAll('.timeline-view-tab').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active'));
   document.querySelectorAll('.timeline-view').forEach(v => v.style.display = 'none');

   if (view === 'visual') {
      document.getElementById('visualViewTab').classList.add('active');
      document.getElementById('visualTimelineView').style.display = 'block';
   } else if (view === 'list') {
      document.getElementById('listViewTab').classList.add('active');
      document.getElementById('listTimelineView').style.display = 'block';
   } else if (view === 'stats') {
      document.getElementById('statsViewTab').classList.add('active');
      document.getElementById('statsTimelineView').style.display = 'block';
   }
}

function sortTimelineBy(order) {
   timelineData.sortOrder = order;
   renderTimeline();
   showStatus(`Timeline sorted by ${order === 'chronological' ? 'chronological order' : 'chapter'}`);
}

// عرض تفاصيل حدث في popup | Show event details popup
function showEventDetails(eventId) {
   let event = timelineData.events.find(e => e.id === eventId);
   if (!event) return;
   alert(`📅 ${event.event}\n\n⏰ Time: ${event.time}\n📖 Chapter: ${event.chapter}\n👥 Characters: ${event.characters}\n🔥 Conflict: ${event.conflict}\n📋 Type: ${event.type}`);
}

// تصدير المخطط الزمني كنص | Export timeline as text
function exportTimeline() {
   if (timelineData.events.length === 0) { alert("Generate the timeline first"); return; }
   let title   = elements.storyTitle.value.trim() || "Story";
   let content = `${title} - Timeline Export\n${'='.repeat(50)}\n\n`;
   let sorted  = [...timelineData.events].sort((a, b) => a.position - b.position);

   sorted.forEach((event, idx) => {
      content += `${idx + 1}. ${event.event}\n`;
      content += `   Time: ${event.time}\n`;
      content += `   Chapter: ${event.chapter}\n`;
      content += `   Characters: ${event.characters}\n`;
      content += `   Conflict Level: ${event.conflict}\n`;
      content += `   Type: ${event.type}\n\n`;
   });

   let blob = new Blob([content], { type: "text/plain;charset=utf-8" });
   let url  = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
   let a    = document.createElement("a");
   a.href   = url; a.download = `${title}-timeline.txt`; a.click();
   URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
   showStatus("Timeline exported");
}

// 26. دوال واجهة المستخدم المساعدة | UI Helper Functions
// ============================================================

// تحديث عداد الكلمات | Update word count display
function updateWordCount() {
   let count = elements.storyContent.value.trim() ? elements.storyContent.value.trim().split(/\s+/).length : 0;
   elements.wordCount.textContent = `${count} words`;
}

// عرض رسالة حالة مؤقتة | Show temporary status message
function showStatus(msg) {
   elements.status.textContent = msg;
   if (hasArabic(msg)) {
      elements.status.style.fontFamily = "'Tajawal',Arial,sans-serif";
      elements.status.style.direction  = 'rtl';
   }
   setTimeout(() => { elements.status.textContent = ""; }, 3000);
}

// التبديل بين تبويبات الشريط الجانبي | Switch sidebar tabs
function switchTab(name) {
  // إزالة التظليل عن كل الأزرار والمحتويات — Remove active from all tabs and contents
  document.querySelectorAll('.vtab').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active'));
  document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('active'));

  // تظليل الزر الصحيح بواسطة data-tab — Highlight correct button via data-tab
  const tabButton = document.querySelector(`.vtab[data-tab="${name}"]`);
  if (tabButton) tabButton.classList.add('active');

  // إظهار المحتوى الصحيح — Show correct content
  const tabContent = document.getElementById(name + 'Tab');
  if (tabContent) tabContent.classList.add('active');

  // تحميل البيانات الخاصة بكل تبويب — Load tab-specific data
    if (name === 'paths') {
    generatePaths();
  } else if (name === 'saved') {
    loadStoryList();
    updateBackupInfo();
  } else if (name === 'dialogue') {
    populateDialogueCharacters();
  } else if (name === 'voice') {
    populateVoiceCharacters();
  } else if (name === 'pov') {
    updatePOVListSidebar();
    populateCharacterDropdown('povCharSelectSidebar');
  } else if (name === 'flashback') {
    populateCharacterDropdown('flashbackCharsSelect');
  } else if (name === 'settings') {
    loadSettings();
  }
}

// ============================================================
// 27. اختصارات لوحة المفاتيح | Keyboard Shortcuts
// ============================================================

document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
   // Ctrl/Cmd+S → حفظ | Save
   if ((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.key === 's') {
      e.preventDefault();
      saveStory();
      showStatus("Saved via shortcut");
   }
   // Ctrl/Cmd+G → توليد | Generate
   if ((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.key === 'g') {
      e.preventDefault();
      generateContent();
   }
   // Ctrl/Cmd+N → فصل جديد | New chapter
   if ((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.key === 'n') {
      e.preventDefault();
      if (window.storyData.chapters[window.storyData.chapters.length - 1].content.trim()) {
         addNewChapterManual();
      }
   }
   // F11 → وضع التركيز | Focus mode
   if (e.key === 'F11') { e.preventDefault(); toggleFocusMode(); }
   // F12 → ملء الشاشة | Fullscreen
   if (e.key === 'F12') { e.preventDefault(); toggleFullscreen(); }
});


// ============================================================
// 28. إدارة تسميات الألسنة | Tab Labels Management
// ============================================================

function toggleTabLabels() {
   const tabs     = document.querySelector('.vertical-tabs');
   const isShowing= tabs.classList.contains('show-labels');
   if (isShowing) {
      tabs.classList.remove('show-labels');
      localStorage.setItem('tabLabelsVisible', 'false');
   } else {
      tabs.classList.add('show-labels');
      localStorage.setItem('tabLabelsVisible', 'true');
   }
}

function loadTabLabelsPreference() {
   const showLabels = localStorage.getItem('tabLabelsVisible') === 'true';
   if (showLabels) {
      document.querySelector('.vertical-tabs').classList.add('show-labels');
   }
}


// ============================================================
// 29. التهيئة الرئيسية | Main Initialization
// ============================================================

async function initEditor() {
   try {
      // قراءة الفلتر المحفوظ | Read saved filter
      let filterAlreadySelected = false;
      let savedFilterValue      = 'standard';
      try {
         filterAlreadySelected = localStorage.getItem('contentFilterSelected') === 'true';
         savedFilterValue      = localStorage.getItem('contentFilterValue') || 'standard';
      } catch (e) {
         console.warn('localStorage غير متاح:', e);
      }

      if (filterAlreadySelected) {
         window.storyData.contentFilter = savedFilterValue;
         if (savedFilterValue === 'child') window.storyData.theme = 'kids';
      }

      updateWordCount();
      renderChapterTabs();
      updateComponentVisibility();

      if (!window.storyData.theme) window.storyData.theme = 'dark';
      applyTheme();

      // تهيئة النسخ الاحتياطي | Initialize backup system
      if (kv && typeof kv.backups !== 'undefined') {
         updateBackupInfo();
         startAutoBackup();
      } else {
         console.warn('ميزات النسخ الاحتياطي معطلة: kv.backups مفقودة');
         document.getElementById('backupCount').textContent    = '0';
         document.getElementById('lastBackupTime').textContent = 'Unavailable';
      }

      // تحميل آخر قصة محفوظة | Load last edited story
      let lastEdited = await kv.storySettings.get("lastEdited");
      if (lastEdited) {
         let story = await kv.stories.get(lastEdited);
         if (story) {
            elements.storyTitle.value = story.title;
            if (story.settings)       window.storyData.settings = story.settings;
            if (story.theme)          { window.storyData.theme = story.theme; applyTheme(); }
            if (story.contentFilter)  window.storyData.contentFilter = story.contentFilter;

            if (story.chapters) {
               window.storyData.chapters       = story.chapters;
               window.storyData.currentChapter = story.currentChapter || 1;
               let chapter = window.storyData.chapters.find(ch => ch.id === window.storyData.currentChapter);
               if (chapter) {
                  elements.storyContent.value    = chapter.content;
                  elements.storyContent.readOnly = chapter.readonly || false;
               }
               renderChapterTabs();
            } else {
               elements.storyContent.value    = story.content || '';
               elements.storyContent.readOnly = false;
            }

            updateWordCount();
            applyArabicStyle(elements.storyTitle);
            applyArabicStyle(elements.storyContent);
         }
      }

      // مستمعو الأحداث | Event listeners
      elements.storyTitle.addEventListener('input', () => applyArabicStyle(elements.storyTitle));
      elements.storyContent.addEventListener('input', () => {
         applyArabicStyle(elements.storyContent);
         updateWordCount();
         checkChapterLimit();
      });
      elements.charactersBox.addEventListener('input', () => applyArabicStyle(elements.charactersBox));
      elements.locationsBox.addEventListener('input',  () => applyArabicStyle(elements.locationsBox));
      elements.itemsBox.addEventListener('input',      () => applyArabicStyle(elements.itemsBox));
      elements.eventsBox.addEventListener('input',     () => applyArabicStyle(elements.eventsBox));
      elements.themesBox.addEventListener('input',     () => applyArabicStyle(elements.themesBox));
      elements.conflictsBox.addEventListener('input',  () => applyArabicStyle(elements.conflictsBox));

      ['extractCharacters', 'extractLocations', 'extractItems', 'extractEvents', 'extractThemes', 'extractConflicts'].forEach(id => {
         document.getElementById(id).addEventListener('change', updateComponentVisibility);
      });

      initResizer();

      // استعادة عرض الشريط الجانبي المحفوظ | Restore saved sidebar width
      try {
         const savedWidth = localStorage.getItem('sidebarWidth');
         if (savedWidth) elements.sidebar.style.width = savedWidth + 'px';
      } catch (e) {
         console.warn('تعذر تحميل عرض الشريط الجانبي');
      }

      // الحفظ التلقائي كل 5 ثوانٍ | Auto-save every 5 seconds
      let autoSaveTimeout;
      elements.storyContent.addEventListener("input", () => {
         updateWordCount();
         clearTimeout(autoSaveTimeout);
         autoSaveTimeout = setTimeout(() => { saveCurrentChapter(); saveStory(); }, 5000);
      });
      elements.storyTitle.addEventListener("input", () => {
         clearTimeout(autoSaveTimeout);
         autoSaveTimeout = setTimeout(saveStory, 5000);
      });

      updateFilterBadge();
      if (document.getElementById('lastBackupTimeSidebar')) updateBackupInfo();

      // تهيئة نظام أمان الأطفال | Initialize child safety
      if (window.storyData.contentFilter === 'child') initializeChildSafety();
      elements.storyContent.addEventListener('input', monitorChildSafetyInput);
      elements.storyContent.addEventListener('paste', () => { setTimeout(monitorChildSafetyInput, 500); });

      initializePlugins().catch(e => console.warn('فشل تهيئة الإضافات:', e));
      loadTabLabelsPreference();
      loadFontSettings();
   } catch (e) {
      console.error('Initialization error:', e);
      showStatus('Editor initialization error');
   }
}

// 30. قائمة التصدير المنسدلة | Export Dropdown Menu
// ============================================================

function toggleExportMenu() {
   const menu = document.getElementById('exportMenu');
   menu.classList.contains('show') ? closeExportMenu() : openExportMenu();
}

function openExportMenu() {
   document.getElementById('exportMenu').classList.add('show');
   setTimeout(() => { document.addEventListener('click', closeExportMenuOutside); }, 100);
}

function closeExportMenu() {
   document.getElementById('exportMenu').classList.remove('show');
   document.removeEventListener('click', closeExportMenuOutside);
}

function closeExportMenuOutside(e) {
   const dropdown = document.querySelector('.export-dropdown');
   if (dropdown && !dropdown.contains(e.target)) closeExportMenu();
}

let dynamicChildSafetyBlacklist = null;
let currentSafetyLanguage       = null;

// رسائل التحذير الإيجابية | Positive warning messages
const childSafetyMessages = {

   ]
};

let childSafetyAttempts = 0;

// توليد قائمة سوداء ديناميكية باستخدام الـ AI | Generate dynamic blacklist via AI
async function generateChildSafetyBlacklist(language) {
   showStatus("🛡️ جاري توليد فلتر الأمان للغة " + language + "...");
   try {
      const result = await generateTextAbortable({
         instruction: `Generate a comprehensive list of inappropriate words for CHILDREN (ages 6-12) in ${language} language.

CRITICAL: Respond ONLY with the word list, nothing else. No explanations, no numbering, no categories.

Include words related to:
1. Violence & Weapons (kill, murder, gun, knife, blood, death, fight, attack, hurt, war, etc.)
2. Fear & Horror (ghost, monster, demon, nightmare, scary, terror, haunted, etc.)
3. Romance & Adult themes (love, kiss, sexy, boyfriend, girlfriend, date, wedding, etc.)
4. Profanity & Insults (curse words, insults, hate speech)
5. Substances (drug, alcohol, beer, wine, cigarette, smoking, drunk, etc.)
6. Body parts (inappropriate references)
7. Negative emotions (hate, angry, sad - if extreme)

Requirements:
- ONLY in ${language} language/script
- 100-150 words minimum
- Common variations and slang included
- One word per line
- NO English translations
- NO explanations
- NO categories or headers
- JUST THE WORDS

Generate the list now:`,
         temperature: 0.3
      });

      const words = result
         .trim().split('\n')
         .map(line => line.trim().toLowerCase())
         .filter(word => word.length > 0 && !word.includes(':') && !/^\d/.test(word))
         .filter((word, index, self) => self.indexOf(word) === index);

      if (words.length < 20) throw new Error("القائمة المولدة قصيرة جداً");

      showStatus(`✅ فلتر الأمان جاهز: ${words.length} كلمة`);
      return words;
   } catch (error) {
      console.error("فشل توليد القائمة السوداء:", error);
      showStatus("⚠️ استخدام فلتر الأمان الطارئ");
      return emergencyBlacklist.universal;
   }
}

// تحميل القائمة السوداء (من الذاكرة المخبأة أو توليد جديد) | Load blacklist (from cache or generate new)
async function loadChildSafetyBlacklist(language) {
   if (dynamicChildSafetyBlacklist && currentSafetyLanguage === language) {
      return dynamicChildSafetyBlacklist;
   }

   const storageKey = `childSafety_${language}`;
   const cached     = localStorage.getItem(storageKey);

   if (cached) {
      try {
         const parsed    = JSON.parse(cached);
         const ageInDays = (Date.now() - parsed.timestamp) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24);
         if (ageInDays < 30 && parsed.words && parsed.words.length > 20) {
            dynamicChildSafetyBlacklist = parsed.words;
            currentSafetyLanguage       = language;
            console.log(`✅ تم تحميل ${parsed.words.length} كلمة أمان من الذاكرة المخبأة`);
            return dynamicChildSafetyBlacklist;
         }
      } catch (e) {
         console.warn("الذاكرة المخبأة تالفة، جاري إعادة التوليد...");
      }
   }

   const words = await generateChildSafetyBlacklist(language);
   try {
      localStorage.setItem(storageKey, JSON.stringify({ words, timestamp: Date.now(), language }));
   } catch (e) {
      console.warn("تعذر تخزين قائمة الأمان مؤقتاً:", e);
   }

   dynamicChildSafetyBlacklist = words;
   currentSafetyLanguage       = language;
   return words;
}

// تهيئة نظام أمان الأطفال | Initialize child safety system
async function initializeChildSafety() {
   if (window.storyData.contentFilter !== 'child') return;

   const language    = detectLanguage(elements.storyContent.value || elements.storyTitle.value);
   const languageMap = {
      'Arabic': 'Arabic', 'Chinese': 'Chinese (Simplified)', 'Japanese': 'Japanese',
      'Korean': 'Korean', 'Russian': 'Russian', 'Hebrew': 'Hebrew', 'Thai': 'Thai',
      'Persian': 'Persian', 'French': 'French', 'German': 'German', 'Spanish': 'Spanish',
      'Italian': 'Italian', 'Portuguese': 'Portuguese', 'Turkish': 'Turkish',
      'Hindi': 'Hindi', 'Urdu': 'Urdu', 'Bengali': 'Bengali', 'default': 'English'
   };

   const targetLanguage = languageMap[language] || languageMap.default;
   loadChildSafetyBlacklist(targetLanguage).catch(err => { console.error("فشلت تهيئة الأمان:", err); });
}

// فحص أمان المحتوى | Check content safety
function checkChildSafety(text) {
   if (window.storyData.contentFilter !== 'child') return { safe: true };

   const lowerText = text.toLowerCase();
   const language  = detectLanguage(text);
   const langCode  = language === 'Arabic' ? 'ar' : 'en';
   const results   = { safe: true, foundWords: [], foundPatterns: [], severity: 'none', message: '' };
   const safeList  = safeContexts[langCode] || {};

   // فحص الأنماط الخطرة | Check dangerous patterns
   for (let category in dangerousPatterns) {
      const patterns = dangerousPatterns[category][langCode] || [];
      for (let pattern of patterns) {
         if (pattern.test(text)) {
            results.safe         = false;
            results.foundPatterns.push(category);
            results.severity     = 'high';
         }
      }
   }

   // فحص القائمة السوداء | Check blacklist
   const blacklist = dynamicChildSafetyBlacklist || emergencyBlacklist.universal;
   for (let word of blacklist) {
      if (!word || word.length < 2) continue;

      let inSafeContext = false;
      for (let safePhrase of Object.values(safeList).flat()) {
         if (lowerText.includes(safePhrase.toLowerCase()) && safePhrase.toLowerCase().includes(word.toLowerCase())) {
            inSafeContext = true; break;
         }
      }
      if (inSafeContext) continue;

      const regex = new RegExp('\\b' + word.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&') + '\\b', 'i');
      if (regex.test(lowerText)) {
         results.safe = false;
         results.foundWords.push(word);
         if (severityLevels.high.includes(word))                                  results.severity = 'high';
         else if (severityLevels.medium.includes(word) && results.severity !== 'high') results.severity = 'medium';
         else if (results.severity === 'none')                                     results.severity = 'low';
      }
   }

   if (!results.safe) {
      childSafetyAttempts++;
      const messages = childSafetyMessages[langCode] || childSafetyMessages.default;
      results.message = messages[Math.floor(Math.random() * messages.length)];
   }

   return results;
}

// عرض تحذير أمان الأطفال | Show child safety warning modal
function showChildSafetyWarning(safetyResult) {
   const language  = detectLanguage(elements.storyContent.value || elements.storyTitle.value);
   const isRTL     = ['Arabic', 'Hebrew', 'Persian', 'Urdu'].includes(language);

   const messages = {
      en: { title: "دعنا نكتب قصة جميلة! 🌟", explanation: "لاحظنا أن القصة تحتوي على كلمات قد لا تكون مناسبة. دعنا نجعل قصتك مليئة بالمرح والإيجابية!", button: "فهمت! سأكتب شيئاً جميلاً ✨" },
      ar: { title: "دعنا نكتب قصة جميلة! 🌟", explanation: "لاحظنا أن القصة تحتوي على كلمات قد لا تكون مناسبة. دعنا نجعل قصتك مليئة بالمرح والإيجابية!", button: "فهمت! سأكتب شيئاً جميلاً ✨" },
      default: { title: "Let's Create Something Wonderful! 🌟", explanation: "Let's make your story positive and fun for everyone!", button: "I'll Write Something Beautiful! ✨" }
   };

   const msg = messages[language.toLowerCase()] || messages.default;
   let severityEmoji = '🌈', severityColor = '#FF6B9D', severityText = '';

   if (safetyResult.severity === 'high')   { severityEmoji = '🚫'; severityColor = '#dc2626'; severityText = isRTL ? 'محتوى غير مناسب جداً' : 'Highly Inappropriate Content'; }
   else if (safetyResult.severity === 'medium') { severityEmoji = '⚠️'; severityColor = '#f59e0b'; severityText = isRTL ? 'محتوى يحتاج تعديل' : 'Content Needs Adjustment'; }
   else { severityEmoji = '🌈'; severityText = isRTL ? 'لنكتب شيئاً أجمل' : 'Let\'s Write Better'; }

   const modal          = document.createElement('div');
   modal.id             = 'childSafetyModal';
   modal.style.cssText  = 'display:flex;position:fixed;top:0;left:0;width:100%;height:100%;background:rgba(0,0,0,0.5);z-index:99999;align-items:center;justify-content:center;backdrop-filter:blur(5px);animation:fadeIn 0.3s ease';
   const dirStyle       = isRTL ? 'direction:rtl;text-align:right' : 'direction:ltr;text-align:center';
   const fontStyle      = isRTL ? "font-family:'Tajawal','Comic Sans MS',cursive" : "font-family:'Comic Sans MS',cursive";

   modal.innerHTML = `
      <div style="background:linear-gradient(135deg, #FFF9E6 0%, #FFE6F0 100%);padding:35px;border-radius:20px;max-width:500px;${dirStyle};border:3px solid #FF6B9D;box-shadow:0 20px 60px rgba(255,107,157,0.3);animation:slideUp 0.4s ease;${fontStyle}">
         <div style="font-size:4rem;margin-bottom:20px;animation:bounce 1s infinite;text-align:center">${severityEmoji}</div>
         ${severityText ? `<div style="background:${severityColor};color:white;padding:8px 16px;border-radius:20px;font-size:0.85rem;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:12px;display:inline-block">${severityText}</div>` : ''}
         <h2 style="margin:0 0 15px 0;color:#FF6B9D;font-size:1.6rem">${msg.title}</h2>
         <p style="color:#5D6D7E;margin-bottom:20px;font-size:1.05rem;line-height:1.6">${msg.explanation}</p>
         <div style="background:#FFF5DC;padding:15px;border-radius:12px;margin-bottom:25px;border-left:4px solid #F4D03F">
            <p style="margin:0;color:#2C3E50;font-size:0.95rem;font-weight:600">${safetyResult.message}</p>
         </div>
         <button onclick="closeChildSafetyWarning()" style="padding:14px 35px;font-size:1.1rem;background:linear-gradient(135deg, #FF6B9D 0%, #FFA8CC 100%);color:white;border:none;border-radius:25px;cursor:pointer;font-weight:700;box-shadow:0 4px 12px rgba(255,107,157,0.4);display:block;margin:0 auto">
            ${msg.button}
         </button>
      </div>
   `;
   document.body.appendChild(modal);

   // حقن أنيميشن الـ modal | Inject modal animations
   if (!document.getElementById('childSafetyAnimations')) {
      const style        = document.createElement('style');
      style.id           = 'childSafetyAnimations';
      style.textContent  = `
         @keyframes bounce  { 0%, 100% { transform: translateY(0); }  50% { transform: translateY(-10px); } }
         @keyframes fadeIn  { from { opacity: 0; }                     to   { opacity: 1; } }
         @keyframes slideUp { from { transform: translateY(30px); opacity: 0; } to { transform: translateY(0); opacity: 1; } }
      `;
      document.head.appendChild(style);
   }
}

function closeChildSafetyWarning() {
   const modal = document.getElementById('childSafetyModal');
   if (modal) { modal.style.animation = 'fadeOut 0.3s ease'; setTimeout(() => modal.remove(), 300); }
}

// مراقبة مدخلات المستخدم للمحتوى غير المناسب | Monitor user input for inappropriate content
let safetyCheckTimeout = null;
function monitorChildSafetyInput() {
   if (window.storyData.contentFilter !== 'child') return;
   clearTimeout(safetyCheckTimeout);
   safetyCheckTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
      const text = elements.storyContent.value;
      if (text.trim().length < 50) return;
      const safetyCheck = checkChildSafety(text);
      if (!safetyCheck.safe) showChildSafetyWarning(safetyCheck);
   }, 2000);
}

function getChildSafetyStats() {
   return {
      attempts:    childSafetyAttempts,
      status:      childSafetyAttempts === 0 ? '🌟 مثالي!' : '📚 يتعلم',
      wordsLoaded: dynamicChildSafetyBlacklist ? dynamicChildSafetyBlacklist.length : 0,
      language:    currentSafetyLanguage || 'لم يتم التحميل'
   };
}

// مسح ذاكرة فلتر الأمان | Clear child safety cache
function clearChildSafetyCache() {
   const keys = Object.keys(localStorage).filter(k => k.startsWith('childSafety_'));
   keys.forEach(k => localStorage.removeItem(k));
   dynamicChildSafetyBlacklist = null;
   currentSafetyLanguage       = null;
   showStatus("🔄 تم مسح ذاكرة فلتر الأمان");
}

// التحقق من مخرجات الـ AI بالذكاء الاصطناعي | Validate AI output via AI check
async function validateAIOutput(generatedText, language = 'English') {
   if (window.storyData.contentFilter !== 'child') return { safe: true };
   if (!generatedText || generatedText.trim().length < 20) return { safe: true };

   try {
      const result = await generateTextAbortable({
         instruction: `You are a child safety expert. Analyze this text for appropriateness for children ages 6-12.

Check for:
1. Violence or death (even indirect references like "stopped breathing")
2. Scary, frightening, or horror elements
3. Romance or adult themes
4. Inappropriate language or insults
5. Drugs, alcohol, or dangerous substances
6. Negative emotions (extreme sadness, despair)

Respond with ONLY ONE WORD: SAFE or UNSAFE

Language: ${language}
Text to analyze:
${generatedText.slice(-1500)}`,
         temperature: 0.1
      });

      const isSafe = result.trim().toUpperCase().includes('SAFE');
      return {
         safe:      isSafe,
         checkedBy: 'AI',
         message:   isSafe ? '' : '🤖 المحتوى المولد يحتاج مراجعة. دعنا نجرب اتجاهاً مختلفاً!'
      };
   } catch (error) {
      console.warn('فشل التحقق بالذكاء الاصطناعي، استخدام فحص الكلمات:', error);
      return checkChildSafety(generatedText);
   }
}

// دالة التوليد مع فحص الأمان | Generate content with safety check
async function generateContentWithSafety() {
   if (window.storyData.contentFilter === 'child') {
      const inputCheck = checkChildSafety(elements.storyContent.value);
      if (!inputCheck.safe) { showChildSafetyWarning(inputCheck); return; }
   }

   const contentBefore = elements.storyContent.value;
   const lengthBefore  = contentBefore.length;
   await _generateContentCore();

   if (window.storyData.contentFilter === 'child') {
      const contentAfter = elements.storyContent.value;
      const newContent   = contentAfter.slice(lengthBefore);

      if (newContent.trim().length > 20) {
         const quickCheck = checkChildSafety(newContent);
         if (!quickCheck.safe) {
            elements.storyContent.value = contentBefore;
            updateWordCount();
            showChildSafetyWarning({ ...quickCheck, message: '🤖 حاول الذكاء الاصطناعي إضافة محتوى غير مناسب. دعنا نوجهه بشكل أفضل!' });
            return;
         }

         showStatus('🛡️ جاري التحقق من سلامة المحتوى...');
         const language = detectLanguage(newContent);
         const aiCheck  = await validateAIOutput(newContent, language);
         if (!aiCheck.safe) {
            elements.storyContent.value = contentBefore;
            updateWordCount();
            showChildSafetyWarning({ safe: false, foundWords: [], message: aiCheck.message || '🤖 دعنا نحاول كتابة هذا الجزء بشكل مختلف!' });
            return;
         }

         showStatus('✅ تم التحقق من سلامة المحتوى!');
      }
   }
}

// — مولد الأسماء | Name Generator —
async function generateNamesSidebar() {
   const culture      = document.getElementById('nameCultureSidebar').value;
   const gender       = document.getElementById('nameGenderSidebar').value;
   const requirements = document.getElementById('nameRequirementsSidebar').value.trim();
   const progress     = document.getElementById('nameGeneratorSidebarProgress');
   const results      = document.getElementById('generatedNamesSidebar');

   progress.style.display = 'flex';
   results.innerHTML = '';

   try {
      let genderInstruction = { 'male': 'male names only', 'female': 'female names only', 'neutral': 'gender-neutral names only', 'mixed': 'a mix of male and female names' }[gender];
      let languageInstruction = getLanguageInstruction();
      let filterInstructions  = getFilterInstructions();

      let result = await generateTextAbortable({
         instruction: `Generate 10 authentic ${culture} ${genderInstruction}.
      
Requirements:
- Full names (first + surname)
- Culturally accurate
${requirements ? '- ' + requirements : ''}${languageInstruction}${filterInstructions}

Format: numbered list
1. Name
2. Name
...`,
         temperature: 0.8
      });

      let names = result.trim().split('\n').filter(line => /^\d+\./.test(line));
      let html  = '<div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:6px">';
      names.forEach(name => {
         let cleanName = name.replace(/^\d+\.\s*/, '');
         html += `<div style="padding:8px;border-radius:4px;background:var(--bg2);display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center">
            <span style="color:var(--txt1);font-size:0.85rem">${cleanName}</span>
            <button onclick="copyToClipboard('${cleanName.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}','${cleanName}')" class="btn-small btn-primary">Copy</button>
         </div>`;
      });
      html += '</div>';
      results.innerHTML = html;
   } catch (e) {
      results.innerHTML = `<p style="color:var(--dng1)">${e.message}</p>`;
   } finally {
      progress.style.display = 'none';
   }
}

// — قوالب القصة | Story Templates —
let sidebarTemplateData = null;

async function generateTemplateSidebar() {
   const genre    = document.getElementById('templateGenreSidebar').value;
   const chapters = document.getElementById('templateChaptersSidebar').value;
   const desc     = document.getElementById('templateDescSidebar').value.trim();
   const progress = document.getElementById('templateSidebarProgress');
   const results  = document.getElementById('generatedTemplateSidebar');

   progress.style.display = 'flex';
   results.innerHTML = '';

   try {
      let languageInstruction = getLanguageInstruction();
      let filterInstructions  = getFilterInstructions();
      let result = await generateTextAbortable({
         instruction: `Create a ${chapters}-chapter ${genre} story structure.
      
${desc ? 'Requirements: ' + desc : ''}

Format each chapter:
Chapter X: [Title]
- Main Events: [description]
- Character Development: [description]
- Conflicts: [description]${languageInstruction}${filterInstructions}`,
         temperature: 0.7
      });
      sidebarTemplateData  = result.trim();
      results.textContent  = result.trim();
   } catch (e) {
      results.innerHTML = `<p style="color:var(--dng1)">${e.message}</p>`;
   } finally {
      progress.style.display = 'none';
   }
}

async function applyTemplateSidebar() {
   if (!sidebarTemplateData) { alert('Generate a template first'); return; }
   if (!confirm('Apply this template to guide your writing?')) return;

   showStatus('Applying template...');
   elements.storyProgress.style.display = 'flex';

   try {
      let languageInstruction = getLanguageInstruction();
      let filterInstructions  = getFilterInstructions();
      let settingsInfo        = getSettingsInstructions();
      let startLength         = elements.storyContent.value.length;

      await generateTextAbortable({
         instruction: `${elements.storyContent.value ? 'Continue' : 'Write'} a story following this structure:

${sidebarTemplateData}

${settingsInfo}${languageInstruction}${filterInstructions}

${elements.storyContent.value ? 'Continue from:\n' + elements.storyContent.value + '\n\nContinue' : 'Begin'}:`,
         temperature: 0.8,
         onChunk: (data) => {
            if (shouldAbortGeneration) return;
            elements.storyContent.value += data.textChunk;
            updateWordCount();
            applyArabicStyle(elements.storyContent);
            elements.storyContent.scrollTop = elements.storyContent.scrollHeight;
            checkChapterLimit();
         }
      });

      if (elements.storyContent.value.length > startLength) elements.storyContent.value += '\n\n';
      showStatus('Template applied');
      await generatePaths();
   } catch (e) {
      showStatus('Error: ' + e.message);
   } finally {
      elements.storyProgress.style.display = 'none';
   }
}

// — محلل صوت الشخصية | Character Voice Analyzer —

   populateCharacterDropdown('voiceCharacterSidebar');
}

async function analyzeVoiceSidebar() {
   const char = document.getElementById('voiceCharacterSidebar').value;
   if (!char) { alert('Select a character'); return; }

   const progress = document.getElementById('voiceSidebarProgress');
   const results  = document.getElementById('voiceSidebarResults');
   progress.style.display = 'flex';
   results.innerHTML = '';

   try {
      let allContent          = window.storyData.chapters.map(ch => ch.content).join('\n\n');
      let languageInstruction = getLanguageInstruction(allContent);
      let filterInstructions  = getFilterInstructions();
      let result = await generateTextAbortable({
         instruction: `Analyze ${char}'s voice and speech patterns.

Consider:
1. Vocabulary and word choice
2. Sentence structure
3. Tone and emotional expression
4. Speech mannerisms
5. How it reflects personality

Provide suggestions for making their voice more distinct.${languageInstruction}${filterInstructions}

Story: ${allContent.slice(-4000)}`,
         temperature: 0.4
      });
      results.textContent = result;
   } catch (e) {
      results.innerHTML = `<p style="color:var(--dng1)">${e.message}</p>`;
   } finally {
      progress.style.display = 'none';
   }
}

// — مدرب الكتابة | Writing Coach —

      };

${question ? 'Question: ' + question : ''}

Provide:
1. Strengths in current writing
2. Areas for improvement
3. Specific techniques
4. Actionable steps${languageInstruction}${filterInstructions}

Story excerpt: ${allContent.slice(-3000)}`,
         temperature: 0.7
      });
      results.textContent = result;
   } catch (e) {
      results.innerHTML = `<p style="color:var(--dng1)">${e.message}</p>`;
   } finally {
      progress.style.display = 'none';
   }
}

// — مدير وجهات النظر (POV) | POV Manager —
function addPOVCharacterSidebar() {
   const name = document.getElementById('povCharNameSidebar').value.trim();
   if (!name) { alert('Enter character name'); return; }
   if (!window.storyData.povCharacters) window.storyData.povCharacters = [];
   if (!window.storyData.povCharacters.includes(name)) {
      window.storyData.povCharacters.push(name);
      updatePOVListSidebar();
      document.getElementById('povCharNameSidebar').value = '';
      showStatus(`${name} added`);
   } else {
      alert('Character already exists');
   }
}

function updatePOVListSidebar() {
   const list   = document.getElementById('povCharListSidebar');
   const select = document.getElementById('povSwitchSidebar');

   if (!window.storyData.povCharacters || window.storyData.povCharacters.length === 0) {
      list.innerHTML   = '<p style="color:var(--txt3);text-align:center;padding:20px">No POV characters</p>';
      select.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- Select --</option>';
      return;
   }

   let html = '<div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:6px">';
   window.storyData.povCharacters.forEach(char => {
      html += `<div style="padding:8px;background:var(--bg2);border-radius:4px;display:flex;justify-content:space-between">
         <span style="color:var(--txt1);font-size:0.85rem">${char}</span>
         <button onclick="removePOVSidebar('${char}')" class="btn-small btn-danger">Remove</button>
      </div>`;
   });
   html += '</div>';
   list.innerHTML = html;

   select.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- Select --</option>';
   window.storyData.povCharacters.forEach(char => {
      const opt = document.createElement('option');
      opt.value = opt.textContent = char;
      select.appendChild(opt);
   });
}

function removePOVSidebar(char) {
   if (window.storyData.povCharacters) {
      window.storyData.povCharacters = window.storyData.povCharacters.filter(c => c !== char);
      updatePOVListSidebar();
   }
}

async function switchPOVSidebar() {
   const newPOV  = document.getElementById('povSwitchSidebar').value;
   if (!newPOV) { alert('Select a character'); return; }
   const content = elements.storyContent.value;
   if (content.trim().length < 50) { alert('Not enough content'); return; }

   const progress = document.getElementById('povSidebarProgress');
   progress.style.display = 'flex';

   try {
      let languageInstruction = getLanguageInstruction(content);
      let filterInstructions  = getFilterInstructions();
      let result = await generateTextAbortable({
         instruction: `Rewrite from ${newPOV}'s POV:

${content.slice(-1500)}

Consider ${newPOV}'s perspective, thoughts, and feelings.${languageInstruction}${filterInstructions}`,
         temperature: 0.6
      });
      insertToStory(result, `[POV: ${newPOV}]\n\n`, '', `Switched to ${newPOV}'s POV`);
   } catch (e) {
      showStatus('Error: ' + e.message);
   } finally {
      progress.style.display = 'none';
   }
}

// — مدير الاسترجاعات | Flashback Manager —
async function generateFlashbackSidebar() {
   const desc     = document.getElementById('flashbackDescSidebar').value.trim();
   const time     = document.getElementById('flashbackTimeSidebar').value.trim();
   const chars    = document.getElementById('flashbackCharsSidebar').value.trim();
   if (!desc) { alert('Describe the flashback'); return; }

   const progress = document.getElementById('flashbackSidebarProgress');
   const results  = document.getElementById('flashbackSidebarResult');
   progress.style.display = 'flex';
   results.innerHTML = '';

   try {
      let languageInstruction = getLanguageInstruction();
      let filterInstructions  = getFilterInstructions();
      let result = await generateTextAbortable({
         instruction: `Write a flashback scene: ${desc}

Time: ${time || 'غير محدد'}
Characters: ${chars || 'غير محدد'}

Make it:
- Vivid and sensory
- Emotionally resonant
- Use past tense${languageInstruction}${filterInstructions}`,
         temperature: 0.7
      });
      results.textContent = result;
   } catch (e) {
      results.innerHTML = `<p style="color:var(--dng1)">${e.message}</p>`;
   } finally {
      progress.style.display = 'none';
   }
}

function insertFlashbackSidebar() {
   const content = document.getElementById('flashbackSidebarResult').textContent;
   if (content && !content.includes('Error')) {
      insertToStory(content, '[Flashback]\n\n', '\n\n[End Flashback]', 'Flashback inserted');
   } else {
      alert('Generate a flashback first');
   }
}

// نسخ نص إلى الحافظة | Copy text to clipboard
function copyToClipboard(text, display) {
   navigator.clipboard.writeText(display);
   showStatus(`Copied: ${display}`);
}

function isMobile() {
   return window.innerWidth <= 768;
}

// عناوين تبويبات الـ Bottom Sheet | Bottom sheet tab titles
const sheetTabTitles = {
   components:  'Story Components',
   analytics:   'Analytics',
   nameGen:     'Name Generator',
   templates:   'Templates',
   dialogue:    'Dialogue',
   consistency: 'Consistency',
   voice:       'Voice Analyzer',
   coach:       'Writing Coach',
   pov:         'POV Manager',
   flashback:   'Flashback',
   timeline:    'Timeline',
   saved:       'Files & Backups',
   guide:       'Help & Guide',
   paths:       'Story Paths',
   comments:    'Comments & Feedback',
   updates:     "What's New"
};

// فتح تبويب في الـ Bottom Sheet (جوال) | Open tab in Bottom Sheet (mobile)
function openSheetTab(tabName) {
   if (!isMobile()) { switchTab(tabName); return; }

   const sheet    = document.getElementById('bottomSheet');
   const overlay  = document.getElementById('bottomSheetOverlay');
   const content  = document.getElementById('sheetContent');
   const titleEl  = document.getElementById('sheetTitle');
   const tabId    = tabName + 'Tab';
   const sourceTab= document.getElementById(tabId);

   if (tabName === 'comments') {
      content.innerHTML = '<div class="section-header"><span><span class="ms">comment</span> Comments & Feedback</span></div>';
      const commentsContainer = document.getElementById('commentsContainer');
      if (commentsContainer) {
         commentsContainer.setAttribute('data-moved-to-sheet', 'true');
         content.appendChild(commentsContainer);
      }
   } else if (tabName === 'paths') {
      content.innerHTML = `<div style="padding:4px 0">${document.getElementById('pathsBox').outerHTML}</div>`;
      setTimeout(() => {
         const newBox = content.querySelector('#pathsBox');
         if (newBox) newBox.id = 'pathsBoxSheet';
      }, 0);
   } else if (sourceTab) {
      content.innerHTML = sourceTab.innerHTML;
   } else {
      content.innerHTML = '<p style="color:var(--txt3);text-align:center;padding:40px">جاري التحميل...</p>';
   }

   titleEl.textContent = sheetTabTitles[tabName] || tabName;
   sheet.classList.add('open');
   overlay.classList.add('active');
   document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';

   document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
   const navBtn = document.getElementById('nav-' + tabName);
   if (navBtn) navBtn.classList.add('active');
}

// إغلاق الـ Bottom Sheet | Close Bottom Sheet
function closeBottomSheet() {
   // إعادة حاوية التعليقات لمكانها | Return comments container to its tab
   const commentsContainer = document.getElementById('commentsContainer');
   if (commentsContainer && commentsContainer.getAttribute('data-moved-to-sheet')) {
      const commentsTab = document.getElementById('commentsTab');
      if (commentsTab) {
         commentsContainer.removeAttribute('data-moved-to-sheet');
         commentsTab.appendChild(commentsContainer);
      }
   }
   document.getElementById('bottomSheet').classList.remove('open');
   document.getElementById('bottomSheetOverlay').classList.remove('active');
   document.body.style.overflow = '';
}

// سحب الـ Bottom Sheet للإغلاق | Swipe Bottom Sheet to close
(function initSheetSwipe() {
   let startY    = 0;
   let isDragging= false;
   const handle  = document.getElementById('sheetHandle');
   if (!handle) return;

   handle.addEventListener('touchstart', (e) => { startY = e.touches[0].clientY; isDragging = true; }, { passive: true });
   document.addEventListener('touchmove', (e) => {
      if (!isDragging) return;
      const dy = e.touches[0].clientY - startY;
      if (dy > 0) document.getElementById('bottomSheet').style.transform = `translateY(${dy}px)`;
   }, { passive: true });
   document.addEventListener('touchend', (e) => {
      if (!isDragging) return;
      isDragging = false;
      const dy   = e.changedTouches[0].clientY - startY;
      document.getElementById('bottomSheet').style.transform = '';
      if (dy > 80) closeBottomSheet();
   });
})();

// تنقل شريط الجوال | Mobile nav bar click handler
function mobileNavClick(tabName, btnEl) {
   if (!isMobile()) return;
   closeMoreMenu();
   document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
   if (btnEl) btnEl.classList.add('active');
   openSheetTab(tabName);
}

// قائمة المزيد | More menu toggle
function toggleMoreMenu(btnEl) {
   const menu   = document.getElementById('moreMenu');
   const isOpen = menu.classList.contains('open');
   if (isOpen) {
      closeMoreMenu();
      document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
   } else {
      menu.classList.add('open');
      document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
      if (btnEl) btnEl.classList.add('active');
   }
}

function closeMoreMenu() {
   document.getElementById('moreMenu').classList.remove('open');
}

// إغلاق قائمة المزيد عند النقر خارجها | Close more menu on outside click
document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
   const menu    = document.getElementById('moreMenu');
   const moreBtn = document.getElementById('nav-more');
   if (menu && !menu.contains(e.target) && moreBtn && !moreBtn.contains(e.target)) closeMoreMenu();
});

// — زر الإجراء السريع (FAB) | Floating Action Button (FAB) —
let fabOpen = false;

function toggleFAB() {
   fabOpen = !fabOpen;
   document.getElementById('fabMain').classList.toggle('open', fabOpen);
   document.getElementById('fabSpeedDial').classList.toggle('open', fabOpen);
}

function closeFAB() {
   fabOpen = false;
   document.getElementById('fabMain').classList.remove('open');
   document.getElementById('fabSpeedDial').classList.remove('open');
}

// تحديث زر إيقاف الـ FAB عند تشغيل الـ AI | Update FAB stop button on AI state change
const origSetAIRunning = window.setAIRunning;
window.setAIRunning = function(running) {
   if (origSetAIRunning) origSetAIRunning(running);
   const stopAction   = document.getElementById('fabStopAction');
   if (stopAction)    stopAction.style.display = running ? 'flex' : 'none';
   const mobileAIBtn  = document.getElementById('mobileAIBtn');
   if (mobileAIBtn && isMobile()) mobileAIBtn.style.display = running ? 'none' : 'inline-flex';
};

// تهيئة واجهة الجوال | Initialize mobile UI
function initMobile() {
   if (!isMobile()) return;
   const mobileAIBtn = document.getElementById('mobileAIBtn');
   if (mobileAIBtn) mobileAIBtn.style.display = 'inline-flex';
   const resizer     = document.getElementById('resizer');
   if (resizer) resizer.style.display = 'none';
}

// تجاوز initEditor لإضافة تهيئة الجوال | Override initEditor to add mobile init
const origInitEditor = window.initEditor;
window.initEditor = async function() {
   if (origInitEditor) await origInitEditor();
   initMobile();
};

// تحديث واجهة الجوال عند تغيير حجم النافذة | Update mobile UI on resize
window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
   if (!isMobile()) { closeBottomSheet(); closeMoreMenu(); closeFAB(); }
   else initMobile();
});

// ============================================================
// أدوات تنسيق خط المحرر | Editor Font Formatting Tools
// ============================================================

const FONT_FAMILY_MAP = {
   'nunito':  "'Nunito', 'Tajawal', -apple-system, sans-serif",
   'tajawal': "'Tajawal', 'Nunito', sans-serif",
   'inter':   "'Inter', -apple-system, sans-serif",
   'georgia': "Georgia, 'Times New Roman', serif",
   'mono':    "'Courier New', 'Consolas', monospace"
};

function applyFontSettings() {
   const size   = document.getElementById('fontSizeSelect')?.value   || '14';
   const weight = document.getElementById('fontWeightSelect')?.value || '400';
   const family = document.getElementById('fontFamilySelect')?.value || 'nunito';
   const lh     = document.getElementById('lineHeightSelect')?.value || '1.7';
   const el     = document.getElementById('storyContent');
   if (el) {
      el.style.fontSize   = size + 'px';
      el.style.fontWeight = weight;
      el.style.fontFamily = FONT_FAMILY_MAP[family] || FONT_FAMILY_MAP['nunito'];
      el.style.lineHeight = lh;
   }
   try {
      localStorage.setItem('editorFontSize',   size);
      localStorage.setItem('editorFontWeight', weight);
      localStorage.setItem('editorFontFamily', family);
      localStorage.setItem('editorLineHeight', lh);
   } catch(e) {}
}

function resetFontSettings() {
   const defaults = {
      fontSizeSelect:   '14',
      fontWeightSelect: '400',
      fontFamilySelect: 'nunito',
      lineHeightSelect: '1.7'
   };
   Object.entries(defaults).forEach(([id, val]) => {
      const el = document.getElementById(id);
      if (el) el.value = val;
   });
   applyFontSettings();
   try {
      ['editorFontSize','editorFontWeight','editorFontFamily','editorLineHeight']
         .forEach(k => localStorage.removeItem(k));
   } catch(e) {}
}

function loadFontSettings() {
   try {
      const map = {
         fontSizeSelect:   localStorage.getItem('editorFontSize')   || '14',
         fontWeightSelect: localStorage.getItem('editorFontWeight') || '400',
         fontFamilySelect: localStorage.getItem('editorFontFamily') || 'nunito',
         lineHeightSelect: localStorage.getItem('editorLineHeight') || '1.7'
      };
      Object.entries(map).forEach(([id, val]) => {
         const el = document.getElementById(id);
         if (el) el.value = val;
      });
      applyFontSettings();
   } catch(e) {}
}
