<script>
/* ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   UNIVERSAL ADMIN PANEL — لوحة التحكم الشاملة
   Story Writer Pro v3.3.0
   Shortcut: Ctrl+Shift+U — الاختصار
   ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// ⚙️ CONFIG — عدّل هذه القيم قبل النشر | Edit before publishing
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
const UPDATES_CONFIG = {
  GITHUB_USERNAME : 'hushamQA',       // ← اسم حسابك — Your GitHub username
  GIST_ID         : 'db8aa17552afe87ff0aaadc54308e967',           // ← معرّف الـ Gist — Gist ID from URL
  ADMIN_HASH      : '18e4c8455d2e5290e448911afbc6416f8c96dd337ab36ee38a36f69215adfecf',   // ← هاش كلمة المرور — From hash calculator
  FILENAME        : 'story-writer-updates.json'    // اسم الملف — Filename in Gist
};

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// ألوان الكتل — Block colors (keep for changelog blocks)
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
const UA_COLORS = {
  blue  : 'var(--acc2)',  green : 'var(--suc1)',
  amber : 'var(--wrn)',   red   : 'var(--dng1)',
  gray  : 'var(--txt3)'
};

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// قائمة أيقونات Material Symbols — Icon list
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
const UA_ALL_ICONS = [
  'new_releases','star','check_circle','build','text_fields','calendar_month',
  'schedule','edit','settings','info','warning','error','lock','person','group',
  'language','translate','auto_awesome','bolt','favorite','bookmark','flag',
  'label','tag','category','folder','download','upload','cloud','cloud_upload',
  'cloud_download','sync','refresh','update','history','timeline','bar_chart',
  'pie_chart','analytics','insights','trending_up','search','filter_list','sort',
  'tune','notifications','mail','chat','forum','link','share','send','publish',
  'rocket_launch','explore','map','home','business','payments','receipt',
  'shopping_cart','add_circle','remove_circle','cancel','done','done_all','close',
  'menu','apps','widgets','dashboard','grid_view','view_list','layers','palette',
  'brush','create','draw','edit_note','content_copy','code','terminal',
  'bug_report','developer_mode','api','security','verified','shield',
  'admin_panel_settings','key','fingerprint','speed','memory','storage',
  'devices','computer','wifi','image','photo_camera','videocam','mic',
  'headphones','volume_up','music_note','movie','article','book','school',
  'science','psychology','public','water_drop','sunny','eco','fitness_center',
  'sports_soccer','emoji_events','celebration','gift','local_offer','percent',
  'currency_exchange','savings','account_balance','credit_card','help',
  'contact_support','question_answer','feedback','thumb_up','thumb_down',
  'horizontal_rule','title','format_bold','format_list_bulleted','table_chart',
  'web','open_in_new','launch','extension','handshake','smart_toy','visibility',
  'route','assignment','campaign','error_outline','announcement','broadcast_on_home',
  'new_label','fiber_new','whatshot','local_fire_department','military_tech',
  'workspace_premium','diamond','hexagon','pentagon','interests','hub',
  'integration_instructions','inventory_2','category','style','format_paint'
];

/* ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   AdminPanel — الكائن الرئيسي الشامل | Main singleton
   ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
const AdminPanel = {
   
   /* ── مساعدات HTML | HTML helpers ───────────────────────── */
  _esc(s) { return String(s).replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;'); },
  _he(s)  { return this._esc(s); },

  /* ── الحالة الداخلية — Internal state ─────────────────────── */
  data: {
    announcement: { active: false, text: '', type: 'info' },
    changelog    : { html: '', blocks: [], lastUpdated: '' },
    featureFlags : {},
    content      : {},
    settings     : { version: 'v3.2', status: 'online', appName: 'Story Writer Pro' },
    maintenance  : { active: false, message: 'We\'ll be back shortly. Thank you for your patience!' },
    quickLinks   : [],
    notes        : ''
  },
  activeModule   : 'announcement',
  collapsedBlocks: new Set(),
  _toastTimer    : null,
  _iconTarget    : null,

  /* ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     INIT — التهيئة
     ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  async init() {
    // اختصار لوحة المفاتيح — Ctrl+Shift+U keyboard shortcut
    document.addEventListener('keydown', e => {
      if ((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.shiftKey && e.key.toUpperCase() === 'U') {
        e.preventDefault(); this.open();
      }
    });
    // إغلاق نافذة الأيقونات عند الضغط خارجها — close icon modal on outside click
    const im = document.getElementById('ua-icon-modal');
    if (im) im.addEventListener('click', e => { if (e.target === im) this.closeIconModal(); });
    // تحميل البيانات من Gist — load data from Gist
    await this.loadFromGist();
  },

  /* ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     AUTH — المصادقة
     ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  open() {
    document.getElementById('updatesAdminOverlay').classList.add('open');
    const tok = sessionStorage.getItem('_ua_tok');
    document.getElementById('ua-token-row').style.display = tok ? 'none' : '';
    if (tok) document.getElementById('ua-token-input').value = tok;
    document.getElementById('ua-password-input').focus();
  },

  close() {
    document.getElementById('updatesAdminOverlay').classList.remove('open');
    document.getElementById('ua-auth-screen').style.display   = '';
    document.getElementById('ua-editor-screen').classList.remove('open');
    document.getElementById('ua-auth-error').style.display    = 'none';
    document.getElementById('ua-password-input').value        = '';
    this.closeIconModal();
  },

  async verify() {
    const pwd = document.getElementById('ua-password-input').value;
    const tok = document.getElementById('ua-token-input').value.trim();
    if (!pwd) { document.getElementById('ua-password-input').focus(); return; }

    const hash = await this._sha256(pwd);
    if (hash !== UPDATES_CONFIG.ADMIN_HASH) {
      document.getElementById('ua-auth-error').style.display = 'block';
      document.getElementById('ua-password-input').value     = '';
      document.getElementById('ua-password-input').focus();
      return;
    }
    // حفظ التوكن في sessionStorage — Save token in sessionStorage ONLY
    if (tok) {
      sessionStorage.setItem('_ua_tok', tok);
      document.getElementById('ua-token-row').style.display = 'none';
    }
    document.getElementById('ua-auth-screen').style.display = 'none';
    document.getElementById('ua-editor-screen').classList.add('open');
    this.switchModule(this.activeModule);
  },

  /* ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     GIST I/O — التحميل والحفظ
     ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  async loadFromGist() {
    const syncStatus = document.getElementById('updates-sync-status');
    if (syncStatus) syncStatus.textContent = '⟳ syncing...';
    try {
      const res = await fetch(`https://api.github.com/gists/${UPDATES_CONFIG.GIST_ID}`, {
        headers: { 'Accept': 'application/vnd.github.v3+json' }
      });
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}`);
      const gist = await res.json();
      const file = gist.files[UPDATES_CONFIG.FILENAME];
      if (!file) throw new Error('File not found in Gist');

      const j = JSON.parse(file.content);

      // دمج البيانات مع الحماية من القيم المفقودة — Merge with fallback protection
      if (j.announcement) this.data.announcement = { ...this.data.announcement, ...j.announcement };
      if (j.featureFlags)  this.data.featureFlags = j.featureFlags;
      if (j.content)       this.data.content      = j.content;
      if (j.settings)      this.data.settings     = { ...this.data.settings,  ...j.settings };
      if (j.maintenance)   this.data.maintenance  = { ...this.data.maintenance, ...j.maintenance };
      if (j.quickLinks)    this.data.quickLinks   = j.quickLinks;
      if (j.notes !== undefined) this.data.notes  = j.notes;

      // توافق مع الصيغة القديمة — Backward compat with old format
      if (j.blocks && Array.isArray(j.blocks)) {
        this.data.changelog.blocks     = j.blocks;
        this.data.changelog.html       = j.html || '';
        this.data.changelog.lastUpdated = j.lastUpdated || '';
      } else if (j.changelog) {
        this.data.changelog = { ...this.data.changelog, ...j.changelog };
      }

      // تحديث عناصر الصفحة — Update page elements
      const container = document.getElementById('updates-content');
      if (container && this.data.changelog.html) container.innerHTML = this.data.changelog.html;
      if (syncStatus) {
        const lu = this.data.changelog.lastUpdated;
        syncStatus.textContent = lu ? `Updated ${new Date(lu).toLocaleDateString()}` : '';
      }

      // تطبيق الوحدات على الصفحة — Apply modules to the page
      this._injectAnnouncementBanner();
      this._applyFeatureFlags();
      this._applyContent();
      this._applyMaintenance();

    } catch (err) {
      if (syncStatus) syncStatus.textContent = '';
      console.warn('[AdminPanel] Gist load failed:', err.message);
    }
  },

  async saveToGist() {
    const tok = sessionStorage.getItem('_ua_tok');
    if (!tok) { this._toast('❌ No GitHub token found in this session'); return; }

    const btn = document.getElementById('ua-save-btn');
    const st  = document.getElementById('ua-save-status');
    btn.disabled  = true;
    btn.innerHTML = '<span class="ms">sync</span> Saving...';
    if (st) st.textContent = '';

    // توليد HTML نهائي للـ changelog — Generate final changelog HTML
    this.data.changelog.html       = this._generateHTML();
    this.data.changelog.lastUpdated = new Date().toISOString();

    // بناء كائن الحفظ (يحتفظ بالصيغة القديمة أيضاً) — Save object (backward compatible)
    const saveData = {
      ...this.data,
      html      : this.data.changelog.html,
      blocks    : this.data.changelog.blocks,
      lastUpdated: this.data.changelog.lastUpdated
    };

    try {
      const res = await fetch(`https://api.github.com/gists/${UPDATES_CONFIG.GIST_ID}`, {
        method : 'PATCH',
        headers: {
          'Authorization': `token ${tok}`,
          'Content-Type' : 'application/json',
          'Accept'       : 'application/vnd.github.v3+json'
        },
        body: JSON.stringify({ files: { [UPDATES_CONFIG.FILENAME]: { content: JSON.stringify(saveData, null, 2) } } })
      });
      if (!res.ok) {
        const e = await res.json().catch(() => ({}));
        throw new Error(e.message || `HTTP ${res.status}`);
      }
      this._toast('✅ Saved to Gist successfully!');
      if (st) st.textContent = `✓ ${new Date().toLocaleTimeString()}`;

      // تحديث الصفحة فوراً — Refresh page immediately
      const container = document.getElementById('updates-content');
      if (container) container.innerHTML = this.data.changelog.html;
      const ss = document.getElementById('updates-sync-status');
      if (ss) ss.textContent = 'Updated just now';
      this._injectAnnouncementBanner();
      this._applyFeatureFlags();
      this._applyContent();
      this._applyMaintenance();

    } catch (err) {
      this._toast(`❌ Save failed: ${err.message}`);
    } finally {
      btn.disabled  = false;
      btn.innerHTML = '<span class="ms">cloud_upload</span> Save to Gist';
    }
  },

  /* ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     MODULE NAVIGATION — التنقل بين الوحدات
     ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  switchModule(name) {
    this.activeModule = name;
    // تحديث أزرار الشريط الجانبي — Update sidebar buttons
    document.querySelectorAll('.ua-nav-btn').forEach(btn =>
      btn.classList.toggle('active', btn.dataset.module === name)
    );
    // إظهار/إخفاء الوحدات — Show/hide module panels
    document.querySelectorAll('.ua-module').forEach(panel =>
      panel.classList.toggle('active', panel.id === `ua-mod-${name}`)
    );
    // رسم الوحدة النشطة — Render active module
    const render = {
      announcement: () => this._renderAnnouncement(),
      changelog    : () => this._renderBlocks(),
      flags        : () => this._renderFlags(),
      content      : () => this._renderContent(),
      settings     : () => this._renderSettings(),
      maintenance  : () => this._renderMaintenance(),
      quicklinks   : () => this._renderQuickLinks(),
      notes        : () => this._renderNotes()
    };
    if (render[name]) render[name]();
  },

  /* ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     MODULE: ANNOUNCEMENT — وحدة شريط الإعلانات
     ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  _renderAnnouncement() {
    const inner = document.getElementById('ua-mod-announcement-inner');
    if (!inner) return;
    const a = this.data.announcement;
    const types = [
      { id:'info',    label:'Info',    color:'#a78bfa', icon:'campaign'      },
      { id:'success', label:'Success', color:'#34d399', icon:'check_circle'  },
      { id:'warning', label:'Warning', color:'#fbbf24', icon:'warning'       },
      { id:'danger',  label:'Danger',  color:'#f87171', icon:'error'         }
    ];

    inner.innerHTML = `
      <div class="ua-mod-header">
        <span class="ms" style="color:var(--ua-acc)">campaign</span>
        Announcement Banner
        <div class="ua-mod-badge" id="ann-status-badge"
          style="background:${a.active?'var(--ua-suc-bg)':'var(--ua-bg4)'};color:${a.active?'var(--ua-suc)':'var(--ua-t3)'}">
          ${a.active ? '● Active' : '○ Inactive'}
        </div>
      </div>

      <!-- Active toggle -->
      <div class="ua-field-row">
        <span class="ua-field-label">Status</span>
        <label class="ua-toggle">
          <input type="checkbox" id="ann-active" ${a.active ? 'checked' : ''}
            onchange="AdminPanel.data.announcement.active=this.checked;
                      AdminPanel._injectAnnouncementBanner();
                      AdminPanel._renderAnnouncement()">
          <span class="ua-toggle-track"></span>
          <span class="ua-toggle-label" id="ann-status-label">
            ${a.active ? 'Active — banner is visible to all visitors' : 'Inactive — banner is hidden'}
          </span>
        </label>
      </div>

      <!-- Type selector -->
      <div class="ua-field-row">
        <span class="ua-field-label">Type</span>
        <div style="display:flex;gap:6px;flex-wrap:wrap">
          ${types.map(t => `
            <label style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:5px;padding:5px 11px;
              border-radius:6px;cursor:pointer;
              border:1px solid ${a.type===t.id ? t.color : 'var(--ua-brd1)'};
              background:${a.type===t.id ? t.color+'18' : 'var(--ua-bg3)'}">
              <input type="radio" name="ann-type" value="${t.id}" ${a.type===t.id?'checked':''}
                style="display:none"
                onchange="AdminPanel.data.announcement.type='${t.id}';AdminPanel._renderAnnouncement();AdminPanel._injectAnnouncementBanner()">
              <span class="ms" style="font-size:14px;color:${t.color}">${t.icon}</span>
              <span style="font-size:11px;font-weight:700;color:${a.type===t.id ? t.color : 'var(--ua-t2)'}">${t.label}</span>
            </label>`).join('')}
        </div>
      </div>

      <!-- Message text -->
      <div class="ua-field-row">
        <span class="ua-field-label">Message</span>
        <textarea class="ua-textarea" id="ann-text" rows="2"
          placeholder="Enter announcement text... supports emoji 🎉🚀✨"
          oninput="AdminPanel.data.announcement.text=this.value;AdminPanel._updateAnnPreview();AdminPanel._injectAnnouncementBanner()"
        >${this._esc(a.text)}</textarea>
        <span style="font-size:.67rem;color:var(--ua-t3)">
          <span class="ms" style="font-size:11px">info</span>
          Empty message hides the banner automatically. Long text scrolls as a ticker.
        </span>
      </div>

      <!-- Live preview -->
      <div class="ua-field-row">
        <span class="ua-field-label">Preview</span>
        <div id="ann-preview" style="border-radius:8px;overflow:hidden;border:1px solid var(--ua-brd1)">
          ${this._annBannerHTML(a.type, a.text, true)}
        </div>
      </div>

      <!-- Instructions -->
      <div class="ua-info-box" style="font-size:.72rem">
        <strong>To show the banner:</strong> Add
        <code>&lt;div id="ap-announcement-bar" style="display:none"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;</code>
        at the very top of your page body (CHANGE 1A). The banner appears automatically when Active.
      </div>`;
  },

  _updateAnnPreview() {
    const p = document.getElementById('ann-preview');
    if (p) p.innerHTML = this._annBannerHTML(
      this.data.announcement.type, this.data.announcement.text, true
    );
  },

  // توليد HTML الشريط — Generate banner HTML
  _annBannerHTML(type, text, isPreview = false) {
    const cfgMap = {
      info    : { bg:'rgba(139,92,246,.12)',  border:'rgba(139,92,246,.3)',  color:'#a78bfa', icon:'campaign'      },
      success : { bg:'rgba(52,211,153,.12)',   border:'rgba(52,211,153,.3)',  color:'#34d399', icon:'check_circle'  },
      warning : { bg:'rgba(251,191,36,.12)',   border:'rgba(251,191,36,.3)',  color:'#fbbf24', icon:'warning'       },
      danger  : { bg:'rgba(248,113,113,.12)',  border:'rgba(248,113,113,.3)', color:'#f87171', icon:'error'         }
    };
    const c    = cfgMap[type] || cfgMap.info;
    const msg  = text || (isPreview ? 'Your announcement message will appear here...' : '');
    const long = msg.length > 55;
    const tColor = isPreview ? 'var(--ua-t1)' : 'var(--txt1)';

    return `
      <div style="background:${c.bg};border-bottom:1px solid ${c.border};
        padding:9px 14px;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;">
        <span class="ms" style="font-size:17px;color:${c.color};flex-shrink:0">${c.icon}</span>
        <div class="ap-ticker-wrap" style="flex:1;min-width:0">
          <span class="ap-ticker-track ${long && !isPreview ? '' : 'static'}"
            style="font-size:13px;font-weight:500;color:${tColor};line-height:1.4">
            ${long && !isPreview
              ? `${this._he(msg)}&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;${this._he(msg)}`
              : this._he(msg)}
          </span>
        </div>
        ${!isPreview
          ? `<button onclick="AdminPanel._dismissBanner()"
              style="background:none;border:none;cursor:pointer;color:${c.color};
                     padding:2px;display:flex;align-items:center;flex-shrink:0;
                     opacity:.7;transition:opacity .15s"
              onmouseenter="this.style.opacity='1'" onmouseleave="this.style.opacity='.7'">
              <span class="ms" style="font-size:17px">close</span>
            </button>`
          : ''}
      </div>`;
  },

  // حقن الشريط في الصفحة — Inject banner into page
  _injectAnnouncementBanner() {
    const bar = document.getElementById('ap-announcement-bar');
    if (!bar) return;
    const a = this.data.announcement;
    if (!a.active || !a.text.trim()) { bar.style.display = 'none'; return; }

    // مفتاح الإخفاء يعتمد على النص — Dismiss key based on message content
    const dk = '_ap_ann_' + btoa(unescape(encodeURIComponent(a.text.slice(0, 40)))).slice(0, 20);
    if (sessionStorage.getItem(dk)) { bar.style.display = 'none'; return; }

    bar.innerHTML       = this._annBannerHTML(a.type, a.text);
    bar.style.display   = 'block';
    bar.dataset.dismissKey = dk;
  },

  _dismissBanner() {
    const bar = document.getElementById('ap-announcement-bar');
    if (!bar) return;
    if (bar.dataset.dismissKey) sessionStorage.setItem(bar.dataset.dismissKey, '1');
    bar.style.animation = 'none';
    bar.style.opacity   = '0';
    bar.style.transform = 'translateY(-100%)';
    bar.style.transition = 'opacity .25s, transform .25s';
    setTimeout(() => { bar.style.display = 'none'; }, 260);
  },

  /* ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     MODULE: CHANGELOG — وحدة التحديثات (الموجودة سابقاً)
     ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

  // رسم قائمة الكتل — Render blocks list
  _renderBlocks() {
    const area  = document.getElementById('ue-blocks-area');
    const count = document.getElementById('ua-block-count');
    if (!area) return;

    const blocks = this.data.changelog.blocks;
    if (count) count.textContent = `${blocks.length} block${blocks.length !== 1 ? 's' : ''}`;

    if (blocks.length === 0) {
      area.innerHTML = `<div style="text-align:center;padding:30px;color:var(--ua-t3);font-size:.8rem">
        <span class="ms" style="display:block;font-size:28px;opacity:.3;margin-bottom:8px">layers</span>
        Add blocks from the toolbar above</div>`;
      this._renderPreview(); return;
    }

    area.innerHTML = blocks.map((b, idx) => this._blockHTML(b, idx)).join('');
    this._renderPreview();
  },

  // HTML لكتلة واحدة — HTML for a single block
  _blockHTML(b, idx) {
    const blocks   = this.data.changelog.blocks;
    const isFirst  = idx === 0;
    const isLast   = idx === blocks.length - 1;
    const collapsed = this.collapsedBlocks.has(b.id);

    const LABELS = { 'update-card':'Update','section-header':'Section','feature-item':'Feature',
                     'fix-item':'Fix','footer-note':'Footer','divider':'Divider' };
    const BCOLORS = { 'update-card':'#6c8fff','section-header':'#585b70','feature-item':'#3ecf8e',
                      'fix-item':'#f59e0b','footer-note':'#585b70','divider':'#585b70' };
    const barTitle = b.type === 'update-card' ? `${b.version} — ${b.title}` : (b.text || b.title || '─');

    const IS = 'padding:3px 6px;font-size:11px;background:var(--ua-bg1);border:1px solid var(--ua-brd2);border-radius:4px;color:var(--ua-t1);font-family:inherit;outline:none';
    const LBL = 'font-size:9px;color:var(--ua-t3);font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;white-space:nowrap;flex-shrink:0';
    const ROW = 'display:flex;align-items:center;gap:5px;margin-bottom:4px;flex-wrap:nowrap';
    const TA  = `${IS};resize:vertical;min-height:36px;line-height:1.4;flex:1`;

    // زر الأيقونة — Icon button
    const iconBtn = (bid, ico) =>
      `<div id="ua-iprev-${bid}" onclick="AdminPanel.openIconModal('${bid}','icon')" title="Click to change icon"
        style="width:26px;height:26px;background:var(--ua-bg3);border:1px solid var(--ua-brd2);border-radius:4px;
               display:inline-flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;cursor:pointer;flex-shrink:0"
        onmouseenter="this.style.borderColor='var(--ua-acc)'" onmouseleave="this.style.borderColor='var(--ua-brd2)'">
        <span class="ms" style="font-size:16px;color:var(--ua-acc)">${ico}</span>
      </div>
      <input id="ua-iinp-${bid}" value="${this._esc(ico)}" placeholder="icon_name" style="${IS};width:88px;flex-shrink:0"
        oninput="AdminPanel.updateBlock('${bid}','icon',this.value);
                 const p=document.getElementById('ua-iprev-${bid}');
                 if(p) p.querySelector('.ms').textContent=this.value">`;

    // نقاط الألوان — Color dots
    const colorDots = (bid, sel) =>
      ['blue','green','amber','red','gray'].map(c =>
        `<div onclick="AdminPanel.updateBlock('${bid}','color','${c}');AdminPanel._renderBlocks()" title="${c}"
          style="width:13px;height:13px;border-radius:50%;background:${UA_COLORS[c]};cursor:pointer;flex-shrink:0;
                 border:2px solid ${sel===c?'#fff':'transparent'};transition:transform .1s"
          onmouseenter="this.style.transform='scale(1.3)'" onmouseleave="this.style.transform='scale(1)'">
        </div>`).join('');

    let body = '';
    if (b.type === 'update-card') {
      body = `
        <div style="${ROW}">
          <span style="${LBL}">Icon</span>${iconBtn(b.id, b.icon)}
          <span style="${LBL};margin-left:4px">Version</span>
          <input value="${this._esc(b.version)}" placeholder="v3.2" style="${IS};width:52px;flex-shrink:0"
            oninput="AdminPanel.updateBlock('${b.id}','version',this.value)">
          <span style="${LBL}">Title</span>
          <input value="${this._esc(b.title)}" placeholder="What's New" style="${IS};flex:1;min-width:0"
            oninput="AdminPanel.updateBlock('${b.id}','title',this.value)">
        </div>
        <div style="${ROW};align-items:flex-start">
          <span style="${LBL};padding-top:4px">Desc</span>
          <textarea placeholder="Description..." style="${TA}"
            oninput="AdminPanel.updateBlock('${b.id}','description',this.value)">${this._esc(b.description)}</textarea>
        </div>`;
    } else if (b.type === 'section-header') {
      body = `<div style="${ROW}">
        <span style="${LBL}">Icon</span>${iconBtn(b.id, b.icon)}
        <span style="${LBL};margin-left:4px">Text</span>
        <input value="${this._esc(b.text)}" placeholder="Section heading" style="${IS};flex:1;min-width:0"
          oninput="AdminPanel.updateBlock('${b.id}','text',this.value)">
      </div>`;
    } else if (b.type === 'feature-item') {
      body = `
        <div style="${ROW}">
          <span style="${LBL}">Icon</span>${iconBtn(b.id, b.icon)}
          <span style="${LBL};margin-left:4px">Title</span>
          <input value="${this._esc(b.title)}" placeholder="Feature title" style="${IS};flex:1;min-width:0"
            oninput="AdminPanel.updateBlock('${b.id}','title',this.value)">
          <span style="${LBL}">Color</span>${colorDots(b.id, b.color)}
        </div>
        <div style="${ROW};align-items:flex-start">
          <span style="${LBL};padding-top:4px">Desc</span>
          <textarea placeholder="Description..." style="${TA}"
            oninput="AdminPanel.updateBlock('${b.id}','description',this.value)">${this._esc(b.description)}</textarea>
        </div>`;
    } else if (b.type === 'fix-item') {
      body = `<div style="${ROW}">
        <span style="${LBL}">Text</span>
        <input value="${this._esc(b.text)}" placeholder="Fix or improvement" style="${IS};flex:1;min-width:0"
          oninput="AdminPanel.updateBlock('${b.id}','text',this.value)">
      </div>`;
    } else if (b.type === 'footer-note') {
      body = `<div style="${ROW}">
        <span style="${LBL}">Icon</span>${iconBtn(b.id, b.icon)}
        <span style="${LBL};margin-left:4px">Text</span>
        <input value="${this._esc(b.text)}" placeholder="Footer text" style="${IS};flex:1;min-width:0"
          oninput="AdminPanel.updateBlock('${b.id}','text',this.value)">
      </div>`;
    } else if (b.type === 'divider') {
      body = `<div style="text-align:center;color:var(--ua-t3);font-size:.7rem;padding:2px">──── horizontal divider ────</div>`;
    }

    const NAV = (ico, fn, title, danger = false) =>
      `<button onclick="${fn}" title="${title}"
        style="background:transparent;border:none;cursor:pointer;color:var(--ua-t3);width:20px;height:20px;padding:0;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;border-radius:3px"
        onmouseenter="this.style.color='${danger ? 'var(--ua-err)' : 'var(--ua-t1)'}'" onmouseleave="this.style.color='var(--ua-t3)'">
        <span class="ms" style="font-size:14px">${ico}</span>
      </button>`;

    return `
      <div class="ue-block${collapsed ? ' ue-collapsed' : ''}" data-bid="${b.id}" style="margin-bottom:3px">
        <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:5px;padding:5px 7px;background:var(--ua-bg4);cursor:pointer;user-select:none"
          onclick="AdminPanel.toggleCollapse('${b.id}')">
          <span class="ms" style="font-size:13px;color:var(--ua-t3);flex-shrink:0">${collapsed ? 'chevron_right' : 'expand_more'}</span>
          <span style="font-size:9px;font-weight:700;padding:1px 5px;border-radius:8px;text-transform:uppercase;background:rgba(255,255,255,.06);color:${BCOLORS[b.type]};flex-shrink:0">${LABELS[b.type]}</span>
          <span style="flex:1;font-size:11px;color:var(--ua-t2);overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;white-space:nowrap">${this._esc(barTitle)}</span>
          <div style="display:flex;gap:1px;flex-shrink:0" onclick="event.stopPropagation()">
            ${!isFirst ? NAV('arrow_upward',  `AdminPanel.moveBlock('${b.id}',-1)`, 'Move up') : ''}
            ${!isLast  ? NAV('arrow_downward', `AdminPanel.moveBlock('${b.id}',1)`,  'Move down') : ''}
            ${NAV('delete', `AdminPanel.removeBlock('${b.id}')`, 'Delete', true)}
          </div>
        </div>
        <div class="ue-block-body" style="padding:6px 8px 5px">${body}</div>
      </div>`;
  },

  // رسم المعاينة الحية (قابلة للتحرير) — Render live editable preview
  _renderPreview() {
    const area = document.getElementById('ue-preview-area');
    if (!area) return;
    const blocks = this.data.changelog.blocks;
    if (blocks.length === 0) {
      area.innerHTML = `<div style="text-align:center;padding:30px;color:var(--ua-t3);font-size:.8rem">
        <span class="ms" style="display:block;font-size:28px;opacity:.3;margin-bottom:8px">auto_awesome</span>
        Preview appears here</div>`;
      return;
    }
    const CE = `outline:none;border-bottom:1px dashed var(--ua-acc);cursor:text;display:inline`;
    const ce = (bid, field, val) =>
      `<span style="${CE}" contenteditable="true"
        onblur="AdminPanel._updateFromPreview('${bid}','${field}',this.innerText)">${this._esc(val)}</span>`;

    let html = '';
    let i = 0;
    while (i < blocks.length) {
      const b = blocks[i];
      if (b.type === 'update-card') {
        html += `<div style="background:var(--acc3);padding:10px;border-radius:6px;margin-bottom:10px;border-left:3px solid var(--acc2)">
          <strong style="color:var(--acc2);font-size:12px;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:4px;flex-wrap:wrap">
            <span class="ms" style="font-size:14px">${b.icon}</span>
            ${ce(b.id,'version',b.version)} — ${ce(b.id,'title',b.title)}
          </strong>
          <p style="margin:4px 0 0;font-size:11px;color:var(--txt2);line-height:1.4">${ce(b.id,'description',b.description)}</p>
        </div>`; i++;
      } else if (b.type === 'section-header') {
        html += `<h3 style="font-size:12px;color:var(--acc2);margin:0 0 4px;padding-bottom:4px;border-bottom:1px solid var(--brd1);font-weight:600;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:4px">
          <span class="ms" style="font-size:14px">${b.icon}</span>${ce(b.id,'text',b.text)}</h3>`; i++;
        const fis = [];
        while (i < blocks.length && blocks[i].type === 'feature-item') { fis.push(blocks[i]); i++; }
        if (fis.length) {
          html += `<div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:4px;margin-bottom:10px">`;
          fis.forEach(fi => {
            const bc = UA_COLORS[fi.color] || UA_COLORS.blue;
            html += `<div style="padding:6px 8px;background:var(--bg3);border-radius:4px;border-left:2px solid ${bc}">
              <strong style="font-size:11px;color:var(--txt1);display:block;margin-bottom:2px">
                <span class="ms" style="font-size:12px">${fi.icon}</span>${ce(fi.id,'title',fi.title)}
              </strong>
              <span style="font-size:10px;color:var(--txt2);line-height:1.3;display:block">${ce(fi.id,'description',fi.description)}</span>
            </div>`;
          });
          html += `</div>`;
        }
      } else if (b.type === 'feature-item') {
        const bc = UA_COLORS[b.color] || UA_COLORS.blue;
        html += `<div style="padding:6px 8px;background:var(--bg3);border-radius:4px;border-left:2px solid ${bc};margin-bottom:4px">
          <strong style="font-size:11px;color:var(--txt1);display:block;margin-bottom:2px">
            <span class="ms" style="font-size:12px">${b.icon}</span>${ce(b.id,'title',b.title)}
          </strong>
          <span style="font-size:10px;color:var(--txt2);line-height:1.3;display:block">${ce(b.id,'description',b.description)}</span>
        </div>`; i++;
      } else if (b.type === 'fix-item') {
        const fixes = [];
        while (i < blocks.length && blocks[i].type === 'fix-item') { fixes.push(blocks[i]); i++; }
        html += `<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--txt2);line-height:1.9;padding-left:4px">`;
        fixes.forEach(fi => { html += `<div><span style="color:var(--suc1)">✓</span> ${ce(fi.id,'text',fi.text)}</div>`; });
        html += `</div>`;
      } else if (b.type === 'footer-note') {
        html += `<div style="margin-top:10px;padding:6px 8px;background:var(--bg3);border-radius:4px;font-size:10px;color:var(--txt3);display:flex;align-items:center;gap:4px">
          <span class="ms" style="font-size:12px">${b.icon}</span>${ce(b.id,'text',b.text)}</div>`; i++;
      } else if (b.type === 'divider') {
        html += `<hr style="border:none;border-top:1px solid var(--brd1);margin:10px 0">`; i++;
      } else { i++; }
    }
    area.innerHTML = html;
  },

  _updateFromPreview(id, key, value) {
    const b = this.data.changelog.blocks.find(b => b.id === id);
    if (b && b[key] !== value) { b[key] = value; this._renderBlocks(); }
  },

  // توليد HTML النهائي للـ Gist — Generate final HTML for Gist storage
  _generateHTML() {
    const parts = [];
    const blocks = this.data.changelog.blocks;
    let i = 0;
    while (i < blocks.length) {
      const b = blocks[i];
      if (b.type === 'update-card') {
        parts.push(`<div style="background:var(--acc3);padding:10px;border-radius:6px;margin-bottom:10px;border-left:3px solid var(--acc2)"><strong style="color:var(--acc2);font-size:12px"><span class="ms">${b.icon}</span> ${this._he(b.version)} — ${this._he(b.title)}</strong><p style="margin:4px 0 0;font-size:11px;color:var(--txt2);line-height:1.4">${this._he(b.description)}</p></div>`); i++;
      } else if (b.type === 'section-header') {
        parts.push(`<h3 style="font-size:12px;color:var(--acc2);margin:0 0 6px;padding-bottom:4px;border-bottom:1px solid var(--brd1);font-weight:600"><span class="ms">${b.icon}</span> ${this._he(b.text)}</h3>`); i++;
        const fis = [];
        while (i < blocks.length && blocks[i].type === 'feature-item') { fis.push(blocks[i]); i++; }
        if (fis.length) {
          const items = fis.map(fi => { const bc = UA_COLORS[fi.color]||UA_COLORS.blue; return `  <div style="padding:6px 8px;background:var(--bg3);border-radius:4px;border-left:2px solid ${bc}"><strong style="font-size:11px;color:var(--txt1);display:block;margin-bottom:2px"><span class="ms" style="font-size:12px">${fi.icon}</span> ${this._he(fi.title)}</strong><span style="font-size:10px;color:var(--txt2);line-height:1.3">${this._he(fi.description)}</span></div>`; }).join('\n');
          parts.push(`<div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:4px;margin-bottom:10px">\n${items}\n</div>`);
        }
      } else if (b.type === 'feature-item') {
        const bc = UA_COLORS[b.color]||UA_COLORS.blue;
        parts.push(`<div style="padding:6px 8px;background:var(--bg3);border-radius:4px;border-left:2px solid ${bc};margin-bottom:4px"><strong style="font-size:11px;color:var(--txt1);display:block;margin-bottom:2px"><span class="ms" style="font-size:12px">${b.icon}</span> ${this._he(b.title)}</strong><span style="font-size:10px;color:var(--txt2);line-height:1.3">${this._he(b.description)}</span></div>`); i++;
      } else if (b.type === 'fix-item') {
        const fixes = [];
        while (i < blocks.length && blocks[i].type === 'fix-item') { fixes.push(blocks[i]); i++; }
        parts.push(`<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--txt2);line-height:1.6;padding-left:4px">\n${fixes.map(fi=>`  <div><span style="color:var(--suc1)">✓</span> ${this._he(fi.text)}</div>`).join('\n')}\n</div>`);
      } else if (b.type === 'footer-note') {
        parts.push(`<div style="margin-top:10px;padding:6px 8px;background:var(--bg3);border-radius:4px;font-size:10px;color:var(--txt3);display:flex;align-items:center;gap:4px"><span class="ms" style="font-size:12px">${b.icon}</span>${this._he(b.text)}</div>`); i++;
      } else if (b.type === 'divider') {
        parts.push(`<hr style="border:none;border-top:1px solid var(--brd1);margin:10px 0">`); i++;
      } else { i++; }
    }
    return parts.join('\n\n');
  },

  // عمليات الكتل — Block operations
  addBlock(type) {
    const b = { ...this._blockDefaults(type), id: this._uid() };
    this.data.changelog.blocks.push(b);
    this._renderBlocks();
    setTimeout(() => { const a = document.getElementById('ue-blocks-area'); if (a) a.scrollTop = a.scrollHeight; }, 60);
  },
  removeBlock(id) {
    this.data.changelog.blocks = this.data.changelog.blocks.filter(b => b.id !== id);
    this.collapsedBlocks.delete(id);
    this._renderBlocks();
  },
  moveBlock(id, dir) {
    const arr = this.data.changelog.blocks;
    const i = arr.findIndex(b => b.id === id);
    const ni = i + dir;
    if (i < 0 || ni < 0 || ni >= arr.length) return;
    [arr[i], arr[ni]] = [arr[ni], arr[i]];
    this._renderBlocks();
  },
  updateBlock(id, key, value) {
    const b = this.data.changelog.blocks.find(b => b.id === id);
    if (b) { b[key] = value; this._renderPreview(); }
  },
  toggleCollapse(id) {
    if (this.collapsedBlocks.has(id)) this.collapsedBlocks.delete(id);
    else this.collapsedBlocks.add(id);
    this._renderBlocks();
  },
  _blockDefaults(type) {
    const m = {
      'update-card'   : { type, id:'', icon:'new_releases', version:'v3.2', title:"What's New", description:'Latest improvements in Story Writer Pro.' },
      'section-header': { type, id:'', icon:'star', text:'New Features' },
      'feature-item'  : { type, id:'', icon:'auto_awesome', title:'Feature Name', description:'Feature description here...', color:'blue' },
      'fix-item'      : { type, id:'', text:'Bug fix or improvement' },
      'footer-note'   : { type, id:'', icon:'schedule', text:`Last updated: ${new Date().toLocaleDateString('en',{year:'numeric',month:'long'})}` },
      'divider'       : { type, id:'' }
    };
    return m[type] || { type, id:'' };
  },

  /* ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     MODULE: FEATURE FLAGS — وحدة الخصائص القابلة للتبديل
     ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  _renderFlags() {
    const inner = document.getElementById('ua-mod-flags-inner');
    if (!inner) return;
    const flags = this.data.featureFlags;
    const keys  = Object.keys(flags);

    inner.innerHTML = `
      <div class="ua-mod-header">
        <span class="ms" style="color:var(--ua-acc)">flag</span>
        Feature Flags
        <div class="ua-mod-badge">${keys.length} flag${keys.length!==1?'s':''}</div>
      </div>

      <div class="ua-info-box">
        Toggle features on/off without changing code. Elements with
        <code>data-ap="feature:flagName"</code> show/hide based on flag state.
        Changes are applied to the page immediately and saved on next Save.
      </div>

      <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:4px">
        ${keys.length === 0
          ? `<div style="text-align:center;padding:24px;color:var(--ua-t3);font-size:.8rem;background:var(--ua-bg3);border-radius:8px;border:1px dashed var(--ua-brd1)">
              <span class="ms" style="display:block;font-size:24px;opacity:.4;margin-bottom:6px">flag</span>
              No flags yet. Add one below.
             </div>`
          : keys.map(k => `
            <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;padding:9px 12px;background:var(--ua-bg3);border:1px solid var(--ua-brd1);border-radius:8px">
              <label class="ua-toggle-sm">
                <input type="checkbox" ${flags[k]?'checked':''}
                  onchange="AdminPanel.data.featureFlags['${k}']=this.checked;AdminPanel._applyFeatureFlags();AdminPanel._renderFlags()">
                <span class="ua-toggle-track-sm"></span>
              </label>
              <code style="flex:1;font-size:12px;color:var(--ua-acc-l);background:var(--ua-bg1);padding:2px 8px;border-radius:5px;font-family:monospace">${k}</code>
              <span style="font-size:11px;font-weight:700;min-width:28px;text-align:right;color:${flags[k]?'var(--ua-suc)':'var(--ua-t3)'}">${flags[k]?'ON':'OFF'}</span>
              <button onclick="AdminPanel.removeFlag('${k}')"
                style="background:none;border:none;cursor:pointer;color:var(--ua-t3);display:flex;align-items:center;padding:2px"
                onmouseenter="this.style.color='var(--ua-err)'" onmouseleave="this.style.color='var(--ua-t3)'">
                <span class="ms" style="font-size:16px">delete</span>
              </button>
            </div>`).join('')
        }
      </div>

      <!-- Add new flag -->
      <div style="display:flex;gap:6px;align-items:center;padding:10px 12px;background:var(--ua-bg3);border:1px dashed var(--ua-brd2);border-radius:8px">
        <span class="ms" style="color:var(--ua-t3);font-size:18px">add_circle</span>
        <input id="new-flag-key" placeholder="flagName (camelCase, no spaces)"
          class="ua-input" style="flex:1;font-family:monospace"
          onkeydown="if(event.key==='Enter') AdminPanel.addFlag()">
        <button onclick="AdminPanel.addFlag()" class="ua-btn ua-btn-primary">Add Flag</button>
      </div>`;
  },

  addFlag() {
    const inp = document.getElementById('new-flag-key');
    const k   = (inp?.value || '').trim().replace(/\s+/g, '');
    if (!k) return;
    if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(this.data.featureFlags, k)) {
      this._toast('⚠️ Flag already exists'); return;
    }
    this.data.featureFlags[k] = false;
    if (inp) inp.value = '';
    this._renderFlags();
    this._applyFeatureFlags();
  },
  removeFlag(key) {
    delete this.data.featureFlags[key];
    this._renderFlags();
    this._applyFeatureFlags();
  },
  _applyFeatureFlags() {
    document.querySelectorAll('[data-ap^="feature:"]').forEach(el => {
      const flag = el.getAttribute('data-ap').replace('feature:', '');
      el.style.display = this.data.featureFlags[flag] ? '' : 'none';
    });
  },

  /* ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     MODULE: CONTENT MANAGER — وحدة إدارة النصوص
     ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  _renderContent() {
    const inner = document.getElementById('ua-mod-content-inner');
    if (!inner) return;
    const ct   = this.data.content;
    const keys = Object.keys(ct);

    inner.innerHTML = `
      <div class="ua-mod-header">
        <span class="ms" style="color:var(--ua-acc)">edit_note</span>
        Content Manager
        <div class="ua-mod-badge">${keys.length} field${keys.length!==1?'s':''}</div>
      </div>

      <div class="ua-info-box">
        Edit any text on your page without touching code. Add
        <code>data-ap="content:key"</code> to any HTML element
        and its content will be replaced with the value you set here.
      </div>

      <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:6px">
        ${keys.length === 0
          ? `<div style="text-align:center;padding:24px;color:var(--ua-t3);font-size:.8rem;background:var(--ua-bg3);border-radius:8px;border:1px dashed var(--ua-brd1)">
              <span class="ms" style="display:block;font-size:24px;opacity:.4;margin-bottom:6px">edit_note</span>
              No content keys yet. Add one below.
             </div>`
          : keys.map(k => `
            <div style="background:var(--ua-bg3);border:1px solid var(--ua-brd1);border-radius:8px;padding:10px 12px">
              <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px;margin-bottom:6px">
                <code style="font-size:11px;color:var(--ua-acc-l);background:var(--ua-bg1);padding:2px 8px;border-radius:5px;font-family:monospace;flex:1">${k}</code>
                <button onclick="AdminPanel.removeContent('${k}')"
                  style="background:none;border:none;cursor:pointer;color:var(--ua-t3);display:flex;align-items:center"
                  onmouseenter="this.style.color='var(--ua-err)'" onmouseleave="this.style.color='var(--ua-t3)'">
                  <span class="ms" style="font-size:16px">delete</span>
                </button>
              </div>
              <textarea class="ua-textarea" rows="2"
                style="min-height:36px"
                oninput="AdminPanel.data.content['${k}']=this.value;AdminPanel._applyContent()"
              >${this._esc(ct[k])}</textarea>
            </div>`).join('')
        }
      </div>

      <!-- Add new key -->
      <div style="display:flex;gap:6px;align-items:center;padding:10px 12px;background:var(--ua-bg3);border:1px dashed var(--ua-brd2);border-radius:8px">
        <span class="ms" style="color:var(--ua-t3);font-size:18px">add_circle</span>
        <input id="new-content-key" placeholder="content-key (kebab-case)"
          class="ua-input" style="flex:1;font-family:monospace"
          onkeydown="if(event.key==='Enter') AdminPanel.addContent()">
        <button onclick="AdminPanel.addContent()" class="ua-btn ua-btn-primary">Add Key</button>
      </div>`;
  },

  addContent() {
    const inp = document.getElementById('new-content-key');
    const k   = (inp?.value || '').trim().replace(/\s+/g, '-');
    if (!k) return;
    if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(this.data.content, k)) {
      this._toast('⚠️ Key already exists'); return;
    }
    this.data.content[k] = '';
    if (inp) inp.value = '';
    this._renderContent();
  },
  removeContent(key) {
    delete this.data.content[key];
    this._renderContent();
    this._applyContent();
  },
  _applyContent() {
    document.querySelectorAll('[data-ap^="content:"]').forEach(el => {
      const key = el.getAttribute('data-ap').replace('content:', '');
      if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(this.data.content, key)) {
        el.textContent = this.data.content[key];
      }
    });
  },

  /* ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     MODULE: SETTINGS — وحدة إعدادات التطبيق
     ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  _renderSettings() {
    const inner = document.getElementById('ua-mod-settings-inner');
    if (!inner) return;
    const s = this.data.settings;
    const statuses = [
      { id:'online',      color:'var(--ua-suc)', label:'Online',      icon:'check_circle' },
      { id:'beta',        color:'var(--ua-wrn)', label:'Beta',        icon:'science' },
      { id:'maintenance', color:'var(--ua-err)', label:'Maintenance', icon:'build' }
    ];

    inner.innerHTML = `
      <div class="ua-mod-header">
        <span class="ms" style="color:var(--ua-acc)">settings</span>
        App Settings
      </div>

      <!-- App Name -->
      <div class="ua-field-row">
        <span class="ua-field-label">App Name</span>
        <input class="ua-input" value="${this._esc(s.appName)}" placeholder="Story Writer Pro"
          oninput="AdminPanel.data.settings.appName=this.value">
      </div>

      <!-- Version -->
      <div class="ua-field-row">
        <span class="ua-field-label">Current Version</span>
        <div style="display:flex;gap:8px;align-items:center">
          <input class="ua-input" value="${this._esc(s.version)}" placeholder="v3.2"
            style="width:100px;font-family:monospace"
            oninput="AdminPanel.data.settings.version=this.value">
          <span style="font-size:.75rem;color:var(--ua-t3)">
            Displayed in <code style="background:var(--ua-bg3);padding:1px 5px;border-radius:3px;font-family:monospace;font-size:10px;color:var(--ua-acc-l)">data-ap="version"</code> elements
          </span>
        </div>
      </div>

      <!-- App Status -->
      <div class="ua-field-row">
        <span class="ua-field-label">App Status</span>
        <div style="display:flex;gap:6px;flex-wrap:wrap">
          ${statuses.map(st => `
            <label style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px;padding:7px 14px;border-radius:8px;cursor:pointer;
              border:1px solid ${s.status===st.id ? st.color : 'var(--ua-brd1)'};
              background:${s.status===st.id ? st.color+'18' : 'var(--ua-bg3)'}">
              <input type="radio" name="app-status" value="${st.id}" ${s.status===st.id?'checked':''} style="display:none"
                onchange="AdminPanel.data.settings.status='${st.id}';AdminPanel._renderSettings()">
              <span class="ms" style="font-size:15px;color:${st.color}">${st.icon}</span>
              <span style="font-size:12px;font-weight:700;color:${s.status===st.id ? st.color : 'var(--ua-t2)'}">${st.label}</span>
            </label>`).join('')}
        </div>
      </div>

      <!-- Security section -->
      <div class="ua-danger-zone">
        <div class="ua-danger-title"><span class="ms" style="font-size:14px">security</span> Security</div>
        <p style="font-size:.75rem;color:var(--ua-t2);line-height:1.5;margin-bottom:10px">
          Your GitHub token is stored in <code style="background:var(--ua-bg3);padding:1px 5px;border-radius:3px;font-family:monospace;font-size:10px">sessionStorage</code>
          — automatically cleared when this tab closes. It is never stored in the page code.
        </p>
        <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;flex-wrap:wrap">
          <button onclick="sessionStorage.removeItem('_ua_tok');AdminPanel._toast('✅ Token cleared');AdminPanel._renderSettings()"
            class="ua-btn ua-btn-danger">
            <span class="ms" style="font-size:14px">key_off</span>
            Clear Token Now
          </button>
          <span style="font-size:.72rem;color:var(--ua-t3)">
            ${sessionStorage.getItem('_ua_tok') ? '🔑 Token active in this session' : '○ No token stored'}
          </span>
        </div>
      </div>`;
  },

  /* ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     MODULE: MAINTENANCE — وحدة وضع الصيانة
     ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  _renderMaintenance() {
    const inner = document.getElementById('ua-mod-maintenance-inner');
    if (!inner) return;
    const m = this.data.maintenance;

    inner.innerHTML = `
      <div class="ua-mod-header">
        <span class="ms" style="color:var(--ua-acc)">build</span>
        Maintenance Mode
        <div class="ua-mod-badge"
          style="background:${m.active?'var(--ua-err-bg)':'var(--ua-bg4)'};color:${m.active?'var(--ua-err)':'var(--ua-t3)'}">
          ${m.active ? '⚠ Active' : '○ Off'}
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="ua-info-box" style="${m.active?'background:var(--ua-err-bg);border-color:rgba(248,113,113,.3)':''}">
        ${m.active
          ? '<strong style="color:var(--ua-err)">⚠ Maintenance mode is ON.</strong> Visitors are seeing the maintenance overlay.'
          : 'When active, a maintenance overlay covers your app. Visitors see your custom message instead of the generator.'}
      </div>

      <!-- Toggle -->
      <div class="ua-field-row">
        <span class="ua-field-label">Status</span>
        <label class="ua-toggle">
          <input type="checkbox" ${m.active?'checked':''}
            onchange="AdminPanel.data.maintenance.active=this.checked;
                      AdminPanel._applyMaintenance();AdminPanel._renderMaintenance()">
          <span class="ua-toggle-track"></span>
          <span class="ua-toggle-label">${m.active ? '⚠ Maintenance mode is ON' : 'Maintenance mode is off'}</span>
        </label>
      </div>

      <!-- Message -->
      <div class="ua-field-row">
        <span class="ua-field-label">Visitor Message</span>
        <textarea class="ua-textarea" rows="3"
          placeholder="We'll be back shortly. Thank you for your patience!"
          oninput="AdminPanel.data.maintenance.message=this.value;AdminPanel._applyMaintenance()"
        >${this._esc(m.message)}</textarea>
      </div>

      <!-- Preview -->
      <div class="ua-field-row">
        <span class="ua-field-label">Overlay Preview</span>
        <div style="border-radius:8px;overflow:hidden;border:1px solid var(--ua-brd1);background:rgba(0,0,0,.7);padding:24px;text-align:center">
          <span class="ms" style="font-size:28px;color:#fbbf24;display:block;margin-bottom:8px">build</span>
          <p style="color:#f0f0f0;font-size:14px;font-weight:600;margin-bottom:6px">Under Maintenance</p>
          <p style="color:#aaa;font-size:12px">${this._he(m.message || 'We\'ll be back shortly.')}</p>
        </div>
      </div>`;
  },

  _applyMaintenance() {
    const m = this.data.maintenance;
    let overlay = document.getElementById('ap-maintenance-overlay');
    if (m.active) {
      if (!overlay) {
        overlay = document.createElement('div');
        overlay.id = 'ap-maintenance-overlay';
        overlay.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;inset:0;background:rgba(10,12,14,.95);z-index:1999;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;flex-direction:column;gap:12px';
        document.body.appendChild(overlay);
      }
      overlay.innerHTML = `
        <span class="ms" style="font-size:48px;color:#fbbf24">build</span>
        <h2 style="color:#f0f0f0;font-size:1.2rem;font-weight:700;margin:0">Under Maintenance</h2>
        <p style="color:#888;font-size:.88rem;max-width:340px;text-align:center;line-height:1.55;margin:0">${this._he(m.message)}</p>`;
      overlay.style.display = 'flex';
    } else if (overlay) {
      overlay.style.display = 'none';
    }
  },

  /* ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     MODULE: QUICK LINKS — وحدة الروابط السريعة
     ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  _renderQuickLinks() {
    const inner = document.getElementById('ua-mod-quicklinks-inner');
    if (!inner) return;
    const links = this.data.quickLinks;

    inner.innerHTML = `
      <div class="ua-mod-header">
        <span class="ms" style="color:var(--ua-acc)">link</span>
        Quick Links
        <div class="ua-mod-badge">${links.length} link${links.length!==1?'s':''}</div>
      </div>

      <div class="ua-info-box">
        Manage a list of links rendered on your page. Add
        <code>data-ap="quicklinks"</code> to any container element.
      </div>

      <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:4px;margin-bottom:10px">
        ${links.length === 0
          ? `<div style="text-align:center;padding:22px;color:var(--ua-t3);font-size:.8rem;background:var(--ua-bg3);border-radius:8px;border:1px dashed var(--ua-brd1)">
              <span class="ms" style="display:block;font-size:24px;opacity:.4;margin-bottom:6px">link</span>
              No links yet.
             </div>`
          : links.map((lnk, i) => `
            <div style="display:flex;gap:6px;align-items:center;padding:8px 10px;background:var(--ua-bg3);border:1px solid var(--ua-brd1);border-radius:7px">
              <span class="ms" style="color:var(--ua-acc-l);font-size:16px">link</span>
              <input value="${this._esc(lnk.label)}" placeholder="Label"
                class="ua-input" style="flex:1;font-size:.8rem"
                oninput="AdminPanel.data.quickLinks[${i}].label=this.value;AdminPanel._applyQuickLinks()">
              <input value="${this._esc(lnk.url)}" placeholder="https://..."
                class="ua-input" style="flex:2;font-size:.8rem;font-family:monospace"
                oninput="AdminPanel.data.quickLinks[${i}].url=this.value;AdminPanel._applyQuickLinks()">
              <button onclick="AdminPanel.removeLink(${i})"
                style="background:none;border:none;cursor:pointer;color:var(--ua-t3);display:flex;align-items:center"
                onmouseenter="this.style.color='var(--ua-err)'" onmouseleave="this.style.color='var(--ua-t3)'">
                <span class="ms" style="font-size:16px">delete</span>
              </button>
            </div>`).join('')
        }
      </div>

      <button onclick="AdminPanel.addLink()" class="ua-btn ua-btn-ghost" style="width:100%;justify-content:center">
        <span class="ms" style="font-size:16px">add_link</span> Add Link
      </button>`;
  },

  addLink() {
    this.data.quickLinks.push({ label: 'New Link', url: 'https://' });
    this._renderQuickLinks();
  },
  removeLink(i) {
    this.data.quickLinks.splice(i, 1);
    this._renderQuickLinks();
    this._applyQuickLinks();
  },
  _applyQuickLinks() {
    document.querySelectorAll('[data-ap="quicklinks"]').forEach(el => {
      el.innerHTML = this.data.quickLinks.map(lnk =>
        `<a href="${this._he(lnk.url)}" target="_blank" style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:4px;font-size:12px;color:var(--acc2);text-decoration:none;padding:4px 8px;background:var(--acc3);border-radius:5px;margin:2px">
          <span class="ms" style="font-size:13px">open_in_new</span>${this._he(lnk.label)}
        </a>`).join('');
    });
  },

  /* ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

        Saved automatically when you click "Save to Gist"
      </span>`;
  },

  /* ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     ICON PICKER — منتقي الأيقونات
     ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  openIconModal(blockId, field) {
    this._iconTarget = { blockId, field };
    const modal = document.getElementById('ua-icon-modal');
    if (!modal) return;
    document.getElementById('ua-icon-search').value = '';
    this._renderIconGrid(UA_ALL_ICONS);
    modal.style.display = 'flex';
    setTimeout(() => document.getElementById('ua-icon-search').focus(), 80);
  },

  closeIconModal() {
    const modal = document.getElementById('ua-icon-modal');
    if (modal) modal.style.display = 'none';
    this._iconTarget = null;
  },

  filterIcons(q) {
    const filtered = q
      ? UA_ALL_ICONS.filter(i => i.includes(q.toLowerCase().replace(/ /g, '_')))
      : UA_ALL_ICONS;
    this._renderIconGrid(filtered);
  },

  _renderIconGrid(icons) {
    const grid = document.getElementById('ua-icon-grid');
    if (!grid) return;
    grid.innerHTML = icons.map(ico => `
      <div onclick="AdminPanel._selectIcon('${ico}')"
        style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;gap:2px;padding:5px 3px;border-radius:5px;cursor:pointer;border:1px solid transparent;transition:all .1s"
        onmouseenter="this.style.background='var(--bg4)';this.style.borderColor='var(--acc2)'"
        onmouseleave="this.style.background='transparent';this.style.borderColor='transparent'"
        title="${ico}">
        <span class="ms" style="font-size:19px;color:var(--acc2)">${ico}</span>
        <span style="font-size:7px;color:var(--txt3);text-align:center;line-height:1.2;word-break:break-all;max-width:42px">${ico}</span>
      </div>`).join('');
  },

  _selectIcon(ico) {
    if (!this._iconTarget) return;
    const { blockId, field } = this._iconTarget;
    this.updateBlock(blockId, field, ico);
    const inp  = document.getElementById(`ua-iinp-${blockId}`);
    if (inp)  inp.value = ico;
    const prev = document.getElementById(`ua-iprev-${blockId}`);
    if (prev) prev.querySelector('.ms').textContent = ico;
    this.closeIconModal();
    this._renderBlocks();
  },

  /* ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     HELPERS — المساعدات
     ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  _uid() { return Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 9); },

  async _sha256(msg) {
    const buf = await crypto.subtle.digest('SHA-256', new TextEncoder().encode(msg));
    return Array.from(new Uint8Array(buf)).map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0')).join('');
  },

  // escaping للمحرر (attributes) — for editor HTML attributes
  _esc(s) {
    return String(s || '').replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;');
  },

  // escaping للخرج النهائي — for final Gist output
  _he(s) {
    return String(s || '').replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;');
  },

  _toast(msg) {
    const t = document.getElementById('ua-toast');
    if (!t) return;
    t.textContent = msg;
    t.classList.add('show');
    clearTimeout(this._toastTimer);
    this._toastTimer = setTimeout(() => t.classList.remove('show'), 2800);
  }
};

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// خلف التوافق — Backward compatibility alias (keeps old code working)
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
const UpdatesAdmin = AdminPanel;

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// تهيئة — Initialize after DOM is ready
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => AdminPanel.init());

</script>


</body>
</html>
